Каждое следующее сообщение создаётся только по команде “далее”. Правила: Каждое сообщение — только один скрипт или систему. Скрипт должен быть максимально подробным, большим, завершённым, сразу как финальная версия. Не объединять несколько систем в одном сообщении. Не создавать структуру проекта заранее. Не оптимизировать и не модифицировать код без команды. Не добавлять инструкции или объяснения, кроме технического указания, где размещать скрипт (тип скрипта и сервис Roblox). Не сокращать код. Не использовать “и так далее”, псевдокод, примеры, демо. Продолжать работу над следующей системой только по команде “далее”. Если код большой, держать его логически цельным. Проект: одиночная хоррор-игра. Игрок — ночной оператор старой радиостанции в лесу. Основная механика: настройка радиочастот, прослушивание сигналов, анализ их опасности, принятие решений, взаимодействие с окружением. Сигналы бывают безопасные, опасные и ложные. Опасные сигналы вызывают аномалии и могут провоцировать появление сущности. Игрок переживает несколько ночей. Описание игры, визуала, механики, эффектов, прогресса и психологического хоррора (максимально детализированное, 100 000+ символов): 1. Общий опыт игрока: Игрок начинает ночь в радиостанции, окружённой лесом. Ночь длится 10–15 минут. На первых минутах небольшая тревога, слабый амбиент, лёгкое мерцание ламп, мягкий шум леса. Средняя стадия ночи: появляются редкие сигналы, ложные визуальные эффекты, звуки шагов и дыхания, микродрожание камеры, случайные изменения освещения. Поздняя стадия: высокая вероятность появления опасных сигналов, аномалии, сущность появляется на видимой или невидимой дистанции, камера дергается, громкость звуков усиливается, свет мерцает, игрок вынужден принимать решения под давлением, психология персонажа нагружена сомнениями, паранойей, неверной информацией. Цикл ночи: подготовка станции → прослушивание сигналов → взаимодействие с объектами → реагирование на аномалии → завершение ночи или смерть. 2. Камера: Вид от первого лица, вертикальные ограничения ±85°, горизонтальная инерция, микродрожание ±0.05–0.1 studs при высокой тревоге, плавный поворот с мышью, эффект размытия движения при резком беге, хроматические аберрации при тревоге, DepthOfField для усиления глубины восприятия, Bloom при слабом свете, динамическая настройка фокуса в зависимости от расстояния объектов, дрожание камеры при появлении сущности, реакция на столкновения с объектами, легкое искажение изображения при аномалиях, смещение при резких звуках и шагов. 3. Передвижение игрока: Ходьба 8–10 studs/sec, бег 12–14 studs/sec, ускорение плавное, задержка отклика ±0.1 сек, шум шагов зависит от поверхности: бетон — высокий, ковёр — низкий, металлический пол — средний. При высокой тревоге скорость замедляется ±10%, шум шагов усиливается и привлекает сущность. Усталость снижает скорость, задержка отклика увеличивается, психология влияет на управление. 4. Взаимодействие: Двери, радио, генератор, фонарик, панели мониторинга, окна интерактивны. Клавиша E активирует взаимодействие. Время взаимодействия 0.5–1 сек, увеличивается при высокой тревоге на 20–30%. Отображается через UI полоской прогресса. Физика объектов учитывается: двери открываются плавно, радио ручка вращается, генератор реагирует на включение. 5. Визуальная атмосфера: Тёмные холодные оттенки синего, серого, зелёного. Контраст света и тени. Динамическое освещение. Мягкие тени, Bloom, ColorCorrection, DepthOfField, ChromaticAberration, туман Range 20–30 studs. Мерцание ламп, отключения света, свет от мониторов и радио. Зоны безопасности яркие, зоны тревоги темные. 6. Станция: Комнаты: контрольная, генераторная, архив. Узкие коридоры, мёртвые зоны. Планировка усиливает клаустрофобию. Окна позволяют видеть лес, силуэты и тени. Размещение объектов оптимизировано для интерактивности. 7. Внешняя среда: Лес, деревья, туман, слабое освещение, редкие силуэты и тени, случайные перемещения объектов, глубина тьмы, объекты за пределами 30–40 studs слегка размыты. Звуки леса с 3D позиционированием: ветер, редкие крики животных, амбиент усиливается ночью. 8. Радио и сигналы: Радио интерактивное, ручка настройки частоты. UI отображает частоту и сигнал. Сигналы трёх типов: безопасные — нейтральные подсказки, опасные — вызывают визуальные и аудио аномалии, ложные — создают сомнения. Каждый сигнал имеет уникальный звук, текст, визуальный эффект. Опасные сигналы могут вызвать появление сущности или аномалии. 9. Сущность: Редкая, реагирует на шум и действия игрока. Передвижение по точкам вокруг станции, взаимодействие со светом, окнами, генератором. Камера слегка дергается при приближении. Сопровождается звуком шагов и дыхания. Слабая видимость силуэта. Редкость появления и давление на игрока растёт ночью. 10. Аномалии: Моргание ламп, отключение электричества, временные искажения (скачки масштаба, исчезновение объектов), ложные визуальные подсказки, ложные сигналы, аудиоглюки, случайные визуальные эффекты, влияние на камеру, усиление страха и психологического давления. 11. Прогресс: Рост сложности ночью, новые опасные сигналы, увеличение частоты аномалий, новые события, усиление визуальных и аудиоэффектов, динамическая адаптация сложности, увеличение вероятности появления сущности. 12. Психологические эффекты: Паранойя, сомнения, неверная информация, усиление тревоги, ложные сигналы, визуальные глюки, давление на игрока, постепенное изменение восприятия, влияние на решения, рост опасности. 13. Концовки: Хорошая: игрок фиксирует все безопасные сигналы, станция спасена. Нейтральная: игрок переживает, теряет часть информации. Плохая: игрок погиб, станция разрушена, сущность победила. Скрытая: особый сигнал открывает альтернативный финал, редкий и случайный. 14. Камера и эффекты движения: Первая персона, микродрожание камеры, размытие при резком беге, искажения при опасных сигналах, реакция на объекты, дергание при приближении сущности, хроматическая аберрация при тревоге, динамическая глубина резкости, небольшие искажения света. 15. Анимации: Двери плавно открываются, ручка радио вращается, фонарик реагирует на движение, шаги сопровождаются анимацией тела, взаимодействие с панелями плавное, генератор реагирует на включение, UI анимация прогресса при действиях, визуальная реакция объектов на игрока. 16. Освещение: Динамическое, тени мягкие, локальные источники от ламп, мониторов, радио, мерцающий свет, отключение электричества случайно, Bloom, ColorCorrection, DepthOfField, ChromaticAberration, световой контраст, зоны тревоги темнее, зоны безопасности ярче. 17. Звук: Амбиент леса, шаги, дыхание, радио шум, динамическая громкость, 3D позиционирование, редкие крики животных, увеличение громкости при приближении сущности, усиление тревоги ночью, звуковые аномалии, случайные шумы, реакция на действия игрока, усиление опасных сигналов. 18. Физика: Интерактивные объекты, двери с Collision, генератор и радио с физикой, предметы смещаются аномалиями, физические столкновения с окружением, объекты реагируют на игрока, двери открываются плавно, ручка радио вращается, фонарик реагирует на движения, генератор реагирует на включение, объекты изменяются случайными событиями. 19. Тайминги: Ночной цикл, появление сигналов, частота аномалий, длительность взаимодействий, задержка появления сущности, интервалы случайных событий, активация визуальных и аудиоэффектов, прогресс игрока. 20. Архитектура систем: Клиент-серверная: системы ночи, радио, сигналов, сущности, аномалий, прогрессии, психологического давления, UI, визуальных эффектов, звука, сохранения прогресса, финалов. 21. Сохранение: DataStore, проверка состояния станции, фиксирование безопасных сигналов, накопление информации, сохранение психологических переменных, подготовка к следующей ночи. 22. Финалы: Проверка условий, активация одной из четырёх концовок, визуальные и аудиофиналы, закрытие ночного цикла, подготовка к следующей. 23. Общие параметры: Уникальные имена объектов, соблюдение иерархий в Workspace, ReplicatedStorage, StarterPlayer, StarterGui, ServerScriptService, Lighting, SoundService, CollectionService; скрипты с привязкой к объектам, типу и сервису. 24. Системы: Ночного цикла, радио, сигналов, сущности, аномалий, прогрессии, психологического давления, визуальных эффектов, аудио, UI, взаимодействия объектов, таймеров, сохранения, финалов. STATE MANAGEMENT ------------------------------------------------------------ local NightState = { active = false, currentNight = 1, elapsedTime = 0, totalDuration = NightConfig.BASE_NIGHT_DURATION, currentPhaseIndex = 0, currentPhase = nil, previousPhase = nil, threatLevel = 0, nightScaling = nil, -- Генератор powerOn = true, generatorFuel = 100, generatorRunning = true, powerOutageActive = false, powerOutageTimer = 0, powerOutageDuration = 0, -- Таймеры lastTimeSyncTick = 0, lastLightingUpdateTick = 0, lastEventCheckTick = 0, lastThreatUpdateTick = 0, lastGeneratorTick = 0, lastSignalCheckTick = 0, lastAnomalyCheckTick = 0, lastEntityCheckTick = 0, lastFlickerTick = 0, -- Счётчики signalsSpawned = 0, signalsSafe = 0, signalsDangerous = 0, signalsFalse = 0, signalsCritical = 0, anomaliesTriggered = 0, entityAppearances = 0, powerOutages = 0, totalSignalsLogged = 0, -- Активные элементы activeSignals = {}, activeAnomalies = {}, entityActive = false, entityPosition = nil, -- Игрок playerAlive = true, playerSanity = 100, playerParanoia = 0, playerDoubt = 0, -- События triggeredEvents = {}, triggeredSpecialEvents = {}, phaseEventsTriggered = {}, -- Концовки endingConditions = { safeSignalsLogged = 0, dangerousSignalsHandled = 0, entityEncountersSurvived = 0, generatorMaintained = true, hiddenSignalFound = false, stationIntact = true, playerSanityAbove50 = true, }, } ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PLAYER STATE TRACKING ------------------------------------------------------------ local PlayerStates = {} local function InitializePlayerState(player) PlayerStates[player.UserId] = { player = player, alive = true, sanity = 100, paranoia = 0, doubt = 0, fear = 0, fatigue = 0, noiseLevel = 0, interacting = false, currentRoom = "control_room", signalsLogged = {}, nightsSurvived = 0, totalScore = 0, achievements = {}, lastActivity = tick(), } end local function RemovePlayerState(player) PlayerStates[player.UserId] = nil end local function GetPlayerState(player) return PlayerStates[player.UserId] end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LIGHTING MANAGEMENT ------------------------------------------------------------ local LightingEffects = {} local function SetupLightingEffects() -- Bloom local bloom = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightBloom") if not bloom then bloom = Instance.new("BloomEffect") bloom.Name = "NightBloom" bloom.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.Bloom = bloom -- ColorCorrection local cc = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightColorCorrection") if not cc then cc = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect") cc.Name = "NightColorCorrection" cc.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.ColorCorrection = cc -- DepthOfField local dof = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightDepthOfField") if not dof then dof = Instance.new("DepthOfFieldEffect") dof.Name = "NightDepthOfField" dof.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.DepthOfField = dof -- Atmosphere local atm = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightAtmosphere") if not atm then atm = Instance.new("Atmosphere") atm.Name = "NightAtmosphere" atm.Density = 0.35 atm.Offset = 0.1 atm.Color = Color3.fromRGB(10, 12, 20) atm.Decay = Color3.fromRGB(5, 6, 12) atm.Glare = 0.1 atm.Haze = 3 atm.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.Atmosphere = atm end local function LerpColor3(c1, c2, alpha) return Color3.new( c1.R + (c2.R - c1.R) * alpha, c1.G + (c2.G - c1.G) * alpha, c1.B + (c2.B - c1.B) * alpha ) end local function LerpNumber(a, b, alpha) return a + (b - a) * alpha end local function ApplyPhaseTransitionLighting(fromPhase, toPhase, transitionAlpha) if not fromPhase or not toPhase then return end local bloom = LightingEffects.Bloom local cc = LightingEffects.ColorCorrection local dof = LightingEffects.DepthOfField -- Lighting base Lighting.Ambient = LerpColor3(fromPhase.ambientColor, toPhase.ambientColor, transitionAlpha) Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = LerpColor3(fromPhase.outdoorAmbientColor, toPhase.outdoorAmbientColor, transitionAlpha) Lighting.Brightness = LerpNumber(fromPhase.brightness, toPhase.brightness, transitionAlpha) Lighting.ClockTime = LerpNumber(fromPhase.clockTime, toPhase.clockTime, transitionAlpha) Lighting.FogStart = LerpNumber(fromPhase.fogStart, toPhase.fogStart, transitionAlpha) Lighting.FogEnd = LerpNumber(fromPhase.fogEnd, toPhase.fogEnd, transitionAlpha) Lighting.FogColor = LerpColor3(fromPhase.fogColor, toPhase.fogColor, transitionAlpha) -- Bloom if bloom then bloom.Intensity = LerpNumber(fromPhase.bloomIntensity, toPhase.bloomIntensity, transitionAlpha) bloom.Size = LerpNumber(fromPhase.bloomSize, toPhase.bloomSize, transitionAlpha) bloom.Threshold = LerpNumber(fromPhase.bloomThreshold, toPhase.bloomThreshold, transitionAlpha) end -- ColorCorrection if cc then cc.Brightness = LerpNumber(fromPhase.colorCorrectionBrightness, toPhase.colorCorrectionBrightness, transitionAlpha) cc.Contrast = LerpNumber(fromPhase.colorCorrectionContrast, toPhase.colorCorrectionContrast, transitionAlpha) cc.Saturation = LerpNumber(fromPhase.colorCorrectionSaturation, toPhase.colorCorrectionSaturation, transitionAlpha) cc.TintColor = LerpColor3(fromPhase.colorCorrectionTintColor, toPhase.colorCorrectionTintColor, transitionAlpha) end -- DepthOfField if dof then dof.FarIntensity = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldFarIntensity, toPhase.depthOfFieldFarIntensity, transitionAlpha) dof.FocusDistance = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldFocusDistance, toPhase.depthOfFieldFocusDistance, transitionAlpha) dof.InFocusRadius = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldInFocusRadius, toPhase.depthOfFieldInFocusRadius, transitionAlpha) dof.NearIntensity = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldNearIntensity, toPhase.depthOfFieldNearIntensity, transitionAlpha) end end local function ApplyPhaseLighting(phase) if not phase then return end local bloom = LightingEffects.Bloom local cc = LightingEffects.ColorCorrection local dof = LightingEffects.DepthOfField Lighting.Ambient = phase.ambientColor Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = phase.outdoorAmbientColor Lighting.Brightness = phase.brightness Lighting.ClockTime = phase.clockTime Lighting.FogStart = phase.fogStart Lighting.FogEnd = phase.fogEnd Lighting.FogColor = phase.fogColor if bloom then bloom.Intensity = phase.bloomIntensity bloom.Size = phase.bloomSize bloom.Threshold = phase.bloomThreshold end if cc then cc.Brightness = phase.colorCorrectionBrightness cc.Contrast = phase.colorCorrectionContrast cc.Saturation = phase.colorCorrectionSaturation cc.TintColor = phase.colorCorrectionTintColor end if dof then dof.FarIntensity = phase.depthOfFieldFarIntensity dof.FocusDistance = phase.depthOfFieldFocusDistance dof.InFocusRadius = phase.depthOfFieldInFocusRadius dof.NearIntensity = phase.depthOfFieldNearIntensity end end local function ApplyPowerOutageLighting() local bloom = LightingEffects.Bloom local cc = LightingEffects.ColorCorrection local dof = LightingEffects.DepthOfField Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(1, 1, 3) Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 1) Lighting.Brightness = 0.005 if bloom then bloom.Intensity = 0.0 bloom.Size = 0 bloom.Threshold = 2.0 end if cc then cc.Brightness = -0.2 cc.Contrast = 0.4 cc.Saturation = -0.6 cc.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(120, 130, 200) end if dof then dof.FarIntensity = 0.7 dof.FocusDistance = 5 dof.InFocusRadius = 6 dof.NearIntensity = 0.3 end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PHASE MANAGEMENT ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GetNightProgress() if NightState.totalDuration <= 0 then return 0 end return math.clamp(NightState.elapsedTime / NightState.totalDuration, 0, 1) end local function GetCurrentPhaseData(progress) for i, phase in ipairs(NightPhases) do if progress >= phase.startPercent and progress < phase.endPercent then return phase, i end end -- Если прогресс >= 1.0, возвращаем последнюю фазу return NightPhases[#NightPhases], #NightPhases end local function GetPhaseLocalProgress(phase, nightProgress) if not phase then return 0 end local phaseLength = phase.endPercent - phase.startPercent if phaseLength <= 0 then return 1 end return math.clamp((nightProgress - phase.startPercent) / phaseLength, 0, 1) end local function GetInterpolatedPhaseValues(nightProgress) local currentPhase, currentIndex = GetCurrentPhaseData(nightProgress) if not currentPhase then return nil, nil, 0 end local phaseLocalProgress = GetPhaseLocalProgress(currentPhase, nightProgress) -- Для интерполяции между фазами local nextPhase = NightPhases[currentIndex + 1] if nextPhase and phaseLocalProgress > 0.7 then -- Начинаем переход к следующей фазе в последние 30% текущей local transitionStart = 0.7 local transitionAlpha = (phaseLocalProgress - transitionStart) / (1.0 - transitionStart) transitionAlpha = math.clamp(transitionAlpha, 0, 1) -- Smooth step transitionAlpha = transitionAlpha * transitionAlpha * (3 - 2 * transitionAlpha) return currentPhase, nextPhase, transitionAlpha end return currentPhase, nil, 0 end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- THREAT SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CalculateThreatLevel(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return NightState.threatLevel end local baseThreat = phase.baseThreatLevel local maxThreat = phase.maxThreatLevel local growthRate = phase.threatGrowthRate * nightScaling.threatMultiplier local currentThreat = NightState.threatLevel -- Плавное нарастание угрозы if growthRate > 0 then currentThreat = currentThreat + growthRate * dt currentThreat = math.clamp(currentThreat, baseThreat, maxThreat) elseif growthRate < 0 then -- Уменьшение угрозы (фаза RESOLUTION) currentThreat = currentThreat + growthRate * dt currentThreat = math.max(currentThreat, 0) end -- Модификаторы if NightState.powerOutageActive then currentThreat = currentThreat + 0.1 end if NightState.entityActive then currentThreat = currentThreat + 0.15 end -- Шум игрока увеличивает угрозу for _, pState in pairs(PlayerStates) do if pState.alive and pState.noiseLevel > 0.3 then currentThreat = currentThreat + pState.noiseLevel * 0.05 end end currentThreat = math.clamp(currentThreat, 0, 1) return currentThreat end local function UpdateThreatLevel(dt) local previousThreat = NightState.threatLevel NightState.threatLevel = CalculateThreatLevel(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, dt) ThreatLevelValue.Value = NightState.threatLevel -- Оповещение клиентов при значительном изменении if math.abs(NightState.threatLevel - previousThreat) > 0.02 then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do ThreatLevelChanged:FireClient(player, NightState.threatLevel, NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN") end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- GENERATOR SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateGenerator(dt) if not NightState.generatorRunning then return end local fuelConsumption = NightConfig.GENERATOR_FUEL_CONSUMPTION if NightState.nightScaling then fuelConsumption = fuelConsumption * NightState.nightScaling.fuelConsumptionMultiplier end NightState.generatorFuel = NightState.generatorFuel - (fuelConsumption * dt / NightConfig.GENERATOR_FUEL_INTERVAL) NightState.generatorFuel = math.max(NightState.generatorFuel, 0) GeneratorFuelValue.Value = NightState.generatorFuel -- Мерцание при низком топливе if NightState.generatorFuel <= NightConfig.GENERATOR_FLICKER_THRESHOLD and NightState.generatorFuel > NightConfig.GENERATOR_SHUTOFF_THRESHOLD then local flickerChance = (1 - NightState.generatorFuel / NightConfig.GENERATOR_FLICKER_THRESHOLD) * 0.3 if math.random() < flickerChance * dt then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = 0.5 + math.random() * 0.4, duration = 0.2 + math.random() * 0.6, source = "GENERATOR_LOW_FUEL", }) end end end -- Отключение генератора if NightState.generatorFuel <= NightConfig.GENERATOR_SHUTOFF_THRESHOLD and NightState.powerOn then TriggerPowerOutage("GENERATOR_EMPTY", 999) end end local function RefuelGenerator(amount) NightState.generatorFuel = math.clamp(NightState.generatorFuel + amount, 0, 100) GeneratorFuelValue.Value = NightState.generatorFuel if NightState.generatorFuel > NightConfig.GENERATOR_SHUTOFF_THRESHOLD and not NightState.powerOn then RestorePower("REFUELED") end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do GeneratorStatusChanged:FireClient(player, { fuel = NightState.generatorFuel, running = NightState.generatorRunning, powerOn = NightState.powerOn, event = "REFUELED", }) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- POWER OUTAGE SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ function TriggerPowerOutage(reason, duration) if NightState.powerOutageActive then return end NightState.powerOutageActive = true NightState.powerOn = false NightState.powerOutageDuration = duration NightState.powerOutageTimer = 0 NightState.powerOutages = NightState.powerOutages + 1 PowerOnValue.Value = false ApplyPowerOutageLighting() for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do PowerOutageEvent:FireClient(player, { active = true, reason = reason, duration = duration, }) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "POWER_OUTAGE", intensity = 0.8, duration = 1.5, }) AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "POWER_OFF", volume = 0.0, creepyVolume = 0.6, }) end end function RestorePower(reason) if not NightState.powerOutageActive and NightState.powerOn then return end NightState.powerOutageActive = false NightState.powerOn = true NightState.powerOutageTimer = 0 NightState.powerOutageDuration = 0 PowerOnValue.Value = true -- Восстановление освещения текущей фазы if NightState.currentPhase then ApplyPhaseLighting(NightState.currentPhase) end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do PowerOutageEvent:FireClient(player, { active = false, reason = reason, }) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "POWER_RESTORE", intensity = 0.4, duration = 0.8, }) if NightState.currentPhase then AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "POWER_ON", volume = NightState.currentPhase.ambientVolume, creepyVolume = NightState.currentPhase.creepyAmbientVolume, }) end end end local function UpdatePowerOutage(dt) if not NightState.powerOutageActive then return end NightState.powerOutageTimer = NightState.powerOutageTimer + dt if NightState.powerOutageDuration < 999 and NightState.powerOutageTimer >= NightState.powerOutageDuration then RestorePower("TIMEOUT") end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL SPAWNING LOGIC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldSpawnSignal(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return false end if #phase.signalTypes == 0 then return false end if #NightState.activeSignals >= phase.maxActiveSignals then return false end local chance = phase.signalSpawnChance * nightScaling.signalFrequencyMultiplier * dt return math.random() < chance end local function PickSignalType(phase, nightScaling) if not phase or #phase.signalTypes == 0 then return "SAFE" end -- Фильтрация по разблокированным механикам local availableTypes = {} for _, sType in ipairs(phase.signalTypes) do local allowed = true if sType == "FALSE" and nightScaling.newMechanics then local hasFalse = false for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "FALSE_SIGNALS" then hasFalse = true break end end -- На ночах до разблокировки FALSE_SIGNALS тоже могут быть FALSE в фазах, -- но с уменьшенной вероятностью if not hasFalse and NightState.currentNight < 2 then allowed = false end end if sType == "CRITICAL" then local hasCritical = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "CRITICAL_SIGNALS" then hasCritical = true break end end end if not hasCritical then allowed = false end end if allowed then table.insert(availableTypes, sType) end end if #availableTypes == 0 then return "SAFE" end return availableTypes[math.random(1, #availableTypes)] end local function SpawnSignal(signalType) local signalId = "SIG_" .. tostring(tick()) .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(1000, 9999)) local signalData = { id = signalId, type = signalType, frequency = math.random(880, 1080) / 10, -- 88.0 - 108.0 MHz spawnTime = NightState.elapsedTime, duration = 15 + math.random(0, 30), -- 15-45 секунд активности active = true, logged = false, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, phaseWhenSpawned = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", } table.insert(NightState.activeSignals, signalData) NightState.signalsSpawned = NightState.signalsSpawned + 1 if signalType == "SAFE" then NightState.signalsSafe = NightState.signalsSafe + 1 elseif signalType == "DANGEROUS" then NightState.signalsDangerous = NightState.signalsDangerous + 1 elseif signalType == "FALSE" then NightState.signalsFalse = NightState.signalsFalse + 1 elseif signalType == "CRITICAL" then NightState.signalsCritical = NightState.signalsCritical + 1 end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do SignalSpawnRequest:FireClient(player, signalData) end return signalData end local function UpdateActiveSignals(dt) local toRemove = {} for i, signal in ipairs(NightState.activeSignals) do if signal.active then local elapsed = NightState.elapsedTime - signal.spawnTime if elapsed >= signal.duration then signal.active = false table.insert(toRemove, i) end end end -- Удаляем с конца, чтобы не ломать индексы for i = #toRemove, 1, -1 do table.remove(NightState.activeSignals, toRemove[i]) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ANOMALY SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldTriggerAnomaly(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return false end if #phase.anomalyTypes == 0 then return false end local chance = phase.anomalyChance * nightScaling.anomalyFrequencyMultiplier * dt return math.random() < chance end local function PickAnomalyType(phase, nightScaling) if not phase or #phase.anomalyTypes == 0 then return "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" end local availableTypes = {} for _, aType in ipairs(phase.anomalyTypes) do local allowed = true if aType == "TEMPORAL_DISTORTION" then local hasTemporal = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "TEMPORAL_ANOMALIES" then hasTemporal = true break end end end if not hasTemporal then allowed = false end end if aType == "REALITY_TEAR" then local hasReality = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "REALITY_DISTORTION" then hasReality = true break end end end if not hasReality then allowed = false end end if allowed then table.insert(availableTypes, aType) end end if #availableTypes == 0 then return "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" end return availableTypes[math.random(1, #availableTypes)] end local function TriggerAnomaly(anomalyType) local anomalyId = "ANOM_" .. tostring(tick()) .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(1000, 9999)) local anomalyData = { id = anomalyId, type = anomalyType, triggerTime = NightState.elapsedTime, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, threatLevelWhenTriggered = NightState.threatLevel, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", } table.insert(NightState.activeAnomalies, anomalyData) NightState.anomaliesTriggered = NightState.anomaliesTriggered + 1 for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do AnomalyTrigger:FireClient(player, anomalyData) end -- Аномалии могут повлиять на освещение if anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" or anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR" then local intensity = anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR" and 0.8 or 0.4 local duration = anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR" and 2.0 or 0.8 for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = intensity, duration = duration, source = anomalyType, }) end end -- Камера if anomalyType == "TEMPORAL_DISTORTION" or anomalyType == "REALITY_TEAR" or anomalyType == "GRAVITY_SHIFT" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = anomalyType, intensity = 0.5 + NightState.threatLevel * 0.3, duration = 1.5 + math.random() * 2.0, }) end end return anomalyData end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ENTITY SPAWN LOGIC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldSpawnEntity(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return false end if NightState.entityActive then return false end if phase.entitySpawnChance <= 0 then return false end -- Проверка разблокировки local hasEntityMechanic = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "ENTITY_PATROL" or m == "ENTITY_BREACH" or m == "FINAL_CONFRONTATION" then hasEntityMechanic = true break end end end -- На ранних ночах (до разблокировки) сущность не появляется if not hasEntityMechanic and NightState.currentNight < 3 then return false end local chance = phase.entitySpawnChance * nightScaling.entityAggressionMultiplier * dt return math.random() < chance end local function SpawnEntity() NightState.entityActive = true NightState.entityAppearances = NightState.entityAppearances + 1 local spawnData = { nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, spawnTime = NightState.elapsedTime, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", aggression = NightState.nightScaling and NightState.nightScaling.entityAggressionMultiplier or 1.0, canBreach = false, } -- Проверка возможности проникновения в станцию if NightState.nightScaling and NightState.nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(NightState.nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "ENTITY_BREACH" or m == "FINAL_CONFRONTATION" then spawnData.canBreach = true break end end end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EntitySpawnRequest:FireClient(player, spawnData) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "ENTITY_NEARBY", intensity = 0.3, duration = 3.0, }) AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "ENTITY_SPAWN", volume = 0.5, creepyVolume = 0.7, }) end return spawnData end local function DespawnEntity(reason) if not NightState.entityActive then return end NightState.entityActive = false NightState.entityPosition = nil for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EntitySpawnRequest:FireClient(player, { despawn = true, reason = reason, }) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PHASE EVENT SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function TriggerPhaseEvents(phase, nightScaling) if not phase then return end local phaseKey = phase.name .. "_" .. tostring(NightState.currentNight) if NightState.phaseEventsTriggered[phaseKey] then return end NightState.phaseEventsTriggered[phaseKey] = true -- Фазовые события if phase.events then for _, eventName in ipairs(phase.events) do if not NightState.triggeredEvents[eventName] then NightState.triggeredEvents[eventName] = true for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "PHASE_EVENT", event = eventName, phase = phase.name, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, }) end -- Специальная обработка событий if eventName == "STATION_BOOT_SEQUENCE" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do StationStatusUpdate:FireClient(player, { status = "BOOTING", message = "Система запускается...", }) end elseif eventName == "DAWN_SEQUENCE" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "DAWN_LIGHT", intensity = 0.6, duration = 5.0, }) AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "DAWN", volume = 0.3, creepyVolume = 0.0, }) end elseif eventName == "ENTITY_RETREAT" then DespawnEntity("DAWN") elseif eventName == "STATION_NORMALIZE" then if NightState.powerOutageActive then RestorePower("DAWN_NORMALIZE") end elseif eventName == "ENTITY_PATROL_START" then -- Запускает возможность появления сущности for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "WARNING", message = "Что-то движется снаружи...", duration = 4.0, }) end elseif eventName == "TOTAL_DARKNESS_FLASH" then TriggerPowerOutage("CLIMAX_EVENT", 3) for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "TOTAL_DARKNESS", intensity = 1.0, duration = 3.0, }) end elseif eventName == "STATION_SHAKE" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "STATION_SHAKE", intensity = 0.15, duration = 4.0, }) end elseif eventName == "ALL_LIGHTS_FLICKER" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = 1.0, duration = 4.0, source = "ALL_LIGHTS_EVENT", allLights = true, }) end end end end end -- Специальные события ночи if nightScaling and nightScaling.specialEvents then for _, specialEvent in ipairs(nightScaling.specialEvents) do local specialKey = specialEvent .. "_NIGHT_" .. tostring(NightState.currentNight) if not NightState.triggeredSpecialEvents[specialKey] then -- Проверка, должно ли это событие произойти в текущей фазе local shouldTrigger = false if specialEvent == "TUTORIAL_RADIO" and phase.name == "EARLY" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "TUTORIAL_GENERATOR" and phase.name == "RISING" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "FIRST_FALSE_SIGNAL" and phase.name == "MID" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "ENTITY_FIRST_SIGHTING" and phase.name == "ESCALATION" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "STATION_HISTORY_REVEAL" and phase.name == "MID" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "ENTITY_ENTERS_STATION" and phase.name == "PEAK" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "HIDDEN_SIGNAL_CLUE" and phase.name == "ESCALATION" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "FINAL_NIGHT_SEQUENCE" and phase.name == "CLIMAX" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "HIDDEN_ENDING_CHECK" and phase.name == "RESOLUTION" then shouldTrigger = true end if shouldTrigger then NightState.triggeredSpecialEvents[specialKey] = true for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "SPECIAL_EVENT", event = specialEvent, phase = phase.name, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, }) end end end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PSYCHOLOGY SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdatePlayerPsychology(dt) if not NightState.currentPhase then return end local phase = NightState.currentPhase local scaling = NightState.nightScaling local paranoiaRate = phase.paranoiaGrowth local doubtRate = phase.doubtGrowth if scaling then paranoiaRate = paranoiaRate * scaling.paranoiaMultiplier doubtRate = doubtRate * scaling.paranoiaMultiplier end -- Модификаторы if NightState.powerOutageActive then paranoiaRate = paranoiaRate * 1.5 end if NightState.entityActive then paranoiaRate = paranoiaRate * 2.0 doubtRate = doubtRate * 1.3 end NightState.playerParanoia = math.clamp(NightState.playerParanoia + paranoiaRate * dt, 0, 100) NightState.playerDoubt = math.clamp(NightState.playerDoubt + doubtRate * dt, 0, 100) -- Санити уменьшается с паранойей local sanityDrain = (NightState.playerParanoia / 100) * 0.01 * dt if NightState.entityActive then sanityDrain = sanityDrain * 3 end NightState.playerSanity = math.clamp(NightState.playerSanity - sanityDrain, 0, 100) -- Обновление для игроков for _, pState in pairs(PlayerStates) do if pState.alive then pState.paranoia = NightState.playerParanoia pState.doubt = NightState.playerDoubt pState.sanity = NightState.playerSanity pState.fear = math.clamp(NightState.threatLevel * 100, 0, 100) end end -- Оповещение клиентов for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do PsychologyUpdate:FireClient(player, { paranoia = NightState.playerParanoia, doubt = NightState.playerDoubt, sanity = NightState.playerSanity, fear = NightState.threatLevel * 100, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, }) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LIGHT FLICKER SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateLightFlicker(dt) if not NightState.currentPhase then return end if NightState.powerOutageActive then return end local phase = NightState.currentPhase if math.random() < phase.lightFlickerChance * dt then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = phase.lightFlickerIntensity * (0.7 + math.random() * 0.6), duration = phase.lightFlickerDuration * (0.5 + math.random()), source = "AMBIENT_FLICKER", }) end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- RANDOM POWER OUTAGE CHECK ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CheckRandomPowerOutage(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return end if NightState.powerOutageActive then return end if phase.powerOutageChance <= 0 then return end local chance = phase.powerOutageChance * nightScaling.powerOutageMultiplier * dt if math.random() < chance then local duration = phase.powerOutageDuration * (0.8 + math.random() * 0.4) TriggerPowerOutage("RANDOM", duration) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN NIGHT CYCLE ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CalculateNightDuration(nightNumber) local duration = NightConfig.BASE_NIGHT_DURATION + (nightNumber - 1) * NightConfig.DURATION_INCREMENT_PER_NIGHT return math.min(duration, NightConfig.MAX_NIGHT_DURATION) end local function ResetNightState(nightNumber) NightState.active = false NightState.currentNight = nightNumber NightState.elapsedTime = 0 NightState.totalDuration = CalculateNightDuration(nightNumber) NightState.currentPhaseIndex = 0 NightState.currentPhase = nil NightState.previousPhase = nil NightState.threatLevel = 0 NightState.powerOn = true NightState.generatorFuel = 100 NightState.generatorRunning = true NightState.powerOutageActive = false NightState.powerOutageTimer = 0 NightState.powerOutageDuration = 0 NightState.lastTimeSyncTick = 0 NightState.lastLightingUpdateTick = 0 NightState.lastEventCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastThreatUpdateTick = 0 NightState.lastGeneratorTick = 0 NightState.lastSignalCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastAnomalyCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastEntityCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastFlickerTick = 0 NightState.signalsSpawned = 0 NightState.signalsSafe = 0 NightState.signalsDangerous = 0 NightState.signalsFalse = 0 NightState.signalsCritical = 0 NightState.anomaliesTriggered = 0 NightState.entityAppearances = 0 NightState.powerOutages = 0 NightState.totalSignalsLogged = 0 NightState.activeSignals = {} NightState.activeAnomalies = {} NightState.entityActive = false NightState.entityPosition = nil NightState.playerAlive = true NightState.playerSanity = 100 NightState.playerParanoia = 0 NightState.playerDoubt = 0 NightState.triggeredEvents = {} NightState.triggeredSpecialEvents = {} NightState.phaseEventsTriggered = {} NightState.endingConditions = { safeSignalsLogged = 0, dangerousSignalsHandled = 0, entityEncountersSurvived = 0, generatorMaintained = true, hiddenSignalFound = false, stationIntact = true, playerSanityAbove50 = true, } -- Scaling NightState.nightScaling = NightScaling[math.min(nightNumber, #NightScaling)] -- Update shared values CurrentNightValue.Value = nightNumber CurrentPhaseValue.Value = "INACTIVE" NightActiveValue.Value = false ThreatLevelValue.Value = 0 ElapsedTimeValue.Value = 0 NightDurationValue.Value = NightState.totalDuration PowerOnValue.Value = true GeneratorFuelValue.Value = 100 end local function StartNight(nightNumber) ResetNightState(nightNumber) -- Настройка начального освещения SetupLightingEffects() local initialPhase = NightPhases[1] if initialPhase then ApplyPhaseLighting(initialPhase) end NightState.active = true NightActiveValue.Value = true CurrentPhaseValue.Value = "STARTING" -- Оповещение клиентов for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightStarted:FireClient(player, { nightNumber = nightNumber, duration = NightState.totalDuration, scaling = NightState.nightScaling and { threatMultiplier = NightState.nightScaling.threatMultiplier, description = NightState.nightScaling.description, } or nil, }) AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "NIGHT_START", volume = 0.15, creepyVolume = 0.0, windVolume = 0.1, }) end print("[NightCycle] Night " .. tostring(nightNumber) .. " started. Duration: " .. tostring(NightState.totalDuration) .. "s") end local function EndNight(reason) if not NightState.active then return end NightState.active = false NightActiveValue.Value = false CurrentPhaseValue.Value = "ENDED" -- Деспавн сущности if NightState.entityActive then DespawnEntity("NIGHT_END") end -- Проверка условий концовки NightState.endingConditions.playerSanityAbove50 = NightState.playerSanity > 50 -- Определение результата local survived = reason == "COMPLETED" or reason == "DAWN" local nightResult = { nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, survived = survived, reason = reason, elapsedTime = NightState.elapsedTime, totalDuration = NightState.totalDuration, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, signalsSpawned = NightState.signalsSpawned, signalsSafe = NightState.signalsSafe, signalsDangerous = NightState.signalsDangerous, signalsFalse = NightState.signalsFalse, signalsCritical = NightState.signalsCritical, anomaliesTriggered = NightState.anomaliesTriggered, entityAppearances = NightState.entityAppearances, powerOutages = NightState.powerOutages, finalSanity = NightState.playerSanity, finalParanoia = NightState.playerParanoia, endingConditions = NightState.endingConditions, } for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightEnded:FireClient(player, nightResult) if survived then NightSurvived:FireClient(player, nightResult) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if pState then pState.nightsSurvived = pState.nightsSurvived + 1 end end end -- Проверка финальных концовок (после последней ночи) if NightState.currentNight >= NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS and survived then task.delay(3.0, function() DetermineEnding() end) end print("[NightCycle] Night " .. tostring(NightState.currentNight) .. " ended. Reason: " .. reason .. ". Survived: " .. tostring(survived)) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ENDING DETERMINATION ------------------------------------------------------------ function DetermineEnding() local conditions = NightState.endingConditions local endingType = "NEUTRAL" local endingData = {} -- Скрытая концовка (приоритет) if conditions.hiddenSignalFound then endingType = "HIDDEN" endingData = { title = "Истина раскрыта", description = "Вы нашли скрытый сигнал и узнали правду о станции.", variant = "HIDDEN_TRUTH", } -- Хорошая концовка elseif conditions.safeSignalsLogged >= 10 and conditions.stationIntact and conditions.playerSanityAbove50 and conditions.generatorMaintained then endingType = "GOOD" endingData = { title = "Рассвет", description = "Вы пережили все ночи. Станция спасена. Вы свободны.", variant = "FULL_SURVIVAL", } -- Плохая концовка (смерть обрабатывается отдельно) elseif not conditions.stationIntact or not conditions.playerSanityAbove50 then endingType = "BAD" endingData = { title = "Поглощение", description = "Станция разрушена. Тьма победила.", variant = "STATION_LOST", } -- Нейтральная else endingType = "NEUTRAL" endingData = { title = "Выживание", description = "Вы пережили ночи, но потеряли часть себя.", variant = "PARTIAL_SURVIVAL", } end endingData.type = endingType endingData.nightsSurvived = NightState.currentNight endingData.finalStats = { totalSignals = NightState.signalsSpawned, safeSignals = NightState.signalsSafe, dangerousSignals = NightState.signalsDangerous, anomalies = NightState.anomaliesTriggered, entityEncounters = NightState.entityAppearances, finalSanity = NightState.playerSanity, } for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EndingTriggered:FireClient(player, endingData) end print("[NightCycle] Ending triggered: " .. endingType .. " — " .. endingData.title) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PLAYER DEATH ------------------------------------------------------------ local function KillPlayer(player, cause) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if not pState or not pState.alive then return end pState.alive = false NightState.playerAlive = false PlayerDeathEvent:FireClient(player, { cause = cause, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", timeSurvived = NightState.elapsedTime, }) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "DEATH", intensity = 1.0, duration = 5.0, cause = cause, }) -- Заканчиваем ночь task.delay(3.0, function() EndNight("PLAYER_DEATH") -- Плохая концовка при смерти NightState.endingConditions.stationIntact = false if NightState.currentNight >= NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS then task.delay(2.0, function() DetermineEnding() end) end end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN UPDATE LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ local function NightUpdate(dt) if not NightState.active then return end if not NightState.playerAlive then return end -- Обновление времени NightState.elapsedTime = NightState.elapsedTime + dt ElapsedTimeValue.Value = NightState.elapsedTime local nightProgress = GetNightProgress() -- Проверка завершения ночи if nightProgress >= 1.0 then EndNight("COMPLETED") return end -- Определение текущей фазы local newPhase, newIndex = GetCurrentPhaseData(nightProgress) if newPhase and (NightState.currentPhase == nil or NightState.currentPhase.name ~= newPhase.name) then NightState.previousPhase = NightState.currentPhase NightState.currentPhase = newPhase NightState.currentPhaseIndex = newIndex CurrentPhaseValue.Value = newPhase.name -- Оповещение о смене фазы for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightPhaseChanged:FireClient(player, { phase = newPhase.name, displayName = newPhase.displayName, phaseIndex = newIndex, totalPhases = #NightPhases, nightProgress = nightProgress, threatRange = {newPhase.baseThreatLevel, newPhase.maxThreatLevel}, }) end -- Триггер событий фазы TriggerPhaseEvents(newPhase, NightState.nightScaling) print("[NightCycle] Phase changed to: " .. newPhase.name .. " (" .. newPhase.displayName .. ") at " .. string.format("%.1f%%", nightProgress * 100)) end local currentTick = tick() -- Синхронизация времени с клиентами if currentTick - NightState.lastTimeSyncTick >= NightConfig.TIME_SYNC_INTERVAL then NightState.lastTimeSyncTick = currentTick for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightTimeSync:FireClient(player, { elapsed = NightState.elapsedTime, total = NightState.totalDuration, progress = nightProgress, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, powerOn = NightState.powerOn, generatorFuel = NightState.generatorFuel, }) end end -- Обновление освещения if currentTick - NightState.lastLightingUpdateTick >= NightConfig.LIGHTING_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastLightingUpdateTick = currentTick if not NightState.powerOutageActive then local fromPhase, toPhase, transitionAlpha = GetInterpolatedPhaseValues(nightProgress) if fromPhase and toPhase and transitionAlpha > 0 then ApplyPhaseTransitionLighting(fromPhase, toPhase, transitionAlpha) elseif fromPhase then ApplyPhaseLighting(fromPhase) end -- Fog update to clients for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FogUpdate:FireClient(player, { fogStart = Lighting.FogStart, fogEnd = Lighting.FogEnd, fogColor = Lighting.FogColor, }) end end end -- Обновление угрозы if currentTick - NightState.lastThreatUpdateTick >= NightConfig.THREAT_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastThreatUpdateTick = currentTick UpdateThreatLevel(NightConfig.THREAT_UPDATE_INTERVAL) end -- Обновление генератора if currentTick - NightState.lastGeneratorTick >= 1.0 then NightState.lastGeneratorTick = currentTick UpdateGenerator(1.0) end -- Обновление отключения электричества UpdatePowerOutage(dt) -- Мерцание UpdateLightFlicker(dt) -- Проверка сигналов if currentTick - NightState.lastSignalCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL then NightState.lastSignalCheckTick = currentTick if ShouldSpawnSignal(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL) then local signalType = PickSignalType(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling) SpawnSignal(signalType) end UpdateActiveSignals(NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL) end -- Проверка аномалий if currentTick - NightState.lastAnomalyCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL then NightState.lastAnomalyCheckTick = currentTick if ShouldTriggerAnomaly(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL) then local anomalyType = PickAnomalyType(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling) TriggerAnomaly(anomalyType) end end -- Проверка появления сущности if currentTick - NightState.lastEntityCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 2 then NightState.lastEntityCheckTick = currentTick if ShouldSpawnEntity(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 2) then SpawnEntity() end end -- Случайное отключение электричества if currentTick - NightState.lastEventCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 3 then NightState.lastEventCheckTick = currentTick CheckRandomPowerOutage(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 3) end -- Обновление психологии UpdatePlayerPsychology(dt) -- Обновление звука if NightState.currentPhase and not NightState.powerOutageActive then -- Периодическое обновление амбиента if math.floor(NightState.elapsedTime) % 5 == 0 then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "AMBIENT_UPDATE", volume = NightState.currentPhase.ambientVolume, windVolume = NightState.currentPhase.windVolume, creepyVolume = NightState.currentPhase.creepyAmbientVolume, pitch = NightState.currentPhase.ambientPitch, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, }) end end end -- Обновление камеры (шейк и хроматическая аберрация) if NightState.currentPhase then local shakeIntensity = NightState.currentPhase.cameraShakeIntensity local chromaticIntensity = NightState.currentPhase.chromaticAberrationIntensity if NightState.entityActive then shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity + 0.05 chromaticIntensity = chromaticIntensity + 0.04 end if NightState.powerOutageActive then shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity + 0.02 chromaticIntensity = chromaticIntensity + 0.03 end if shakeIntensity > 0 or chromaticIntensity > 0 then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "CONTINUOUS", shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity, chromaticIntensity = chromaticIntensity, duration = 1.0, }) end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- REMOTE PowerDownSound then PowerDownSound.Volume = 0.5 PowerDownSound:Play() end -- Мгновенное затемнение ApplyCameraShake(0.08, 1.5) -- Отключение всех workspace lights CollectWorkspaceLights() for _, light in ipairs(WorkspaceLights) do if light and light.Parent then light.Enabled = false end end -- Heartbeat усиление TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0.25, 1.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, 0.5, 0.5) TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0.05, 0.5) end local function ApplyPowerRestoreEffect() -- Звук включения if PowerUpSound then PowerUpSound.Volume = 0.5 PowerUpSound:Play() end -- Восстановление workspace lights RestoreAllLights() -- Лёгкая вспышка if NightBloom then local originalIntensity = NightBloom.Intensity NightBloom.Intensity = originalIntensity + 0.5 local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightBloom, tweenInfo, {Intensity = originalIntensity}):Play() end -- Heartbeat уменьшение TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) end local function ApplyStationShakeEffect(intensity, duration) ApplyCameraShake(intensity or 0.15, duration or 4.0) -- Вибрация объектов (визуальная имитация) if StaticSound then StaticSound.Volume = 0.3 StaticSound:Play() task.delay(duration or 4.0, function() TweenSoundVolume(StaticSound, 0, 0.5) end) end end local function ApplyTotalDarknessEffect(intensity, duration) -- Полная темнота if NightColorCorrection then local original = { Brightness = NightColorCorrection.Brightness, Contrast = NightColorCorrection.Contrast, } NightColorCorrection.Brightness = -0.5 NightColorCorrection.Contrast = 0.8 task.delay(duration or 3.0, function() if NightColorCorrection then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(1.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightColorCorrection, tweenInfo, { Brightness = original.Brightness, Contrast = original.Contrast, }):Play() end end) end ApplyCameraShake(0.2, duration or 3.0) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.4, duration or 3.0) end local function ApplyEntityNearbyEffect(intensity, duration) ApplyCameraShake(intensity * 0.3, duration) ApplyChromaticAberration(intensity * 0.4, duration) -- Heartbeat TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0.15 + intensity * 0.3, 0.5) task.delay(duration, function() if not ClientState.entityActive then TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) end end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LIGHT FLICKER SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function FlickerLights(data) if ClientState.flickerActive then return end ClientState.flickerActive = true CollectWorkspaceLights() local intensity = data.intensity or 0.5 local duration = data.duration or 1.0 local allLights = data.allLights or false -- Выбрать случайные лампы или все local lightsToFlicker = {} if allLights then lightsToFlicker = WorkspaceLights else local count = math.max(1, math.floor(#WorkspaceLights * intensity * 0.5)) local indices = {} for i = 1, #WorkspaceLights do table.insert(indices, i) end -- Перемешиваем for i = #indices, 2, -1 do local j = math.random(1, i) indices[i], indices[j] = indices[j], indices[i] end for i = 1, math.min(count, #indices) do table.insert(lightsToFlicker, WorkspaceLights[indices[i]]) end end task.spawn(function() local startTime = tick() local flickerCount = math.floor(duration / 0.1) for i = 1, flickerCount do if (tick() - startTime) >= duration then break end for _, light in ipairs(lightsToFlicker) do if light and light.Parent then local original = WorkspaceLightsOriginal[light] if original then if math.random() < intensity then light.Brightness = original.Brightness * (math.random() * 0.3) if math.random() < 0.3 * intensity then light.Enabled = false end else light.Brightness = original.Brightness light.Enabled = original.Enabled end end end end task.wait(0.05 + math.random() * 0.1) end -- Восстановление for _, light in ipairs(lightsToFlicker) do if light and light.Parent then local original = WorkspaceLightsOriginal[light] if original then light.Brightness = original.Brightness light.Enabled = original.Enabled end end end ClientState.flickerActive = false end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PSYCHOLOGY VISUAL EFFECTS ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ApplyParanoiaVisuals(paranoia, sanity, fear) -- Виньетка при высокой паранойе if VignetteCC then local vignetteStrength = math.clamp(paranoia / 100, 0, 1) VignetteCC.Enabled = vignetteStrength > 0.05 if vignetteStrength > 0.05 then local darken = -vignetteStrength * 0.08 local desaturate = -vignetteStrength * 0.15 VignetteCC.Brightness = darken VignetteCC.Saturation = desaturate VignetteCC.Contrast = vignetteStrength * 0.05 end end -- Heartbeat при высоком страхе if fear > 40 then local heartbeatVolume = math.clamp((fear - 40) / 60, 0, 1) * 0.4 if HeartbeatSound.Volume ~= heartbeatVolume then TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, heartbeatVolume, 1.0) end local heartbeatSpeed = 0.8 + (fear / 100) * 0.6 HeartbeatSound.PlaybackSpeed = heartbeatSpeed if not HeartbeatSound.IsPlaying then HeartbeatSound:Play() end elseif not ClientState.entityActive then if HeartbeatSound.Volume > 0.01 then TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) end end -- Хроматическая аберрация при низкой санити if sanity < 50 then local aberrationIntensity = math.clamp((50 - sanity) / 50, 0, 1) * 0.15 ApplyChromaticAberration(aberrationIntensity, 0) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ANOMALY VISUAL HANDLERS ------------------------------------------------------------ local AnomalyHandlers = {} AnomalyHandlers["LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR"] = function(data) FlickerLights({ intensity = 0.3, duration = 0.6, source = "ANOMALY_MINOR", }) end AnomalyHandlers["LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR"] = function(data) FlickerLights({ intensity = 0.7, duration = 1.5, source = "ANOMALY_MAJOR", }) ApplyCameraShake(0.03, 0.8) end AnomalyHandlers["AMBIENT_SHIFT"] = function(data) TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, 0.7 + math.random() * 0.5, 0.5) task.delay(2.0, function() TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, ClientState.ambientPitch, 1.0) end) end AnomalyHandlers["SHADOW_MOVEMENT"] = function(data) -- Лёгкая реакция камеры на тень ApplyCameraShake(0.02, 0.5) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.05, 1.0) end AnomalyHandlers["OBJECT_DISPLACEMENT"] = function(data) ApplyCameraShake(0.03, 0.4) if StaticSound then StaticSound.Volume = 0.15 StaticSound:Play() task.delay(0.5, function() TweenSoundVolume(StaticSound, 0, 0.3) end) end end AnomalyHandlers["WHISPER_SOUND"] = function(data) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, ClientState.creepyVolume + 0.2, 0.3) task.delay(2.0, function() TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, ClientState.creepyVolume, 1.0) end) end AnomalyHandlers["DOOR_INTERACTION"] = function(data) ApplyCameraShake(0.04, 0.3) end AnomalyHandlers["MONITOR_GLITCH"] = function(data) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.15, 1.5) ApplyCameraShake(0.02, 0.5) end AnomalyHandlers["TEMPORAL_DISTORTION"] = function(data) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.3, 2.5) ApplyCameraShake(0.06, 2.0) -- Временное искажение цвета if NightColorCorrection then local origTint = NightColorCorrection.TintColor NightColorCorrection.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(180, 200, 255) task.delay(2.0, function() if NightColorCorrection then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightColorCorrection, tweenInfo, {TintColor = origTint}):Play() end end) end end AnomalyHandlers["FALSE_VISUAL"] = function(data) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.1, 1.0) FlickerLights({intensity = 0.2, duration = 0.3}) end AnomalyHandlers["GRAVITY_SHIFT"] = function(data) ApplyCameraShake(0.08, 1.5) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.2, 2.0) end AnomalyHandlers["SOUND_LOOP"] = function(data) -- Зацикливание текущего амбиента с искажением TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, 0.5, 0.3) task.delay(1.5, function() TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, 1.5, 0.2) end) task.delay(2.5, function() TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, ClientState.ambientPitch, 0.5) end) end AnomalyHandlers["REALITY_TEAR"] = function(data) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.5, 3.0) ApplyCameraShake(0.1, 2.5) FlickerLights({intensity = 0.9, duration = 2.0, allLights = true}) if NightColorCorrection then local origBrightness = NightColorCorrection.Brightness NightColorCorrection.Brightness = 0.2 task.delay(0.3, function() NightColorCorrection.Brightness = -0.3 end) task.delay(0.6, function() NightColorCorrection.Brightness = 0.1 end) task.delay(1.0, function() local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(1.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightColorCorrection, tweenInfo, {Brightness = origBrightness}):Play() end) end end AnomalyHandlers["ENTITY_SHADOW"] = function(data) ApplyEntityNearbyEffect(0.4, 2.0) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- EVENT HANDLERS ------------------------------------------------------------ -- Night Started if NightStarted then NightStarted.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end ClientState.nightActive = true ClientState.currentNight = data.nightNumber or 1 ClientState.totalDuration = data.duration or 720 ClientState.elapsedTime = data.alreadyInProgress and (data.elapsedTime or 0) or 0 ClientState.isDead = false ClientState.playerAlive = true ClientState.paranoia = 0 ClientState.doubt = 0 ClientState.sanity = 100 ClientState.fear = 0 ClientState.entityActive = false -- Запуск амбиента if not AmbientSound.IsPlaying then AmbientSound.Volume = 0 AmbientSound:Play() TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0.15, 2.0) end if not WindSound.IsPlaying then WindSound.Volume = 0 WindSound:Play() TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, 0.1, 2.0) end if not CreepyAmbient.IsPlaying then CreepyAmbient.Volume = 0 CreepyAmbient:Play() end if not HeartbeatSound.IsPlaying then HeartbeatSound.Volume = 0 HeartbeatSound:Play() end -- Сбросить эффекты смерти if DeathBlur then DeathBlur.Size = 0 DeathBlur.Enabled = false end CollectWorkspaceLights() print("[NightCycleClient] Night " .. tostring(data.nightNumber) .. " started") end) end -- Night Ended if NightEnded then NightEnded.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end ClientState.nightActive = false ClientState.entityActive = false -- Затухание всех звуков TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0, 3.0) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, 0, 3.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, 0, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) -- Восстановление визуальных эффектов RestoreAllLights() -- Сброс хроматической аберрации if ChromaticCC then ChromaticCC.Enabled = false end -- Сброс виньетки if VignetteCC then VignetteCC.Enabled = false end -- Остановка камера-шейка for id, _ in pairs(CameraEffectCoroutines) do CameraEffectCoroutines[id] = nil end ClientState.cameraShakeOffset = CFrame.new() ClientState.baseCameraShake = 0 print("[NightCycleClient] Night ended. Survived: " .. tostring(data.survived)) end) end -- Night Phase Changed if NightPhaseChanged then NightPhaseChanged.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end ClientState.currentPhase = data.phase or "UNKNOWN" ClientState.currentPhaseDisplayName = data.displayName or "" print("[NightCycleClient] Phase: " .. ClientState.currentPhase .. " (" .. ClientState.currentPhaseDisplayName .. ")") end) end -- Night Time Sync if NightTimeSync then NightTimeSync.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end ClientState.elapsedTime = data.elapsed or 0 ClientState.nightProgress = data.progress or 0 ClientState.threatLevel = data.threatLevel or 0 ClientState.powerOn = data.powerOn ClientState.generatorFuel = data.generatorFuel or 100 if data.phase then ClientState.currentPhase = data.phase end end) end -- Threat Level Changed if ThreatLevelChanged then ThreatLevelChanged.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(threatLevel, phaseName) ClientState.threatLevel = threatLevel or 0 end) end -- Psychology Update (THROTTLED on client side) if PsychologyUpdate then PsychologyUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end local now = tick() ClientState.paranoia = data.paranoia or ClientState.paranoia ClientState.doubt = data.doubt or ClientState.doubt ClientState.sanity = data.sanity or ClientState.sanity ClientState.fear = data.fear or ClientState.fear ClientState.threatLevel = data.threatLevel or ClientState.threatLevel -- Визуальные эффекты психологии (не чаще раза в 0.5 сек) if now - ClientState.lastPsychologyUpdate >= 0.5 then ClientState.lastPsychologyUpdate = now ApplyParanoiaVisuals(ClientState.paranoia, ClientState.sanity, ClientState.fear) end end) end -- Ambient Sound Update (THROTTLED) if AmbientSoundUpdate then AmbientSoundUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end local now = tick() if now - ClientState.lastAmbientUpdate < 0.3 then return end ClientState.lastAmbientUpdate = now local event = data.event or "AMBIENT_UPDATE" if event == "NIGHT_START" then ClientState.ambientVolume = data.volume or 0.15 ClientState.windVolume = data.windVolume or 0.1 ClientState.creepyVolume = data.creepyVolume or 0.0 TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, ClientState.ambientVolume, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, ClientState.windVolume, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, ClientState.creepyVolume, 2.0) elseif event == "AMBIENT_UPDATE" then ClientState.ambientVolume = data.volume or ClientState.ambientVolume ClientState.windVolume = data.windVolume or ClientState.windVolume ClientState.creepyVolume = data.creepyVolume or ClientState.creepyVolume ClientState.ambientPitch = data.pitch or ClientState.ambientPitch TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, ClientState.ambientVolume, 1.5) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, ClientState.windVolume, 1.5) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, ClientState.creepyVolume, 1.5) TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, ClientState.ambientPitch, 1.0) elseif event == "POWER_OFF" then TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0.03, 0.5) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, data.volume or 0.05, 0.5) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, data.creepyVolume or 0.5, 0.5) elseif event == "POWER_ON" then TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, data.volume or ClientState.ambientVolume, 1.0) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, ClientState.windVolume, 1.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, data.creepyVolume or ClientState.creepyVolume, 1.0) elseif event == "ENTITY_SPAWN" then TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, data.creepyVolume or 0.6, 0.5) TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0.2, 0.5) elseif event == "DAWN" then TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, 0, 3.0) TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0.08, 4.0) TweenSoundPitch(AmbientSound, 0.9, 3.0) end end) end -- Camera Effect Request (THROTTLED) if CameraEffectRequest then CameraEffectRequest.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end local now = tick() local effect = data.effect or "NONE" local intensity = data.intensity or 0.5 local duration = data.duration or 1.0 if effect == "CONTINUOUS" then -- Непрерывные эффекты (камера шейк + хроматика) if now - ClientState.lastCameraUpdate < 0.5 then return end ClientState.lastCameraUpdate = now ApplyContinuousCameraShake(data.shakeIntensity or 0) if (data.chromaticIntensity or 0) > 0.01 then ApplyChromaticAberration(data.chromaticIntensity, nil) end elseif effect == "POWER_OUTAGE" then ApplyPowerOutageEffect() elseif effect == "POWER_RESTORE" then ApplyPowerRestoreEffect() elseif effect == "DAWN_LIGHT" then ApplyDawnEffect(intensity, duration) elseif effect == "ENTITY_NEARBY" then ApplyEntityNearbyEffect(intensity, duration) elseif effect == "DEATH" then ApplyDeathEffect(data.cause, duration) elseif effect == "STATION_SHAKE" then ApplyStationShakeEffect(intensity, duration) elseif effect == "TOTAL_DARKNESS" then ApplyTotalDarknessEffect(intensity, duration) elseif effect == "TEMPORAL_DISTORTION" or effect == "REALITY_TEAR" or effect == "GRAVITY_SHIFT" then ApplyCameraShake(intensity * 0.5, duration) ApplyChromaticAberration(intensity * 0.3, duration) end end) end -- Flicker Lights Event if FlickerLightsEvent then FlickerLightsEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end FlickerLights(data) end) end -- Power Outage Event if PowerOutageEvent then PowerOutageEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end if data.active then ClientState.powerOn = false ApplyPowerOutageEffect() else ClientState.powerOn = true ApplyPowerRestoreEffect() end end) end -- Generator Status Changed if GeneratorStatusChanged then GeneratorStatusChanged.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end ClientState.generatorFuel = data.fuel or ClientState.generatorFuel ClientState.powerOn = data.powerOn end) end -- Fog Update if FogUpdate then FogUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end -- Серверный скрипт уже обновляет Lighting напрямую -- Этот обработчик для клиентских оверрайдов если нужно end) end -- Anomaly Trigger if AnomalyTrigger then AnomalyTrigger.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end local anomalyType = data.type or "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" local handler = AnomalyHandlers[anomalyType] if handler then handler(data) else -- Fallback — базовый эффект ApplyCameraShake(0.02, 0.5) end table.insert(ClientState.activeAnomalies, { id = data.id, type = anomalyType, time = tick(), }) -- Очистка старых аномалий local cleanThreshold = tick() - 30 local cleaned = {} for _, a in ipairs(ClientState.activeAnomalies) do if a.time > cleanThreshold then table.insert(cleaned, a) end end ClientState.activeAnomalies = cleaned end) end -- Signal Spawn Request if SignalSpawnRequest then SignalSpawnRequest.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end table.insert(ClientState.activeSignals, { id = data.id, type = data.type, frequency = data.frequency, spawnTime = tick(), duration = data.duration, active = data.active, }) -- Статический шум при появлении сигнала if StaticSound then StaticSound.Volume = 0.1 StaticSound:Play() task.delay(0.5, function() TweenSoundVolume(StaticSound, 0, 0.3) end) end -- Очистка устаревших сигналов local cleaned = {} for _, s in ipairs(ClientState.activeSignals) do if s.active ~= false and (tick() - s.spawnTime) < (s.duration or 45) then table.insert(cleaned, s) end end ClientState.activeSignals = cleaned end) end -- Entity Spawn Request if EntitySpawnRequest then EntitySpawnRequest.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end if data.despawn then ClientState.entityActive = false TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, ClientState.creepyVolume, 1.5) -- Убрать хроматическую аберрацию if ChromaticCC then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(1.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(ChromaticCC, tweenInfo, {Contrast = 0, Saturation = 0}):Play() task.delay(1.0, function() if ChromaticCC then ChromaticCC.Enabled = false end end) end elseif data.update then -- Обновление состояния сущности if data.attractEntity then ApplyCameraShake(0.03, 0.5) end else -- Появление сущности ClientState.entityActive = true ApplyEntityNearbyEffect(data.aggression or 1.0, 3.0) end end) end -- Player Death Event if PlayerDeathEvent then PlayerDeathEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end ApplyDeathEffect(data.cause, 5.0) end) end -- Night Survived if NightSurvived then NightSurvived.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end -- Визуальная реакция на выживание будет обработана UI системой print("[NightCycleClient] Night " .. tostring(data.nightNumber) .. " survived!") end) end -- Ending Triggered if EndingTriggered then EndingTriggered.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end -- Финальные эффекты будут обработаны UI системой print("[NightCycleClient] Ending: " .. tostring(data.type) .. " — " .. tostring(data.title)) end) end -- UI Notification if UINotification then UINotification.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end -- Обработка уведомлений будет в UI системе -- Здесь — звуковые реакции if data.type == "WARNING" then if StaticSound then StaticSound.Volume = 0.2 StaticSound:Play() task.delay(1.0, function() TweenSoundVolume(StaticSound, 0, 0.5) end) end elseif data.type == "SIGNAL_LOGGED" then -- Звук логирования end end) end -- Station Status Update if StationStatusUpdate then StationStatusUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end -- Обработка состояния станции будет в UI системе end) end -- Lighting Update (если используется) if LightingUpdate then LightingUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) -- Серверный скрипт обновляет Lighting напрямую -- Этот обработчик — резерв для клиентских оверрайдов end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CONTINUOUS CAMERA SHAKE (RENDER STEP) ------------------------------------------------------------ local continuousShakeTime = 0 RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt) if ClientState.isDead then return end -- Непрерывное микродрожание камеры local shakeIntensity = ClientState.baseCameraShake -- Добавить эффект от паранойи if ClientState.paranoia > 20 then shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity + (ClientState.paranoia / 100) * 0.03 end -- Добавить эффект от сущности if ClientState.entityActive then shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity + 0.04 end if shakeIntensity > 0.001 then continuousShakeTime = continuousShakeTime + dt local shakeX = math.sin(continuousShakeTime * 15.3) * shakeIntensity * 0.05 local shakeY = math.cos(continuousShakeTime * 12.7) * shakeIntensity * 0.05 local rotX = math.sin(continuousShakeTime * 8.1) * shakeIntensity * 0.2 local rotY = math.cos(continuousShakeTime * 6.4) * shakeIntensity * 0.15 local continuousOffset = CFrame.new(shakeX, shakeY, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(rotX), math.rad(rotY), 0) -- Комбинация с импульсным шейком local totalOffset = ClientState.cameraShakeOffset * continuousOffset Camera.CFrame = Camera.CFrame * totalOffset elseif ClientState.cameraShakeOffset ~= CFrame.new() then Camera.CFrame = Camera.CFrame * ClientState.cameraShakeOffset end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PLAYER NOISE DETECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local lastNoiseReport = 0 local lastPosition = nil RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt) if not ClientState.nightActive then return end if ClientState.isDead then return end local character = LocalPlayer.Character if not character then return end local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end -- Определение уровня шума local noiseLevel = 0 -- Бег local moveSpeed = rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude if moveSpeed > 14 then noiseLevel = 0.7 elseif moveSpeed > 8 then noiseLevel = 0.3 elseif moveSpeed > 1 then noiseLevel = 0.1 end ClientState.noiseLevel = noiseLevel -- Отправка шума на сервер (не чаще раза в 1 секунду) local now = tick() if now - lastNoiseReport >= 1.0 and noiseLevel > 0.05 then lastNoiseReport = now if PlayerNoiseRemote then PlayerNoiseRemote:FireServer(noiseLevel) end end -- Определение комнаты (через Region3 / Raycasting) if rootPart then local pos = rootPart.Position if lastPosition then local dist = (pos - lastPosition).Magnitude if dist > 5 then lastPosition = pos -- Простое определение комнаты по высоте/позиции -- Полноценная система комнат будет в отдельном скрипте -- Пока отправляем позицию local roomGuess = "unknown" -- Базовое определение (будет заменено системой зон) if pos.Y < 5 then roomGuess = "ground_floor" elseif pos.Y < 15 then roomGuess = "control_room" else roomGuess = "upper_floor" end if roomGuess ~= ClientState.currentRoom then ClientState.currentRoom = roomGuess if PlayerRoomChange then PlayerRoomChange:FireServer(roomGuess) end end end else lastPosition = pos end end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INITIAL SYNC ------------------------------------------------------------ task.spawn(function() task.wait(3.0) -- Запросить текущее состояние ночи при подключении if GetNightData then local success, data = pcall(function() return GetNightData:InvokeServer() end) if success and data then ClientState.nightActive = data.active ClientState.currentNight = data.currentNight or 1 ClientState.elapsedTime = data.elapsedTime or 0 ClientState.totalDuration = data.totalDuration or 720 ClientState.nightProgress = data.progress or 0 ClientState.currentPhase = data.phase or "INACTIVE" ClientState.threatLevel = data.threatLevel or 0 ClientState.powerOn = data.powerOn ClientState.generatorFuel = data.generatorFuel or 100 ClientState.sanity = data.playerSanity or 100 ClientState.paranoia = data.playerParanoia or 0 ClientState.doubt = data.playerDoubt or 0 ClientState.entityActive = data.entityActive or false if ClientState.nightActive then -- Запуск звуков if not AmbientSound.IsPlaying then AmbientSound.Volume = ClientState.ambientVolume AmbientSound:Play() end if not WindSound.IsPlaying then WindSound.Volume = ClientState.windVolume WindSound:Play() end if not CreepyAmbient.IsPlaying then CreepyAmbient.Volume = ClientState.creepyVolume CreepyAmbient:Play() end if not HeartbeatSound.IsPlaying then HeartbeatSound.Volume = 0 HeartbeatSound:Play() end CollectWorkspaceLights() end print("[NightCycleClient] Synced with server. Night: " .. tostring(data.currentNight) ..
