------------------------------------------------------------ local LightingEffects = {} local function SetupLightingEffects() local bloom = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightBloom") if not bloom then bloom = Instance.new("BloomEffect") bloom.Name = "NightBloom" bloom.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.Bloom = bloom local cc = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightColorCorrection") if not cc then cc = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect") cc.Name = "NightColorCorrection" cc.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.ColorCorrection = cc local dof = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightDepthOfField") if not dof then dof = Instance.new("DepthOfFieldEffect") dof.Name = "NightDepthOfField" dof.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.DepthOfField = dof local atm = Lighting:FindFirstChild("NightAtmosphere") if not atm then atm = Instance.new("Atmosphere") atm.Name = "NightAtmosphere" atm.Density = 0.35 atm.Offset = 0.1 atm.Color = Color3.fromRGB(10, 12, 20) atm.Decay = Color3.fromRGB(5, 6, 12) atm.Glare = 0.1 atm.Haze = 3 atm.Parent = Lighting end LightingEffects.Atmosphere = atm end local function LerpColor3(c1, c2, alpha) return Color3.new( c1.R + (c2.R - c1.R) * alpha, c1.G + (c2.G - c1.G) * alpha, c1.B + (c2.B - c1.B) * alpha ) end local function LerpNumber(a, b, alpha) return a + (b - a) * alpha end local function ApplyPhaseTransitionLighting(fromPhase, toPhase, transitionAlpha) if not fromPhase or not toPhase then return end local bloom = LightingEffects.Bloom local cc = LightingEffects.ColorCorrection local dof = LightingEffects.DepthOfField Lighting.Ambient = LerpColor3(fromPhase.ambientColor, toPhase.ambientColor, transitionAlpha) Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = LerpColor3(fromPhase.outdoorAmbientColor, toPhase.outdoorAmbientColor, transitionAlpha) Lighting.Brightness = LerpNumber(fromPhase.brightness, toPhase.brightness, transitionAlpha) Lighting.ClockTime = LerpNumber(fromPhase.clockTime, toPhase.clockTime, transitionAlpha) Lighting.FogStart = LerpNumber(fromPhase.fogStart, toPhase.fogStart, transitionAlpha) Lighting.FogEnd = LerpNumber(fromPhase.fogEnd, toPhase.fogEnd, transitionAlpha) Lighting.FogColor = LerpColor3(fromPhase.fogColor, toPhase.fogColor, transitionAlpha) if bloom then bloom.Intensity = LerpNumber(fromPhase.bloomIntensity, toPhase.bloomIntensity, transitionAlpha) bloom.Size = LerpNumber(fromPhase.bloomSize, toPhase.bloomSize, transitionAlpha) bloom.Threshold = LerpNumber(fromPhase.bloomThreshold, toPhase.bloomThreshold, transitionAlpha) end if cc then cc.Brightness = LerpNumber(fromPhase.colorCorrectionBrightness, toPhase.colorCorrectionBrightness, transitionAlpha) cc.Contrast = LerpNumber(fromPhase.colorCorrectionContrast, toPhase.colorCorrectionContrast, transitionAlpha) cc.Saturation = LerpNumber(fromPhase.colorCorrectionSaturation, toPhase.colorCorrectionSaturation, transitionAlpha) cc.TintColor = LerpColor3(fromPhase.colorCorrectionTintColor, toPhase.colorCorrectionTintColor, transitionAlpha) end if dof then dof.FarIntensity = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldFarIntensity, toPhase.depthOfFieldFarIntensity, transitionAlpha) dof.FocusDistance = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldFocusDistance, toPhase.depthOfFieldFocusDistance, transitionAlpha) dof.InFocusRadius = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldInFocusRadius, toPhase.depthOfFieldInFocusRadius, transitionAlpha) dof.NearIntensity = LerpNumber(fromPhase.depthOfFieldNearIntensity, toPhase.depthOfFieldNearIntensity, transitionAlpha) end end local function ApplyPhaseLighting(phase) if not phase then return end local bloom = LightingEffects.Bloom local cc = LightingEffects.ColorCorrection local dof = LightingEffects.DepthOfField Lighting.Ambient = phase.ambientColor Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = phase.outdoorAmbientColor Lighting.Brightness = phase.brightness Lighting.ClockTime = phase.clockTime Lighting.FogStart = phase.fogStart Lighting.FogEnd = phase.fogEnd Lighting.FogColor = phase.fogColor if bloom then bloom.Intensity = phase.bloomIntensity bloom.Size = phase.bloomSize bloom.Threshold = phase.bloomThreshold end if cc then cc.Brightness = phase.colorCorrectionBrightness cc.Contrast = phase.colorCorrectionContrast cc.Saturation = phase.colorCorrectionSaturation cc.TintColor = phase.colorCorrectionTintColor end if dof then dof.FarIntensity = phase.depthOfFieldFarIntensity dof.FocusDistance = phase.depthOfFieldFocusDistance dof.InFocusRadius = phase.depthOfFieldInFocusRadius dof.NearIntensity = phase.depthOfFieldNearIntensity end end local function ApplyPowerOutageLighting() local bloom = LightingEffects.Bloom local cc = LightingEffects.ColorCorrection local dof = LightingEffects.DepthOfField Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(1, 1, 3) Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 1) Lighting.Brightness = 0.005 if bloom then bloom.Intensity = 0.0 bloom.Size = 0 bloom.Threshold = 2.0 end if cc then cc.Brightness = -0.2 cc.Contrast = 0.4 cc.Saturation = -0.6 cc.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(120, 130, 200) end if dof then dof.FarIntensity = 0.7 dof.FocusDistance = 5 dof.InFocusRadius = 6 dof.NearIntensity = 0.3 end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PHASE MANAGEMENT ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GetNightProgress() if NightState.totalDuration <= 0 then return 0 end return math.clamp(NightState.elapsedTime / NightState.totalDuration, 0, 1) end local function GetCurrentPhaseData(progress) for i, phase in ipairs(NightPhases) do if progress >= phase.startPercent and progress < phase.endPercent then return phase, i end end return NightPhases[#NightPhases], #NightPhases end local function GetPhaseLocalProgress(phase, nightProgress) if not phase then return 0 end local phaseLength = phase.endPercent - phase.startPercent if phaseLength <= 0 then return 1 end return math.clamp((nightProgress - phase.startPercent) / phaseLength, 0, 1) end local function GetInterpolatedPhaseValues(nightProgress) local currentPhase, currentIndex = GetCurrentPhaseData(nightProgress) if not currentPhase then return nil, nil, 0 end local phaseLocalProgress = GetPhaseLocalProgress(currentPhase, nightProgress) local nextPhase = NightPhases[currentIndex + 1] if nextPhase and phaseLocalProgress > 0.7 then local transitionStart = 0.7 local transitionAlpha = (phaseLocalProgress - transitionStart) / (1.0 - transitionStart) transitionAlpha = math.clamp(transitionAlpha, 0, 1) transitionAlpha = transitionAlpha * transitionAlpha * (3 - 2 * transitionAlpha) return currentPhase, nextPhase, transitionAlpha end return currentPhase, nil, 0 end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- THREAT SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CalculateThreatLevel(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return NightState.threatLevel end local baseThreat = phase.baseThreatLevel local maxThreat = phase.maxThreatLevel local growthRate = phase.threatGrowthRate * nightScaling.threatMultiplier local currentThreat = NightState.threatLevel if growthRate > 0 then currentThreat = currentThreat + growthRate * dt currentThreat = math.clamp(currentThreat, baseThreat, maxThreat) elseif growthRate < 0 then currentThreat = currentThreat + growthRate * dt currentThreat = math.max(currentThreat, 0) end if NightState.powerOutageActive then currentThreat = currentThreat + 0.1 end if NightState.entityActive then currentThreat = currentThreat + 0.15 end for _, pState in pairs(PlayerStates) do if pState.alive and pState.noiseLevel > 0.3 then currentThreat = currentThreat + pState.noiseLevel * 0.05 end end currentThreat = math.clamp(currentThreat, 0, 1) return currentThreat end local function UpdateThreatLevel(dt) local previousThreat = NightState.threatLevel NightState.threatLevel = CalculateThreatLevel(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, dt) ThreatLevelValue.Value = NightState.threatLevel if math.abs(NightState.threatLevel - previousThreat) > 0.03 then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do ThreatLevelChanged:FireClient(player, NightState.threatLevel, NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN") end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- GENERATOR SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateGenerator(dt) if not NightState.generatorRunning then return end local fuelConsumption = NightConfig.GENERATOR_FUEL_CONSUMPTION if NightState.nightScaling then fuelConsumption = fuelConsumption * NightState.nightScaling.fuelConsumptionMultiplier end NightState.generatorFuel = NightState.generatorFuel - (fuelConsumption * dt / NightConfig.GENERATOR_FUEL_INTERVAL) NightState.generatorFuel = math.max(NightState.generatorFuel, 0) GeneratorFuelValue.Value = NightState.generatorFuel if NightState.generatorFuel <= NightConfig.GENERATOR_FLICKER_THRESHOLD and NightState.generatorFuel > NightConfig.GENERATOR_SHUTOFF_THRESHOLD then local flickerChance = (1 - NightState.generatorFuel / NightConfig.GENERATOR_FLICKER_THRESHOLD) * 0.1 if math.random() < flickerChance then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = 0.5 + math.random() * 0.4, duration = 0.2 + math.random() * 0.6, source = "GENERATOR_LOW_FUEL", }) end end end if NightState.generatorFuel <= NightConfig.GENERATOR_SHUTOFF_THRESHOLD and NightState.powerOn then TriggerPowerOutage("GENERATOR_EMPTY", 999) end end local function RefuelGenerator(amount) NightState.generatorFuel = math.clamp(NightState.generatorFuel + amount, 0, 100) GeneratorFuelValue.Value = NightState.generatorFuel if NightState.generatorFuel > NightConfig.GENERATOR_SHUTOFF_THRESHOLD and not NightState.powerOn then RestorePower("REFUELED") end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do GeneratorStatusChanged:FireClient(player, { fuel = NightState.generatorFuel, running = NightState.generatorRunning, powerOn = NightState.powerOn, event = "REFUELED", }) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- POWER OUTAGE SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ function TriggerPowerOutage(reason, duration) if NightState.powerOutageActive then return end NightState.powerOutageActive = true NightState.powerOn = false NightState.powerOutageDuration = duration NightState.powerOutageTimer = 0 NightState.powerOutages = NightState.powerOutages + 1 PowerOnValue.Value = false ApplyPowerOutageLighting() for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do PowerOutageEvent:FireClient(player, { active = true, reason = reason, duration = duration, }) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "POWER_OUTAGE", intensity = 0.8, duration = 1.5, }) end end function RestorePower(reason) if not NightState.powerOutageActive and NightState.powerOn then return end NightState.powerOutageActive = false NightState.powerOn = true NightState.powerOutageTimer = 0 NightState.powerOutageDuration = 0 PowerOnValue.Value = true if NightState.currentPhase then ApplyPhaseLighting(NightState.currentPhase) end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do PowerOutageEvent:FireClient(player, { active = false, reason = reason, }) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "POWER_RESTORE", intensity = 0.4, duration = 0.8, }) end end local function UpdatePowerOutage(dt) if not NightState.powerOutageActive then return end NightState.powerOutageTimer = NightState.powerOutageTimer + dt if NightState.powerOutageDuration < 999 and NightState.powerOutageTimer >= NightState.powerOutageDuration then RestorePower("TIMEOUT") end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL SPAWNING LOGIC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldSpawnSignal(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return false end if #phase.signalTypes == 0 then return false end if #NightState.activeSignals >= phase.maxActiveSignals then return false end local chance = phase.signalSpawnChance * nightScaling.signalFrequencyMultiplier * dt return math.random() < chance end local function PickSignalType(phase, nightScaling) if not phase or #phase.signalTypes == 0 then return "SAFE" end local availableTypes = {} for _, sType in ipairs(phase.signalTypes) do local allowed = true if sType == "FALSE" and NightState.currentNight < 2 then local hasFalse = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "FALSE_SIGNALS" then hasFalse = true break end end end if not hasFalse then allowed = false end end if sType == "CRITICAL" then local hasCritical = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "CRITICAL_SIGNALS" then hasCritical = true break end end end if not hasCritical then allowed = false end end if allowed then table.insert(availableTypes, sType) end end if #availableTypes == 0 then return "SAFE" end return availableTypes[math.random(1, #availableTypes)] end local function SpawnSignal(signalType) local signalId = "SIG_" .. tostring(tick()) .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(1000, 9999)) local signalData = { id = signalId, type = signalType, frequency = math.random(880, 1080) / 10, spawnTime = NightState.elapsedTime, duration = 15 + math.random(0, 30), active = true, logged = false, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, phaseWhenSpawned = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", } table.insert(NightState.activeSignals, signalData) NightState.signalsSpawned = NightState.signalsSpawned + 1 if signalType == "SAFE" then NightState.signalsSafe = NightState.signalsSafe + 1 elseif signalType == "DANGEROUS" then NightState.signalsDangerous = NightState.signalsDangerous + 1 elseif signalType == "FALSE" then NightState.signalsFalse = NightState.signalsFalse + 1 elseif signalType == "CRITICAL" then NightState.signalsCritical = NightState.signalsCritical + 1 end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do SignalSpawnRequest:FireClient(player, signalData) end return signalData end local function UpdateActiveSignals(dt) local toRemove = {} for i, signal in ipairs(NightState.activeSignals) do if signal.active then local elapsed = NightState.elapsedTime - signal.spawnTime if elapsed >= signal.duration then signal.active = false table.insert(toRemove, i) end end end for i = #toRemove, 1, -1 do table.remove(NightState.activeSignals, toRemove[i]) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ANOMALY SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldTriggerAnomaly(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return false end if #phase.anomalyTypes == 0 then return false end local chance = phase.anomalyChance * nightScaling.anomalyFrequencyMultiplier * dt return math.random() < chance end local function PickAnomalyType(phase, nightScaling) if not phase or #phase.anomalyTypes == 0 then return "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" end local availableTypes = {} for _, aType in ipairs(phase.anomalyTypes) do local allowed = true if aType == "TEMPORAL_DISTORTION" then local hasTemporal = false if nightScaling and nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "TEMPORAL_ANOMALIES" then hasTemporal = true break end end end if not hasTemporal then allowed = false end end if aType == "REALITY_TEAR" then local hasReality = false if nightScaling and nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "REALITY_DISTORTION" then hasReality = true break end end end if not hasReality then allowed = false end end if allowed then table.insert(availableTypes, aType) end end if #availableTypes == 0 then return "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" end return availableTypes[math.random(1, #availableTypes)] end local function TriggerAnomaly(anomalyType) local anomalyId = "ANOM_" .. tostring(tick()) .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(1000, 9999)) local anomalyData = { id = anomalyId, type = anomalyType, triggerTime = NightState.elapsedTime, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, threatLevelWhenTriggered = NightState.threatLevel, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", } table.insert(NightState.activeAnomalies, anomalyData) NightState.anomaliesTriggered = NightState.anomaliesTriggered + 1 for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do AnomalyTrigger:FireClient(player, anomalyData) end if anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MINOR" or anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR" then local intensity = anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR" and 0.8 or 0.4 local duration = anomalyType == "LIGHT_FLICKER_MAJOR" and 2.0 or 0.8 for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = intensity, duration = duration, source = anomalyType, }) end end if anomalyType == "TEMPORAL_DISTORTION" or anomalyType == "REALITY_TEAR" or anomalyType == "GRAVITY_SHIFT" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = anomalyType, intensity = 0.5 + NightState.threatLevel * 0.3, duration = 1.5 + math.random() * 2.0, }) end end return anomalyData end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ENTITY SPAWN LOGIC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldSpawnEntity(phase, nightScaling, dt) if not phase or not nightScaling then return false end if NightState.entityActive then return false end if phase.entitySpawnChance <= 0 then return false end local hasEntityMechanic = false if nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "ENTITY_PATROL" or m == "ENTITY_BREACH" or m == "FINAL_CONFRONTATION" then hasEntityMechanic = true break end end end if not hasEntityMechanic and NightState.currentNight < 3 then return false end local chance = phase.entitySpawnChance * nightScaling.entityAggressionMultiplier * dt return math.random() < chance end local function SpawnEntity() NightState.entityActive = true NightState.entityAppearances = NightState.entityAppearances + 1 local spawnData = { nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, spawnTime = NightState.elapsedTime, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", aggression = NightState.nightScaling and NightState.nightScaling.entityAggressionMultiplier or 1.0, canBreach = false, } if NightState.nightScaling and NightState.nightScaling.newMechanics then for _, m in ipairs(NightState.nightScaling.newMechanics) do if m == "ENTITY_BREACH" or m == "FINAL_CONFRONTATION" then spawnData.canBreach = true break end end end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EntitySpawnRequest:FireClient(player, spawnData) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "ENTITY_NEARBY", intensity = 0.3, duration = 3.0, }) end return spawnData end local function DespawnEntity(reason) if not NightState.entityActive then return end NightState.entityActive = false NightState.entityPosition = nil for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EntitySpawnRequest:FireClient(player, { despawn = true, reason = reason, }) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PHASE EVENT SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function TriggerPhaseEvents(phase, nightScaling) if not phase then return end local phaseKey = phase.name .. "_" .. tostring(NightState.currentNight) if NightState.phaseEventsTriggered[phaseKey] then return end NightState.phaseEventsTriggered[phaseKey] = true if phase.events then for _, eventName in ipairs(phase.events) do if not NightState.triggeredEvents[eventName] then NightState.triggeredEvents[eventName] = true for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "PHASE_EVENT", event = eventName, phase = phase.name, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, }) end if eventName == "STATION_BOOT_SEQUENCE" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do StationStatusUpdate:FireClient(player, { status = "BOOTING", message = "Система запускается...", }) end elseif eventName == "DAWN_SEQUENCE" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "DAWN_LIGHT", intensity = 0.6, duration = 5.0, }) end elseif eventName == "ENTITY_RETREAT" then DespawnEntity("DAWN") elseif eventName == "STATION_NORMALIZE" then if NightState.powerOutageActive then RestorePower("DAWN_NORMALIZE") end elseif eventName == "ENTITY_PATROL_START" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "WARNING", message = "Что-то движется снаружи...", duration = 4.0, }) end elseif eventName == "TOTAL_DARKNESS_FLASH" then TriggerPowerOutage("CLIMAX_EVENT", 3) for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "TOTAL_DARKNESS", intensity = 1.0, duration = 3.0, }) end elseif eventName == "STATION_SHAKE" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "STATION_SHAKE", intensity = 0.15, duration = 4.0, }) end elseif eventName == "ALL_LIGHTS_FLICKER" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = 1.0, duration = 4.0, source = "ALL_LIGHTS_EVENT", allLights = true, }) end end end end end if nightScaling and nightScaling.specialEvents then for _, specialEvent in ipairs(nightScaling.specialEvents) do local specialKey = specialEvent .. "_NIGHT_" .. tostring(NightState.currentNight) if not NightState.triggeredSpecialEvents[specialKey] then local shouldTrigger = false if specialEvent == "TUTORIAL_RADIO" and phase.name == "EARLY" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "TUTORIAL_GENERATOR" and phase.name == "RISING" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "FIRST_FALSE_SIGNAL" and phase.name == "MID" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "ENTITY_FIRST_SIGHTING" and phase.name == "ESCALATION" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "STATION_HISTORY_REVEAL" and phase.name == "MID" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "ENTITY_ENTERS_STATION" and phase.name == "PEAK" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "HIDDEN_SIGNAL_CLUE" and phase.name == "ESCALATION" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "FINAL_NIGHT_SEQUENCE" and phase.name == "CLIMAX" then shouldTrigger = true elseif specialEvent == "HIDDEN_ENDING_CHECK" and phase.name == "RESOLUTION" then shouldTrigger = true end if shouldTrigger then NightState.triggeredSpecialEvents[specialKey] = true for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "SPECIAL_EVENT", event = specialEvent, phase = phase.name, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, }) end end end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PSYCHOLOGY SYSTEM (THROTTLED) ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdatePlayerPsychology(dt) if not NightState.currentPhase then return end local phase = NightState.currentPhase local scaling = NightState.nightScaling local paranoiaRate = phase.paranoiaGrowth local doubtRate = phase.doubtGrowth if scaling then paranoiaRate = paranoiaRate * scaling.paranoiaMultiplier doubtRate = doubtRate * scaling.paranoiaMultiplier end if NightState.powerOutageActive then paranoiaRate = paranoiaRate * 1.5 end if NightState.entityActive then paranoiaRate = paranoiaRate * 2.0 doubtRate = doubtRate * 1.3 end NightState.playerParanoia = math.clamp(NightState.playerParanoia + paranoiaRate * dt, 0, 100) NightState.playerDoubt = math.clamp(NightState.playerDoubt + doubtRate * dt, 0, 100) local sanityDrain = (NightState.playerParanoia / 100) * 0.01 * dt if NightState.entityActive then sanityDrain = sanityDrain * 3 end NightState.playerSanity = math.clamp(NightState.playerSanity - sanityDrain, 0, 100) for _, pState in pairs(PlayerStates) do if pState.alive then pState.paranoia = NightState.playerParanoia pState.doubt = NightState.playerDoubt pState.sanity = NightState.playerSanity pState.fear = math.clamp(NightState.threatLevel * 100, 0, 100) end end -- Отправка только по таймеру (контролируется в NightUpdate) for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do PsychologyUpdate:FireClient(player, { paranoia = NightState.playerParanoia, doubt = NightState.playerDoubt, sanity = NightState.playerSanity, fear = NightState.threatLevel * 100, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, }) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LIGHT FLICKER (THROTTLED) ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateLightFlicker() if not NightState.currentPhase then return end if NightState.powerOutageActive then return end local phase = NightState.currentPhase if math.random() < phase.lightFlickerChance then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do FlickerLightsEvent:FireClient(player, { intensity = phase.lightFlickerIntensity * (0.7 + math.random() * 0.6), duration = phase.lightFlickerDuration * (0.5 + math.random()), source = "AMBIENT_FLICKER", }) end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- RANDOM POWER OUTAGE CHECK ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CheckRandomPowerOutage(phase, nightScaling) if not phase or not nightScaling then return end if NightState.powerOutageActive then return end if phase.powerOutageChance <= 0 then return end local chance = phase.powerOutageChance * nightScaling.powerOutageMultiplier if math.random() < chance then local duration = phase.powerOutageDuration * (0.8 + math.random() * 0.4) TriggerPowerOutage("RANDOM", duration) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN NIGHT CYCLE ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CalculateNightDuration(nightNumber) local duration = NightConfig.BASE_NIGHT_DURATION + (nightNumber - 1) * NightConfig.DURATION_INCREMENT_PER_NIGHT return math.min(duration, NightConfig.MAX_NIGHT_DURATION) end local function ResetNightState(nightNumber) NightState.active = false NightState.currentNight = nightNumber NightState.elapsedTime = 0 NightState.totalDuration = CalculateNightDuration(nightNumber) NightState.currentPhaseIndex = 0 NightState.currentPhase = nil NightState.previousPhase = nil NightState.threatLevel = 0 NightState.powerOn = true NightState.generatorFuel = 100 NightState.generatorRunning = true NightState.powerOutageActive = false NightState.powerOutageTimer = 0 NightState.powerOutageDuration = 0 NightState.lastTimeSyncTick = 0 NightState.lastLightingUpdateTick = 0 NightState.lastEventCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastThreatUpdateTick = 0 NightState.lastGeneratorTick = 0 NightState.lastSignalCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastAnomalyCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastEntityCheckTick = 0 NightState.lastFlickerTick = 0 NightState.lastPsychologyTick = 0 NightState.lastAmbientSoundTick = 0 NightState.lastCameraEffectTick = 0 NightState.signalsSpawned = 0 NightState.signalsSafe = 0 NightState.signalsDangerous = 0 NightState.signalsFalse = 0 NightState.signalsCritical = 0 NightState.anomaliesTriggered = 0 NightState.entityAppearances = 0 NightState.powerOutages = 0 NightState.totalSignalsLogged = 0 NightState.activeSignals = {} NightState.activeAnomalies = {} NightState.entityActive = false NightState.entityPosition = nil NightState.playerAlive = true NightState.playerSanity = 100 NightState.playerParanoia = 0 NightState.playerDoubt = 0 NightState.triggeredEvents = {} NightState.triggeredSpecialEvents = {} NightState.phaseEventsTriggered = {} NightState.endingConditions = { safeSignalsLogged = 0, dangerousSignalsHandled = 0, entityEncountersSurvived = 0, generatorMaintained = true, hiddenSignalFound = false, stationIntact = true, playerSanityAbove50 = true, } NightState.nightScaling = NightScaling[math.min(nightNumber, #NightScaling)] CurrentNightValue.Value = nightNumber CurrentPhaseValue.Value = "INACTIVE" NightActiveValue.Value = false ThreatLevelValue.Value = 0 ElapsedTimeValue.Value = 0 NightDurationValue.Value = NightState.totalDuration PowerOnValue.Value = true GeneratorFuelValue.Value = 100 end local function DetermineEnding() local conditions = NightState.endingConditions local endingType = "NEUTRAL" local endingData = {} if conditions.hiddenSignalFound then endingType = "HIDDEN" endingData = { title = "Истина раскрыта", description = "Вы нашли скрытый сигнал и узнали правду о станции.", variant = "HIDDEN_TRUTH", } elseif conditions.safeSignalsLogged >= 10 and conditions.stationIntact and conditions.playerSanityAbove50 and conditions.generatorMaintained then endingType = "GOOD" endingData = { title = "Рассвет", description = "Вы пережили все ночи. Станция спасена. Вы свободны.", variant = "FULL_SURVIVAL", } elseif not conditions.stationIntact or not conditions.playerSanityAbove50 then endingType = "BAD" endingData = { title = "Поглощение", description = "Станция разрушена. Тьма победила.", variant = "STATION_LOST", } else endingType = "NEUTRAL" endingData = { title = "Выживание", description = "Вы пережили ночи, но потеряли часть себя.", variant = "PARTIAL_SURVIVAL", } end endingData.type = endingType endingData.nightsSurvived = NightState.currentNight endingData.finalStats = { totalSignals = NightState.signalsSpawned, safeSignals = NightState.signalsSafe, dangerousSignals = NightState.signalsDangerous, anomalies = NightState.anomaliesTriggered, entityEncounters = NightState.entityAppearances, finalSanity = NightState.playerSanity, } for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EndingTriggered:FireClient(player, endingData) end print("[NightCycle] Ending triggered: " .. endingType .. " — " .. endingData.title) end local function KillPlayer(player, cause) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if not pState or not pState.alive then return end pState.alive = false NightState.playerAlive = false PlayerDeathEvent:FireClient(player, { cause = cause, nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", timeSurvived = NightState.elapsedTime, }) CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "DEATH", intensity = 1.0, duration = 5.0, cause = cause, }) task.delay(3.0, function() EndNight("PLAYER_DEATH") NightState.endingConditions.stationIntact = false if NightState.currentNight >= NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS then task.delay(2.0, function() DetermineEnding() end) end end) end local function EndNight(reason) if not NightState.active then return end NightState.active = false NightActiveValue.Value = false CurrentPhaseValue.Value = "ENDED" if NightState.entityActive then DespawnEntity("NIGHT_END") end NightState.endingConditions.playerSanityAbove50 = NightState.playerSanity > 50 local survived = reason == "COMPLETED" or reason == "DAWN" local nightResult = { nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, survived = survived, reason = reason, elapsedTime = NightState.elapsedTime, totalDuration = NightState.totalDuration, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, signalsSpawned = NightState.signalsSpawned, signalsSafe = NightState.signalsSafe, signalsDangerous = NightState.signalsDangerous, signalsFalse = NightState.signalsFalse, signalsCritical = NightState.signalsCritical, anomaliesTriggered = NightState.anomaliesTriggered, entityAppearances = NightState.entityAppearances, powerOutages = NightState.powerOutages, finalSanity = NightState.playerSanity, finalParanoia = NightState.playerParanoia, endingConditions = NightState.endingConditions, } for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightEnded:FireClient(player, nightResult) if survived then NightSurvived:FireClient(player, nightResult) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if pState then pState.nightsSurvived = pState.nightsSurvived + 1 end end end if NightState.currentNight >= NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS and survived then task.delay(3.0, function() DetermineEnding() end) end print("[NightCycle] Night " .. tostring(NightState.currentNight) .. " ended. Reason: " .. reason .. ". Survived: " .. tostring(survived)) end local function StartNight(nightNumber) ResetNightState(nightNumber) SetupLightingEffects() local initialPhase = NightPhases[1] if initialPhase then ApplyPhaseLighting(initialPhase) end NightState.active = true NightActiveValue.Value = true CurrentPhaseValue.Value = "STARTING" for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightStarted:FireClient(player, { nightNumber = nightNumber, duration = NightState.totalDuration, scaling = NightState.nightScaling and { threatMultiplier = NightState.nightScaling.threatMultiplier, description = NightState.nightScaling.description, } or nil, }) end print("[NightCycle] Night " .. tostring(nightNumber) .. " started. Duration: " .. tostring(NightState.totalDuration) .. "s") end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN UPDATE LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ local function NightUpdate(dt) if not NightState.active then return end if not NightState.playerAlive then return end NightState.elapsedTime = NightState.elapsedTime + dt ElapsedTimeValue.Value = NightState.elapsedTime local nightProgress = GetNightProgress() if nightProgress >= 1.0 then EndNight("COMPLETED") return end -- Определение текущей фазы local newPhase, newIndex = GetCurrentPhaseData(nightProgress) if newPhase and (NightState.currentPhase == nil or NightState.currentPhase.name ~= newPhase.name) then NightState.previousPhase = NightState.currentPhase NightState.currentPhase = newPhase NightState.currentPhaseIndex = newIndex CurrentPhaseValue.Value = newPhase.name for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightPhaseChanged:FireClient(player, { phase = newPhase.name, displayName = newPhase.displayName, phaseIndex = newIndex, totalPhases = #NightPhases, nightProgress = nightProgress, threatRange = {newPhase.baseThreatLevel, newPhase.maxThreatLevel}, }) end TriggerPhaseEvents(newPhase, NightState.nightScaling) print("[NightCycle] Phase changed to: " .. newPhase.name .. " (" .. newPhase.displayName .. ") at " .. string.format("%.1f%%", nightProgress * 100)) end local currentTick = tick() -- Синхронизация времени (каждые 2 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastTimeSyncTick >= NightConfig.TIME_SYNC_INTERVAL then NightState.lastTimeSyncTick = currentTick for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do NightTimeSync:FireClient(player, { elapsed = NightState.elapsedTime, total = NightState.totalDuration, progress = nightProgress, phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "UNKNOWN", threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, powerOn = NightState.powerOn, generatorFuel = NightState.generatorFuel, }) end end -- Обновление освещения (каждую 1 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastLightingUpdateTick >= NightConfig.LIGHTING_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastLightingUpdateTick = currentTick if not NightState.powerOutageActive then local fromPhase, toPhase, transitionAlpha = GetInterpolatedPhaseValues(nightProgress) if fromPhase and toPhase and transitionAlpha > 0 then ApplyPhaseTransitionLighting(fromPhase, toPhase, transitionAlpha) elseif fromPhase then ApplyPhaseLighting(fromPhase) end end end -- Обновление угрозы (каждые 4 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastThreatUpdateTick >= NightConfig.THREAT_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastThreatUpdateTick = currentTick UpdateThreatLevel(NightConfig.THREAT_UPDATE_INTERVAL) end -- Обновление генератора (каждые 1 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastGeneratorTick >= 1.0 then NightState.lastGeneratorTick = currentTick UpdateGenerator(1.0) end -- Обновление отключения электричества UpdatePowerOutage(dt) -- Мерцание (каждые 2 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastFlickerTick >= NightConfig.FLICKER_CHECK_INTERVAL then NightState.lastFlickerTick = currentTick UpdateLightFlicker() end -- Проверка сигналов (каждые 3 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastSignalCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL then NightState.lastSignalCheckTick = currentTick if ShouldSpawnSignal(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL) then local signalType = PickSignalType(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling) SpawnSignal(signalType) end UpdateActiveSignals(NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL) end -- Проверка аномалий (каждые 3 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastAnomalyCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL then NightState.lastAnomalyCheckTick = currentTick if ShouldTriggerAnomaly(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL) then local anomalyType = PickAnomalyType(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling) TriggerAnomaly(anomalyType) end end -- Проверка появления сущности (каждые 6 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastEntityCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 2 then NightState.lastEntityCheckTick = currentTick if ShouldSpawnEntity(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling, NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 2) then SpawnEntity() end end -- Случайное отключение электричества (каждые 9 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastEventCheckTick >= NightConfig.EVENT_CHECK_INTERVAL * 3 then NightState.lastEventCheckTick = currentTick CheckRandomPowerOutage(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling) end -- Обновление психологии (каждые 3 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastPsychologyTick >= NightConfig.PSYCHOLOGY_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastPsychologyTick = currentTick UpdatePlayerPsychology(NightConfig.PSYCHOLOGY_UPDATE_INTERVAL) end -- Обновление звука (каждые 8 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastAmbientSoundTick >= NightConfig.AMBIENT_SOUND_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastAmbientSoundTick = currentTick if NightState.currentPhase and not NightState.powerOutageActive then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do AmbientSoundUpdate:FireClient(player, { event = "AMBIENT_UPDATE", volume = NightState.currentPhase.ambientVolume, windVolume = NightState.currentPhase.windVolume, creepyVolume = NightState.currentPhase.creepyAmbientVolume, pitch = NightState.currentPhase.ambientPitch, threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, }) end end end -- Обновление камеры (каждые 4 сек) if currentTick - NightState.lastCameraEffectTick >= NightConfig.CAMERA_EFFECT_UPDATE_INTERVAL then NightState.lastCameraEffectTick = currentTick if NightState.currentPhase then local shakeIntensity = NightState.currentPhase.cameraShakeIntensity local chromaticIntensity = NightState.currentPhase.chromaticAberrationIntensity if NightState.entityActive then shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity + 0.05 chromaticIntensity = chromaticIntensity + 0.04 end if NightState.powerOutageActive then shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity + 0.02 chromaticIntensity = chromaticIntensity + 0.03 end if shakeIntensity > 0 or chromaticIntensity > 0 then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = "CONTINUOUS", shakeIntensity = shakeIntensity, chromaticIntensity = chromaticIntensity, duration = 1.0, }) end end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- REMOTE FUNCTION HANDLERS ------------------------------------------------------------ GetNightData.OnServerInvoke = function(player) return { active = NightState.active, currentNight = NightState.currentNight, elapsedTime = NightState.elapsedTime, totalDuration = NightState.totalDuration, progress = GetNightProgress(), phase = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.name or "INACTIVE", phaseDisplayName = NightState.currentPhase and NightState.currentPhase.displayName or "", threatLevel = NightState.threatLevel, powerOn = NightState.powerOn, generatorFuel = NightState.generatorFuel, playerSanity = NightState.playerSanity, playerParanoia = NightState.playerParanoia, playerDoubt = NightState.playerDoubt, signalsActive = #NightState.activeSignals, entityActive = NightState.entityActive, totalNights = NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS, } end GetPlayerProgress.OnServerInvoke = function(player) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if not pState then return nil end return { nightsSurvived = pState.nightsSurvived, totalScore = pState.totalScore, currentNight = NightState.currentNight, alive = pState.alive, sanity = pState.sanity, paranoia = pState.paranoia, } end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- EXTERNAL API ------------------------------------------------------------ local NightCycleAPI = {} NightCycleAPI.StartNight = StartNight NightCycleAPI.EndNight = EndNight NightCycleAPI.GetState = function() return NightState end NightCycleAPI.GetPhase = function() return NightState.currentPhase end NightCycleAPI.GetThreatLevel = function() return NightState.threatLevel end NightCycleAPI.GetProgress = GetNightProgress NightCycleAPI.IsActive = function() return NightState.active end NightCycleAPI.GetCurrentNight = function() return NightState.currentNight end NightCycleAPI.RefuelGenerator = RefuelGenerator NightCycleAPI.TriggerPowerOutage = TriggerPowerOutage NightCycleAPI.RestorePower = RestorePower NightCycleAPI.KillPlayer = KillPlayer NightCycleAPI.SpawnEntity = SpawnEntity NightCycleAPI.DespawnEntity = DespawnEntity NightCycleAPI.TriggerAnomaly = TriggerAnomaly NightCycleAPI.SpawnSignal = SpawnSignal NightCycleAPI.LogSignal = function(signalId, player) for _, signal in ipairs(NightState.activeSignals) do if signal.id == signalId and not signal.logged then signal.logged = true NightState.totalSignalsLogged = NightState.totalSignalsLogged + 1 if signal.type == "SAFE" then NightState.endingConditions.safeSignalsLogged = NightState.endingConditions.safeSignalsLogged + 1 elseif signal.type == "DANGEROUS" then NightState.endingConditions.dangerousSignalsHandled = NightState.endingConditions.dangerousSignalsHandled + 1 end local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if pState then table.insert(pState.signalsLogged, { id = signalId, type = signal.type, frequency = signal.frequency, night = NightState.currentNight, }) end return true, signal end end return false, nil end NightCycleAPI.SetHiddenSignalFound = function(found) NightState.endingConditions.hiddenSignalFound = found end NightCycleAPI.MarkStationDamaged = function() NightState.endingConditions.stationIntact = false end NightCycleAPI.MarkGeneratorFailed = function() NightState.endingConditions.generatorMaintained = false end NightCycleAPI.IncrementEntitySurvival = function() NightState.endingConditions.entityEncountersSurvived = NightState.endingConditions.entityEncountersSurvived + 1 end NightCycleAPI.AddPlayerNoise = function(player, amount) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if pState then pState.noiseLevel = math.clamp(pState.noiseLevel + amount, 0, 1) end end NightCycleAPI.SetPlayerRoom = function(player, roomName) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if pState then pState.currentRoom = roomName end end -- BindableFunction API для других серверных скриптов local APIBindable = Instance.new("BindableFunction") APIBindable.Name = "NightCycleAPIAccess" APIBindable.Parent = ReplicatedStorage APIBindable.OnInvoke = function(method, ...) if NightCycleAPI[method] then return NightCycleAPI[method](...) end return nil end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- REMOTE EVENT HANDLERS (Validation) ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ValidatePlayerAction(player) local pState = GetPlayerState(player) if not pState then return false end if not pState.alive then return false end if not NightState.active then return false end local now = tick() if now - pState.lastActivity < 0.1 then return false end pState.lastActivity = now return true end GeneratorInteract.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, action, data) if not ValidatePlayerAction(player) then return end if action == "REFUEL" then RefuelGenerator(25) elseif action == "RESTART" then if NightState.generatorFuel > 5 then NightState.generatorRunning = true RestorePower("MANUAL_RESTART") end end end) LogSignalRemote.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, signalId) if not ValidatePlayerAction(player) then return end if type(signalId) ~= "string" then return end local success, signal = NightCycleAPI.LogSignal(signalId, player) if success and signal then UINotification:FireClient(player, { type = "SIGNAL_LOGGED", signalType = signal.type, signalId = signal.id, frequency = signal.frequency, }) if signal.type == "DANGEROUS" or signal.type == "CRITICAL" then local anomalyChance = signal.type == "CRITICAL" and 0.6 or 0.3 if math.random() < anomalyChance then task.delay(1.0 + math.random() * 3.0, function() if NightState.active then local anomalyType = PickAnomalyType(NightState.currentPhase, NightState.nightScaling) TriggerAnomaly(anomalyType) end end) end end end end) PlayerNoiseRemote.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, noiseLevel) if not ValidatePlayerAction(player) then return end if type(noiseLevel) ~= "number" then return end noiseLevel = math.clamp(noiseLevel, 0, 1) NightCycleAPI.AddPlayerNoise(player, noiseLevel) if NightState.entityActive and noiseLevel > 0.5 then for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do EntitySpawnRequest:FireClient(p, { update = true, playerNoise = noiseLevel, attractEntity = true, }) end end end) PlayerRoomChange.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, roomName) if not ValidatePlayerAction(player) then return end if type(roomName) ~= "string" then return end NightCycleAPI.SetPlayerRoom(player, roomName) end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PLAYER CONNECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player) InitializePlayerState(player) if NightState.active then task.delay(2.0, function() if player.Parent then NightStarted:FireClient(player, { nightNumber = NightState.currentNight, duration = NightState.totalDuration, alreadyInProgress = true, elapsedTime = NightState.elapsedTime, }) if NightState.currentPhase then NightPhaseChanged:FireClient(player, { phase = NightState.currentPhase.name, displayName = NightState.currentPhase.displayName, phaseIndex = NightState.currentPhaseIndex, totalPhases = #NightPhases, nightProgress = GetNightProgress(), threatRange = {NightState.currentPhase.baseThreatLevel, NightState.currentPhase.maxThreatLevel}, }) end end end) end end) Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(player) RemovePlayerState(player) end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INITIALIZATION & MAIN LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ SetupLightingEffects() Lighting.ClockTime = 14 Lighting.Brightness = 1 Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(128, 128, 128) Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(128, 128, 128) Lighting.FogStart = 100 Lighting.FogEnd = 500 Lighting.FogColor = Color3.fromRGB(180, 190, 200) RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt) if NightState.active then NightUpdate(dt) end end) -- Автозапуск первой ночи local nightStarted = false local function TryStartFirstNight(player) if nightStarted then return end nightStarted = true task.delay(NightConfig.INITIAL_DELAY, function() local success, savedNight = pcall(function() local ds = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("HorrorRadioStation_Progress") return ds:GetAsync("Player_" .. tostring(player.UserId) .. "_CurrentNight") end) local startNight = 1 if success and savedNight and type(savedNight) == "number" and savedNight >= 1 and savedNight <= NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS then startNight = savedNight end StartNight(startNight) end) end Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player) TryStartFirstNight(player) end) -- Если игроки уже есть for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do InitializePlayerState(player) TryStartFirstNight(player) end -- Автоматический переход к следующей ночи NightActiveValue.Changed:Connect(function(newValue) if newValue == false and NightState.playerAlive then if NightState.currentNight >= NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS then return end local nextNight = NightState.currentNight + 1 for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do pcall(function() local ds = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("HorrorRadioStation_Progress") ds:SetAsync("Player_" .. tostring(player.UserId) .. "_CurrentNight", nextNight) end) end task.delay(NightConfig.BETWEEN_NIGHTS_DELAY, function() StartNight(nextNight) end) end end) print("[NightCycle] Night Cycle System initialized. Total nights: " .. tostring(NightConfig.TOTAL_NIGHTS)) print("[NightCycle] Base night duration: " .. tostring(NightConfig.BASE_NIGHT_DURATION) .. "s") print("[NightCycle] Waiting for players...") ``` --- # Исправленный клиентский скрипт (Night Cycle Client Handler) **Тип скрипта:** LocalScript **Размещение:** StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → NightCycleClient ```lua --[[ NIGHT CYCLE CLIENT HANDLER — Production LocalScript Принимает и обрабатывает все серверные события ночного цикла. Ждёт маркер RemotesReady перед подключением. totalDuration = 720, nightProgress = 0, threatLevel = 0, paranoia = 0, doubt = 0, sanity = 100, fear = 0, powerOn = true, generatorFuel = 100, entityActive = false, baseCameraShake = 0, currentCameraShake = 0, chromaticAberration = 0, cameraShakeOffset = CFrame.new(), activeCameraEffects = {}, flickerActive = false, originalLightStates = {}, lightsCollected = false, ambientVolume = ------------------------------------------------------------ local function TweenSoundVolume(sound, targetVolume, duration) if not sound then return end local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(duration or tweenInfo, {PlaybackSpeed = targetPitch}) tween:Play() return tween end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- POST-PROCESSING REFERENCES ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GetOrCreateEffect(className, name) local effect = Lighting:FindFirstChild(name) if not effect then effect = VignetteCC.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) VignetteCC.Enabled = false VignetteCC.Parent = Lighting end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- WORKSPACE LIGHT COLLECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local WorkspaceLights = {} local WorkspaceLightsOriginal = {} local function CollectWorkspaceLights() if ClientState.lightsCollected then return end ClientState.lightsCollected = true local function ScanForLights(parent) for _, child in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("PointLight") or child:IsA("SpotLight") or child:IsA("SurfaceLight") then table.insert(WorkspaceLights, child) WorkspaceLightsOriginal[child] = { Brightness = child.Brightness, Color = child.Color, Enabled = child.Enabled, } end if child:IsA("Model") or child:IsA("Folder") or child:IsA("Part") or child:IsA("MeshPart") then ScanForLights(child) end end end ScanForLights(workspace) end local function RestoreAllLights() for light, original in pairs(WorkspaceLightsOriginal) do if light and light.Parent then light.Brightness = original.Brightness light.Color = original.Color light.Enabled = original.Enabled end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CAMERA EFFECTS SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local CameraEffectCoroutines = {} local function ApplyCameraShake(intensity, duration) local startTime = tick() local id = "shake_" .. tostring(startTime) .. "_" .. tostring(math.random(1000, 9999)) CameraEffectCoroutines[id] = true task.spawn(function() while CameraEffectCoroutines[id] and (tick() - startTime) < duration do local progress = (tick() - startTime) / duration local fadeMultiplier = 1.0 if progress < 0.1 then fadeMultiplier = progress / 0.1 elseif progress > 0.8 then fadeMultiplier = (1.0 - progress) / 0.2 end local shakeX = (math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * intensity * fadeMultiplier local shakeY = (math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * intensity * fadeMultiplier local shakeZ = (math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * intensity * fadeMultiplier * 0.3 local rotX = (math.random() - 0.5) * intensity * fadeMultiplier * 0.5 local rotY = (math.random() - 0.5) * intensity * fadeMultiplier * 0.3 ClientState.cameraShakeOffset = CFrame.new(shakeX, shakeY, shakeZ) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(rotX), math.rad(rotY), 0) RunService.RenderStepped:Wait() end CameraEffectCoroutines[id] = nil ClientState.cameraShakeOffset = CFrame.new() end) return id end local function ApplyContinuousCameraShake(intensity) ClientState.baseCameraShake = intensity end local function ApplyChromaticAberration(intensity, duration) if not ChromaticCC then return end ChromaticCC.Enabled = intensity > 0.001 local aberrationStrength = math.clamp(intensity, 0, 1) local r = math.clamp(255 + aberrationStrength * 30, 0, 255) local g = math.clamp(255 - aberrationStrength * 15, 0, 255) local b = math.clamp(255 - aberrationStrength * 20, 0, 255) ChromaticCC.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(r, g, b) ChromaticCC.Contrast = aberrationStrength * 0.1 ChromaticCC.Saturation = -aberrationStrength * 0.2 if duration and duration > 0 then task.delay(duration, function() if ChromaticCC then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(ChromaticCC, tweenInfo, {Contrast = 0, Saturation = 0}):Play() ChromaticCC.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255) task.delay(0.5, function() if ChromaticCC then ChromaticCC.Enabled = false end end) end end) end end local function ApplyDeathEffect(cause, duration) ClientState.isDead = true ClientState.playerAlive = false if DeathBlur then DeathBlur.Enabled = true local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(duration or 5.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.In) TweenService:Create(DeathBlur, tweenInfo, {Size = 56}):Play() end if NightColorCorrection then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(duration or 5.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.In) TweenService:Create(NightColorCorrection, tweenInfo, { Brightness = -0.3, Contrast = 0.5, Saturation = -1.0, }):Play() end ApplyCameraShake(0.15, 3.0) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.5, duration) TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, 0, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, 0, 1.0) TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0.6, 1.0) task.delay(2.0, function() TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 3.0) end) end local function ApplyDawnEffect(intensity, duration) if NightColorCorrection Contrast = 0.02, TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 245, 230), }):Play() end if NightBloom then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(duration or 5.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightBloom, tweenInfo, { Intensity = 0.2, Size = 14, Threshold = 1.5, }):Play() end if DawnSound then DawnSound.Volume = 0 DawnSound:Play() TweenSoundVolume(DawnSound, 0.3, 2.0) end TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, 0, 3.0) TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0.08, 4.0) TweenSoundVolume(WindSound, 0.05, 4.0) end local function ApplyPowerOutageEffect() if PowerDownSound then PowerDownSound.Volume = 0.5 PowerDownSound:Play() end ApplyCameraShake(0.08, 1.5) CollectWorkspaceLights() for _, light in ipairs(WorkspaceLights) do if light and light.Parent then light.Enabled = false end end TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0.25, 1.0) TweenSoundVolume(CreepyAmbient, 0.5, 0.5) TweenSoundVolume(AmbientSound, 0.05, 0.5) end local function ApplyPowerRestoreEffect() if PowerUpSound then PowerUpSound.Volume = 0.5 PowerUpSound:Play() end RestoreAllLights() if NightBloom then local originalIntensity = NightBloom.Intensity NightBloom.Intensity = originalIntensity + 0.5 local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.8, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightBloom, tweenInfo, {Intensity = originalIntensity}):Play() end TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) end local function ApplyStationShakeEffect(intensity, duration) ApplyCameraShake(intensity or 0.15, duration or 4.0) if StaticSound then StaticSound.Volume = 0.3 StaticSound:Play() task.delay(duration or 4.0, function() TweenSoundVolume(StaticSound, 0, 0.5) end) end end local function ApplyTotalDarknessEffect(intensity, duration) if NightColorCorrection then local original = { Brightness = NightColorCorrection.Brightness, Contrast = NightColorCorrection.Contrast, } NightColorCorrection.Brightness = -0.5 NightColorCorrection.Contrast = 0.8 task.delay(duration or 3.0, function() if NightColorCorrection then local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(1.0, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out) TweenService:Create(NightColorCorrection, tweenInfo, { Brightness = original.Brightness, Contrast = original.Contrast, }):Play() end end) end ApplyCameraShake(0.2, duration or 3.0) ApplyChromaticAberration(0.4, duration or 3.0) end local function ApplyEntityNearbyEffect(intensity, duration) ApplyCameraShake(intensity * 0.3, duration) ApplyChromaticAberration(intensity * 0.4, duration) TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0.15 + intensity * 0.3, 0.5) task.delay(duration, function() if not ClientState.entityActive then TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) end end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LIGHT FLICKER SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function FlickerLights(data) if ClientState.flickerActive then return end ClientState.flickerActive = true CollectWorkspaceLights() local intensity = data.intensity or 0.5 local duration = data.duration or 1.0 local allLights = data.allLights or false local lightsToFlicker = {} if allLights then lightsToFlicker = WorkspaceLights else local count = math.max(1, math.floor(#WorkspaceLights * intensity * 0.5)) local indices = {} for i = 1, #WorkspaceLights do table.insert(indices, i) end for i = #indices, 2, -1 do local j = math.random(1, i) indices[i], indices[j] = indices[j], indices[i] end for i = 1, math.min(count, #indices) do table.insert(lightsToFlicker, WorkspaceLights[indices[i]]) end end task.spawn(function() local startTime = tick() local flickerCount = math.floor(duration / 0.1) for i = 1, flickerCount do if (tick() - startTime) >= duration then break end for _, light in ipairs(lightsToFlicker) do if light and light.Parent then local original = WorkspaceLightsOriginal[light] if original then if math.random() < intensity then light.Brightness = original.Brightness * (math.random() * 0.3) if math.random() < 0.3 * intensity then light.Enabled = false end else light.Brightness = original.Brightness light.Enabled = original.Enabled end end end end task.wait(0.05 + math.random() * 0.1) end for _, light in ipairs(lightsToFlicker) do if light and light.Parent then local original = WorkspaceLightsOriginal[light] if original then light.Brightness = original.Brightness light.Enabled = original.Enabled end end end ClientState.flickerActive = false end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PSYCHOLOGY VISUAL EFFECTS ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ApplyParanoiaVisuals(paranoia, sanity, fear) if VignetteCC then local vignetteStrength = math.clamp(paranoia / 100, 0, 1) VignetteCC.Enabled = vignetteStrength > 0.05 if vignetteStrength > 0.05 then VignetteCC.Brightness = -vignetteStrength * 0.08 VignetteCC.Saturation = -vignetteStrength * 0.15 VignetteCC.Contrast = vignetteStrength * 0.05 end end if fear > 40 then local heartbeatVolume = math.clamp((fear - 40) / 60, 0, 1) * 0.4 if math.abs(HeartbeatSound.Volume - heartbeatVolume) > 0.02 then TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, heartbeatVolume, 1.0) end HeartbeatSound.PlaybackSpeed = 0.8 + (fear / 100) * 0.6 if not HeartbeatSound.IsPlaying then HeartbeatSound:Play() end elseif not ClientState.entityActive then if HeartbeatSound.Volume > 0.01 then TweenSoundVolume(HeartbeatSound, 0, 2.0) end end if sanity < 50 then local aberrationIntensity = math.clamp((50 - sanity) / 50, 0, 1) * 0.15 ApplyChromaticAberration(aberrationIntensity, 0) end end = continuousShakeTime + dt local shakeX = math.sin(continuousShakeTime * 15.3) * shakeIntensity * 0.05 local shakeY = math.cos(continuousShakeTime * 12.7) * shakeIntensity * 0.05 local rotX = math.sin(continuousShakeTime * 8.1) * shakeIntensity * 0.2 local rotY = math.cos(continuousShakeTime * 6.4) * shakeIntensity * 0.15 local continuousOffset = CFrame.new(shakeX, shakeY, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(rotX), math.rad(rotY), 0) local totalOffset = ClientState.cameraShakeOffset * continuousOffset Camera.CFrame = Camera.CFrame * totalOffset elseif ClientState.cameraShakeOffset ~= CFrame.new() then Camera.CFrame = Camera.CFrame * ClientState.cameraShakeOffset end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PLAYER NOISE DETECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local lastNoiseReport = 0 local lastPosition = nil RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt) if not ClientState.nightActive then return end if ClientState.isDead then return end local character = LocalPlayer.Character if not character then return end local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") local rootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") if not humanoid or not rootPart then return end local noiseLevel = 0 local moveSpeed = rootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude if moveSpeed > 14 then noiseLevel = 0.7 elseif moveSpeed > 8 then noiseLevel = 0.3 elseif moveSpeed > 1 then noiseLevel = 0.1 end ClientState.noiseLevel = noiseLevel local now = tick() if now - lastNoiseReport >= 1.0 and noiseLevel > 0.05 then lastNoiseReport = now if PlayerNoiseRemote then PlayerNoiseRemote:FireServer(noiseLevel) end end if rootPart then local pos = rootPart.Position if lastPosition then local dist = (pos - lastPosition).Magnitude if dist > 5 then lastPosition = pos local roomGuess = "unknown" if pos.Y < 5 then roomGuess = "ground_floor" elseif pos.Y < 15 then roomGuess = "control_room" else roomGuess = "upper_floor" end if roomGuess ~= ClientState.currentRoom then ClientState.currentRoom = roomGuess if PlayerRoomChange then PlayerRoomChange:FireServer(roomGuess) end end end else lastPosition = pos end end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INITIAL SYNC ------------------------------------------------------------ task.spawn(function() task.wait(3.0) if GetNightData then local success, data = pcall(function() return GetNightData:InvokeServer() end) if success and data then ClientState.nightActive = data.active ClientState.currentNight = data.currentNight or 1 ClientState.elapsedTime = data.elapsedTime or 0 ClientState.totalDuration = data.totalDuration or 720 ClientState.nightProgress = data.progress or 0 ClientState.currentPhase = data.phase or "INACTIVE" ClientState.threatLevel = data.threatLevel or 0 ClientState.powerOn = data.powerOn ClientState.generatorFuel = data.generatorFuel or 100 ClientState.sanity = data.playerSanity or 100 ClientState.paranoia = data.playerParanoia or 0 ClientState.doubt = data.playerDoubt or 0 ClientState.entityActive = data.entityActive or false if ClientState.nightActive then if not AmbientSound.IsPlaying then AmbientSound.Volume = ClientState.ambientVolume AmbientSound:Play() end if not WindSound.IsPlaying then WindSound.Volume = ClientState.windVolume WindSound:Play() end if not CreepyAmbient.IsPlaying then CreepyAmbient.Volume = ClientState.creepyVolume CreepyAmbient:Play() end if not HeartbeatSound.IsPlaying then HeartbeatSound.Volume = 0 HeartbeatSound:Play() end CollectWorkspaceLights() end print("[NightCycleClient] Synced with server. Night: " .. tostring(data.currentNight) .. " Phase: " .. tostring(data.phase)) end end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CLEANUP ON CHARACTER RESPAWN ------------------------------------------------------------ LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character) for id, _ in pairs(CameraEffectCoroutines) do CameraEffectCoroutines[id] = nil end ClientState.cameraShakeOffset = CFrame.new() ClientState.baseCameraShake = 0 ClientState.isDead = false ClientState.playerAlive = true lastPosition = nil character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10) character:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10) if DeathBlur then DeathBlur.Size = 0 DeathBlur.Enabled = false end end) print("[NightCycleClient] Night Cycle Client Handler initialized") ``` user: Вроде бы все впорядке, можешь делать далее ai: # Система первого лица и передвижения игрока (First Person & Movement System) **Тип скрипта:** LocalScript **Размещение:** StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → FirstPersonMovementSystem ```lua --[[ FIRST PERSON & MOVEMENT SYSTEM — Production LocalScript Полная система первого лица: камера, инерция, ограничения, боб-эффект, передвижение, бег, усталость, шаги по поверхностям, шум, Head Bob, дыхание, влияние психологии на управление, взаимодействие с объектами.
