------------------------------------------------------------ -- UTILITY ------------------------------------------------------------ local function Lerp(a, b, t) return a + (b - a) * t end local function LerpAngle(a, b, t) local diff = (b - a) while diff > 180 do diff = diff - 360 end while diff < -180 do diff = diff + 360 end return a + diff * t end local function SmoothDamp(current, target, velocity, smoothTime, dt) local omega = 2.0 / math.max(smoothTime, 0.0001) local x = omega * dt local exp = 1.0 / (1.0 + x + 0.48 * x * x + 0.235 * x * x * x) local change = current - target local temp = (velocity + omega * change) * dt velocity = (velocity - omega * temp) * exp local output = target + (change + temp) * exp return output, velocity end local function ClampAngle(angle, min, max) return math.clamp(angle, min, max) end local function GetFloorMaterial(rootPart) if not rootPart then return Enum.Material.Concrete, nil end local rayOrigin = rootPart.Position local rayDirection = Vector3.new(0, -4, 0) local rayParams = RaycastParams.new() rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {rootPart.Parent} local result = workspace:Raycast(rayOrigin, rayDirection, rayParams) if result then return result.Material, result.Instance end return Enum.Material.Concrete, nil end local function GetSurfaceProfile(material) return Config.SURFACE_PROFILES[material] or Config.DEFAULT_SURFACE_PROFILE end local function IsGrounded(rootPart) if not rootPart then return false, Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end local rayOrigin = rootPart.Position local rayDirection = Vector3.new(0, -3.5, 0) local rayParams = RaycastParams.new() rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {rootPart.Parent} local result = workspace:Raycast(rayOrigin, rayDirection, rayParams) if result then return true, result.Normal end return false, Vector3.new(0, 1, 0) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CHARACTER SETUP ------------------------------------------------------------ local function SetupCharacter(character) State.character = character State.humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10) State.rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10) State.head = character:WaitForChild("Head", 10) if not State.humanoid or not State.rootPart or not State.head then warn("[FirstPersonMovement] Failed to find character components!") return end -- Первое лицо Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable Camera.FieldOfView = Config.CAMERA_FOV_NORMAL -- Скрываем тело в первом лице for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do if part:IsA("BasePart") then part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 elseif part:IsA("Accessory") then local handle = part:FindFirstChild("Handle") if handle then handle.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 end end end -- Подключение скрытия тела при изменении character.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(desc) if desc:IsA("BasePart") then desc.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 end end) -- Настройка Humanoid State.humanoid.WalkSpeed = Config.WALK_SPEED State.humanoid.JumpPower = 0 State.humanoid.AutoRotate = false -- Инициализация камеры if State.rootPart then local pos = State.rootPart.Position + Config.CAMERA_HEIGHT_OFFSET local lookDir = State.rootPart.CFrame.LookVector State.cameraYaw = math.deg(math.atan2(-lookDir.X, -lookDir.Z)) State.cameraPitch = 0 State.targetYaw = State.cameraYaw State.targetPitch = 0 Camera.CFrame = CFrame.new(pos, pos + lookDir) end -- Сброс состояния State.stamina = Config.STAMINA_MAX State.isExhausted = false State.isSprinting = false State.isCrouching = false State.currentSpeed = 0 State.bobTime = 0 State.breathTime = 0 State.footstepTimer = 0 State.landingImpact = 0 State.currentFOV = Config.CAMERA_FOV_NORMAL State.targetFOV = Config.CAMERA_FOV_NORMAL State.currentHeightOffset = Config.CAMERA_HEIGHT_OFFSET State.targetHeightOffset = Config.CAMERA_HEIGHT_OFFSET State.interacting = false State.interactProgress = 0 State.motionBlurAmount = 0 State.leanAmount = 0 State.cameraLocked = false -- Запуск дыхания if not BreathIdleSound.IsPlaying then BreathIdleSound.Volume = 0.02 BreathIdleSound:Play() end State.initialized = true print("[FirstPersonMovement] Character setup complete") end local function CleanupCharacter() State.initialized = false State.character = nil State.humanoid = nil State.rootPart = nil State.head = nil BreathIdleSound:Stop() BreathHeavySound:Stop() BreathAnxiousSound:Stop() if MotionBlurEffect then MotionBlurEffect.Size = 0 MotionBlurEffect.Enabled = false end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INPUT HANDLING ------------------------------------------------------------ UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed) if gameProcessed then return end if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W then State.inputW = true elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A then State.inputA = true elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then State.inputS = true elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D then State.inputD = true elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then State.inputSprint = true elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftControl or input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.C then State.inputCrouch = not State.inputCrouch elseif input.KeyCode == Config.INTERACT_KEY then State.inputInteract = true State.inputInteractHeld = true State.interactHoldStartTime = tick() end end) UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed) if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W then State.inputW = false elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A then State.inputA = false elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then State.inputS = false elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D then State.inputD = false elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then State.inputSprint = false elseif input.KeyCode == Config.INTERACT_KEY then State.inputInteract = false State.inputInteractHeld = false State.interactProgress = 0 State.interacting = false end end) -- Блокировка мыши UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = false ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CAMERA SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateCameraInput(dt) if State.cameraLocked or not State.cameraEnabled then return end local mouseDelta = UserInputService:GetMouseDelta() -- Чувствительность local sensX = Config.CAMERA_SENSITIVITY_X local sensY = Config.CAMERA_SENSITIVITY_Y -- Тревога снижает точность управления камерой if State.anxiety > 30 then local anxietyFactor = math.clamp((State.anxiety - 30) / 70, 0, 1) local jitter = anxietyFactor * Config.ANXIETY_INPUT_JITTER mouseDelta = Vector2.new( mouseDelta.X + (math.random() - 0.5) * jitter * 100, mouseDelta.Y + (math.random() - 0.5) * jitter * 100 ) -- Микродрифт мыши при высокой тревоге local driftAmount = anxietyFactor * Config.ANXIETY_MOUSE_DRIFT * dt State.targetYaw = State.targetYaw + (math.random() - 0.5) * driftAmount State.targetPitch = State.targetPitch + (math.random() - 0.5) * driftAmount * 0.5 end State.targetYaw = State.targetYaw - mouseDelta.X * sensX State.targetPitch = ClampAngle( State.targetPitch - mouseDelta.Y * sensY, Config.CAMERA_VERTICAL_MIN, Config.CAMERA_VERTICAL_MAX ) -- Инерция local inertiaX = Config.CAMERA_INERTIA_HORIZONTAL local inertiaY = Config.CAMERA_INERTIA_VERTICAL State.cameraYaw = Lerp(State.cameraYaw, State.targetYaw, 1.0 - math.exp(-dt / math.max(inertiaX, 0.001))) State.cameraPitch = Lerp(State.cameraPitch, State.targetPitch, 1.0 - math.exp(-dt / math.max(inertiaY, 0.001))) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MOVEMENT SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateMovement(dt) if not State.humanoid or not State.rootPart then return end if not State.movementEnabled then State.humanoid:Move(Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), false) State.isMoving = false return end -- Направление движения в пространстве камеры local moveX = 0 local moveZ = 0 if State.inputW then moveZ = moveZ - 1 end if State.inputS then moveZ = moveZ + 1 end if State.inputA then moveX = moveX - 1 end if State.inputD then moveX = moveX + 1 end local rawInput = Vector3.new(moveX, 0, moveZ) local isMovingInput = rawInput.Magnitude > 0.01 if isMovingInput then rawInput = rawInput.Unit end -- Преобразование в мировые координаты через направление камеры local yawRad = math.rad(State.cameraYaw) local cameraCFrame = CFrame.Angles(0, yawRad, 0) local worldDirection = cameraCFrame:VectorToWorldSpace(rawInput) worldDirection = Vector3.new(worldDirection.X, 0, worldDirection.Z) if worldDirection.Magnitude > 0.01 then worldDirection = worldDirection.Unit end State.isMoving = isMovingInput -- Спринт local canSprint = State.inputSprint and isMovingInput and not State.isCrouching and State.stamina > Config.STAMINA_SPRINT_THRESHOLD and not State.isExhausted State.isSprinting = canSprint -- Скорость if State.isCrouching then State.maxSpeed = Config.CROUCH_SPEED State.targetFOV = Config.CAMERA_FOV_CROUCH elseif State.isSprinting then State.maxSpeed = Config.SPRINT_SPEED State.targetFOV = Config.CAMERA_FOV_SPRINT else State.maxSpeed = Config.WALK_SPEED State.targetFOV = Config.CAMERA_FOV_NORMAL end -- Модификаторы скорости local speedMultiplier = 1.0 -- Тревога if State.anxiety > 50 then local anxietyReduction = ((State.anxiety - 50) / 50) * Config.ANXIETY_SPEED_REDUCTION speedMultiplier = speedMultiplier - anxietyReduction end -- Усталость (stamina) if State.stamina < 30 then local fatigueReduction = ((30 - State.stamina) / 30) * Config.FATIGUE_SPEED_REDUCTION speedMultiplier = speedMultiplier - fatigueReduction end -- Санити if State.sanity < 40 then local sanityReduction = ((40 - State.sanity) / 40) * Config.LOW_SANITY_SPEED_REDUCTION speedMultiplier = speedMultiplier - sanityReduction end -- Наклон поверхности if State.isGrounded and State.groundNormal.Y < 0.95 then local slopeAngle = math.acos(State.groundNormal.Y) local slopeFactor = math.clamp(slopeAngle / math.rad(45), 0, 1) speedMultiplier = speedMultiplier - slopeFactor * Config.SLOPE_SPEED_REDUCTION end speedMultiplier = math.clamp(speedMultiplier, 0.3, 1.0) State.maxSpeed = State.maxSpeed * speedMultiplier -- Плавное ускорение/замедление local accel = State.isSprinting and Config.SPRINT_ACCELERATION or Config.ACCELERATION if isMovingInput then State.currentSpeed = Lerp(State.currentSpeed, State.maxSpeed, 1.0 - math.exp(-accel * dt)) else State.currentSpeed = Lerp(State.currentSpeed, 0, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.DECELERATION * dt)) end -- Применение движения if State.currentSpeed > 0.1 and isMovingInput then State.humanoid.WalkSpeed = State.currentSpeed State.humanoid:Move(worldDirection, false) else State.humanoid:Move(Vector3.new(0, 0, 0), false) State.humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0 end -- Поворот персонажа к направлению камеры if State.rootPart then local lookCFrame = CFrame.Angles(0, yawRad, 0) State.rootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(State.rootPart.Position) * lookCFrame end -- Lean (наклон при стрейфе) if isMovingInput then State.targetLean = -moveX * 0.8 else State.targetLean = 0 end State.leanAmount = Lerp(State.leanAmount, State.targetLean, 1.0 - math.exp(-6.0 * dt)) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- STAMINA SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateStamina(dt) if State.isSprinting and State.isMoving then State.stamina = State.stamina - Config.STAMINA_DRAIN_RATE * dt State.staminaDraining = true State.staminaRegenTimer = 0 if State.stamina <= Config.STAMINA_EXHAUSTION_THRESHOLD then State.stamina = 0 State.isExhausted = true State.isSprinting = false if ExhaustionSound then ExhaustionSound.Volume = 0.3 ExhaustionSound:Play() end end else State.staminaDraining = false State.staminaRegenTimer = State.staminaRegenTimer + dt if State.staminaRegenTimer >= Config.STAMINA_REGEN_DELAY then local regenRate = Config.STAMINA_REGEN_RATE if State.isCrouching then regenRate = regenRate * 1.3 end if not State.isMoving then regenRate = regenRate * 1.5 end State.stamina = math.min(State.stamina + regenRate * dt, Config.STAMINA_MAX) if State.isExhausted and State.stamina >= Config.STAMINA_EXHAUSTION_RECOVERY then State.isExhausted = false end end end State.stamina = math.clamp(State.stamina, 0, Config.STAMINA_MAX) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CROUCH SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateCrouch(dt) if State.inputCrouch then State.isCrouching = true State.targetHeightOffset = Config.CROUCH_HEIGHT_OFFSET if State.humanoid then State.humanoid.HipHeight = Lerp( State.humanoid.HipHeight, Config.CROUCH_HIPHEIGHT_CROUCH, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.CROUCH_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt) ) end else State.isCrouching = false State.targetHeightOffset = Config.CAMERA_HEIGHT_OFFSET if State.humanoid then State.humanoid.HipHeight = Lerp( State.humanoid.HipHeight, Config.CROUCH_HIPHEIGHT_NORMAL, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.CROUCH_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt) ) end end State.currentHeightOffset = Vector3.new( Lerp(State.currentHeightOffset.X, State.targetHeightOffset.X, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.CROUCH_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt)), Lerp(State.currentHeightOffset.Y, State.targetHeightOffset.Y, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.CROUCH_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt)), Lerp(State.currentHeightOffset.Z, State.targetHeightOffset.Z, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.CROUCH_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt)) ) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- HEAD BOB SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateHeadBob(dt) local targetFreq, targetAmpX, targetAmpY if State.isMoving and State.currentSpeed > 0.5 then if State.isSprinting then targetFreq = Config.BOB_SPRINT_FREQUENCY targetAmpX = Config.BOB_SPRINT_AMPLITUDE_X targetAmpY = Config.BOB_SPRINT_AMPLITUDE_Y elseif State.isCrouching then targetFreq = Config.BOB_CROUCH_FREQUENCY targetAmpX = Config.BOB_CROUCH_AMPLITUDE_X targetAmpY = Config.BOB_CROUCH_AMPLITUDE_Y else targetFreq = Config.BOB_WALK_FREQUENCY targetAmpX = Config.BOB_WALK_AMPLITUDE_X targetAmpY = Config.BOB_WALK_AMPLITUDE_Y end -- Масштабирование по скорости local speedRatio = math.clamp(State.currentSpeed / Config.SPRINT_SPEED, 0, 1) targetAmpX = targetAmpX * (0.5 + speedRatio * 0.5) targetAmpY = targetAmpY * (0.5 + speedRatio * 0.5) else targetFreq = Config.BOB_IDLE_FREQUENCY targetAmpX = Config.BOB_IDLE_AMPLITUDE_X targetAmpY = Config.BOB_IDLE_AMPLITUDE_Y end -- Тревога усиливает боб if State.anxiety > 40 then local anxietyFactor = math.clamp((State.anxiety - 40) / 60, 0, 1) targetAmpX = targetAmpX * (1.0 + anxietyFactor * 0.4) targetAmpY = targetAmpY * (1.0 + anxietyFactor * 0.3) end -- Плавный переход параметров local smoothing = Config.BOB_SMOOTHING State.currentBobFrequency = Lerp(State.currentBobFrequency, targetFreq, 1.0 - math.exp(-smoothing * dt)) State.currentBobAmplitudeX = Lerp(State.currentBobAmplitudeX, targetAmpX, 1.0 - math.exp(-smoothing * dt)) State.currentBobAmplitudeY = Lerp(State.currentBobAmplitudeY, targetAmpY, 1.0 - math.exp(-smoothing * dt)) State.bobTime = State.bobTime + dt * State.currentBobFrequency State.bobOffsetX = math.sin(State.bobTime * math.pi) * State.currentBobAmplitudeX State.bobOffsetY = -math.abs(math.sin(State.bobTime * math.pi)) * State.currentBobAmplitudeY -- Наклон головы при ходьбе State.bobTilt = math.sin(State.bobTime * math.pi) * Config.BOB_TILT_AMOUNT * State.currentBobAmplitudeX * 50 end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- BREATHING SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateBreathing(dt) -- Определяем целевой режим дыхания if State.isExhausted or (State.stamina < 20 and State.staminaDraining) then State.targetBreathFrequency = Config.BREATH_HEAVY_FREQUENCY State.targetBreathAmplitude = Config.BREATH_HEAVY_AMPLITUDE elseif State.anxiety > 50 or State.fear > 50 then State.targetBreathFrequency = Config.BREATH_ANXIETY_FREQUENCY State.targetBreathAmplitude = Config.BREATH_ANXIETY_AMPLITUDE else State.targetBreathFrequency = Config.BREATH_IDLE_FREQUENCY State.targetBreathAmplitude = Config.BREATH_IDLE_AMPLITUDE end local transitionSpeed = Config.BREATH_TRANSITION_SPEED State.currentBreathFrequency = Lerp(State.currentBreathFrequency, State.targetBreathFrequency, 1.0 - math.exp(-transitionSpeed * dt)) State.currentBreathAmplitude = Lerp(State.currentBreathAmplitude, State.targetBreathAmplitude, 1.0 - math.exp(-transitionSpeed * dt)) State.breathTime = State.breathTime + dt * State.currentBreathFrequency State.breathOffset = math.sin(State.breathTime * math.pi * 2) * State.currentBreathAmplitude -- Звуки дыхания local heavyBreathTarget = 0 local anxiousBreathTarget = 0 local idleBreathTarget = 0.02 if State.isExhausted or State.stamina < 20 then heavyBreathTarget = 0.25 idleBreathTarget = 0.0 elseif State.anxiety > 50 or State.fear > 50 then anxiousBreathTarget = math.clamp((math.max(State.anxiety, State.fear) - 50) / 50, 0, 1) * 0.15 idleBreathTarget = 0.01 end if not BreathIdleSound.IsPlaying then BreathIdleSound:Play() end local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine) TweenService:Create(BreathIdleSound, tweenInfo, {Volume = idleBreathTarget}):Play() if heavyBreathTarget > 0.01 then if not BreathHeavySound.IsPlaying then BreathHeavySound:Play() end TweenService:Create(BreathHeavySound, tweenInfo, {Volume = heavyBreathTarget}):Play() else TweenService:Create(BreathHeavySound, tweenInfo, {Volume = 0}):Play() end if anxiousBreathTarget > 0.01 then if not BreathAnxiousSound.IsPlaying then BreathAnxiousSound:Play() end TweenService:Create(BreathAnxiousSound, tweenInfo, {Volume = anxiousBreathTarget}):Play() else TweenService:Create(BreathAnxiousSound, tweenInfo, {Volume = 0}):Play() end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ANXIETY SWAY ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateAnxietySway(dt) if State.anxiety < 15 and State.paranoia < 15 then State.anxietySwayX = Lerp(State.anxietySwayX, 0, 1.0 - math.exp(-4.0 * dt)) State.anxietySwayY = Lerp(State.anxietySwayY, 0, 1.0 - math.exp(-4.0 * dt)) return end local anxietyFactor = math.clamp(math.max(State.anxiety, State.paranoia) / 100, 0, 1) State.anxietySwayTime = State.anxietySwayTime + dt local freq = Config.ANXIETY_SWAY_FREQUENCY * (1.0 + anxietyFactor * 0.5) local amp = Config.ANXIETY_SWAY_AMPLITUDE * anxietyFactor State.anxietySwayX = math.sin(State.anxietySwayTime * freq * 1.3) * amp + math.sin(State.anxietySwayTime * freq * 0.7) * amp * 0.5 State.anxietySwayY = math.cos(State.anxietySwayTime * freq * 1.1) * amp * 0.7 + math.cos(State.anxietySwayTime * freq * 0.5) * amp * 0.3 end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- FOOTSTEP SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function PlayFootstep() local profile = State.currentSurfaceProfile local soundSetName = profile.soundSet or "concrete" local soundSet = FootstepSoundSets[soundSetName] if not soundSet or #soundSet == 0 then soundSet = FootstepSoundSets["concrete"] end if not soundSet or #soundSet == 0 then return end -- Чередование L/R local startIndex if State.lastFootSide == "left" then startIndex = 3 State.lastFootSide = "right" else startIndex = 1 State.lastFootSide = "left" end local soundIndex = startIndex + math.random(0, 1) soundIndex = math.clamp(soundIndex, 1, #soundSet) local sound = soundSet[soundIndex] if not sound then return end -- Громкость local baseVolume if State.isSprinting then baseVolume = Config.FOOTSTEP_VOLUME_SPRINT elseif State.isCrouching then baseVolume = Config.FOOTSTEP_VOLUME_CROUCH else baseVolume = Config.FOOTSTEP_VOLUME_WALK end baseVolume = baseVolume * profile.volume -- Высота local basePitch = profile.pitch local pitchVariance = Config.FOOTSTEP_PITCH_VARIANCE local finalPitch = basePitch + (math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * pitchVariance sound.Volume = baseVolume sound.PlaybackSpeed = finalPitch sound:Play() -- Маленький импакт камеры при шаге State.stepLandBob = -0.003 * baseVolume * 2 end local function UpdateFootsteps(dt) if not State.isMoving or State.currentSpeed < 0.5 or not State.isGrounded then State.footstepTimer = 0 return end -- Интервал шагов local interval if State.isSprinting then interval = Config.FOOTSTEP_SPRINT_INTERVAL elseif State.isCrouching then interval = Config.FOOTSTEP_CROUCH_INTERVAL else interval = Config.FOOTSTEP_WALK_INTERVAL end -- Скорость шагов пропорциональна скорости local speedRatio = math.clamp(State.currentSpeed / Config.SPRINT_SPEED, 0.3, 1.5) interval = interval / speedRatio State.footstepTimer = State.footstepTimer + dt if State.footstepTimer >= interval then State.footstepTimer = State.footstepTimer - interval PlayFootstep() end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SURFACE DETECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateSurfaceDetection() if not State.rootPart then return end local grounded, normal = IsGrounded(State.rootPart) State.isGrounded = grounded State.groundNormal = normal if grounded then local material, floorPart = GetFloorMaterial(State.rootPart) if material ~= State.currentSurfaceMaterial then State.currentSurfaceMaterial = material State.currentSurfaceProfile = GetSurfaceProfile(material) end State.floorPart = floorPart end -- Landing impact if grounded and not State.wasGrounded then -- Приземление local fallDistance = State.fallStartY - State.rootPart.Position.Y if fallDistance > 2 then local impactStrength = math.clamp((fallDistance - 2) / 10, 0, 1) State.landingImpact = -impactStrength * 0.08 PlayFootstep() end elseif not grounded and State.wasGrounded then State.fallStartY = State.rootPart.Position.Y end State.wasGrounded = grounded end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- NOISE SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateNoiseLevel(dt) local noise if State.isSprinting and State.isMoving then noise = Config.NOISE_SPRINT elseif State.isCrouching and State.isMoving then noise = Config.NOISE_CROUCH elseif State.isMoving then noise = Config.NOISE_WALK else noise = Config.NOISE_IDLE end -- Модификатор поверхности if State.currentSurfaceProfile then noise = noise * State.currentSurfaceProfile.noiseMultiplier end State.currentNoiseLevel = noise -- Отправка на сервер local now = tick() if now - State.lastNoiseReport >= Config.NOISE_REPORT_INTERVAL and noise > 0.01 then State.lastNoiseReport = now if PlayerNoiseRemote then PlayerNoiseRemote:FireServer(noise) end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MOTION BLUR ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateMotionBlur(dt) if not MotionBlurEffect then return end local targetBlur = 0 if State.isSprinting and State.currentSpeed > Config.MOTION_BLUR_SPRINT_THRESHOLD then local speedOver = State.currentSpeed - Config.MOTION_BLUR_SPRINT_THRESHOLD local maxSpeedOver = Config.SPRINT_SPEED - Config.MOTION_BLUR_SPRINT_THRESHOLD if maxSpeedOver > 0 then targetBlur = (speedOver / maxSpeedOver) * Config.MOTION_BLUR_MAX_SIZE end end State.motionBlurAmount = Lerp(State.motionBlurAmount, targetBlur, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.MOTION_BLUR_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt)) if State.motionBlurAmount > 0.1 then MotionBlurEffect.Enabled = true MotionBlurEffect.Size = State.motionBlurAmount else MotionBlurEffect.Enabled = false MotionBlurEffect.Size = 0 end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- FOV ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateFOV(dt) State.currentFOV = Lerp(State.currentFOV, State.targetFOV, 1.0 - math.exp(-Config.CAMERA_FOV_TRANSITION_SPEED * dt)) Camera.FieldOfView = State.currentFOV end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INTERACTION SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GetLookedAtObject() if not State.rootPart then return nil, 0 end local camCF = Camera.CFrame local origin = camCF.Position local direction = camCF.LookVector * Config.INTERACT_DISTANCE local rayParams = RaycastParams.new() rayParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude rayParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {State.character} local result = workspace:Raycast(origin, direction, rayParams) if result and result.Instance then local target = result.Instance -- Ищем интерактивный объект (по тегу или атрибуту) local interactable = nil local current = target for _ = 1, 5 do if current:GetAttribute("Interactable") then interactable = current break end if current:FindFirstChild("InteractConfig") then interactable = current break end if current.Parent and current.Parent ~= workspace then current = current.Parent else break end end if interactable then -- Проверка угла обзора local toObject = (result.Position - origin).Unit local dotProduct = camCF.LookVector:Dot(toObject) if dotProduct >= Config.INTERACT_DOT_THRESHOLD then return interactable, (result.Position - origin).Magnitude end end end return nil, 0 end local function UpdateInteraction(dt) local lookedAt, distance = GetLookedAtObject() State.lookAtObject = lookedAt State.lookAtDistance = distance if lookedAt then State.interactPromptVisible = true else State.interactPromptVisible = false end -- Удерживание E для взаимодействия if State.inputInteractHeld and lookedAt then State.interacting = true State.interactTarget = lookedAt -- Время взаимодействия с модификатором тревоги local holdTime = Config.INTERACT_HOLD_TIME_BASE if State.anxiety > 40 then local anxietyMult = 1.0 + ((State.anxiety - 40) / 60) * (Config.INTERACT_HOLD_TIME_ANXIETY_MULT - 1.0) holdTime = holdTime * anxietyMult end State.interactHoldTime = holdTime local elapsed = tick() - State.interactHoldStartTime State.interactProgress = math.clamp(elapsed / holdTime, 0, 1) if State.interactProgress >= 1.0 then -- Взаимодействие завершено local objectName = lookedAt.Name local interactType = lookedAt:GetAttribute("InteractType") or "USE" -- Отправляем на сервер local InteractRemote = RemotesFolder:FindFirstChild("ObjectInteract") if InteractRemote then InteractRemote:FireServer(objectName, interactType, { objectPath = lookedAt:GetFullName(), distance = distance, }) end -- Сброс State.interacting = false State.interactProgress = 0 State.inputInteractHeld = false State.interactHoldStartTime = 0 end else if not State.inputInteractHeld then State.interacting = false State.interactProgress = 0 State.interactTarget = nil end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LANDING IMPACT DECAY ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateLandingImpact(dt) State.landingImpact = Lerp(State.landingImpact, 0, 1.0 - math.exp(-8.0 * dt)) State.stepLandBob = Lerp(State.stepLandBob, 0, 1.0 - math.exp(-12.0 * dt)) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PSYCHOLOGY SYNC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdatePsychologyFromShared() if SharedDataFolder then local threatVal = SharedDataFolder:FindFirstChild("ThreatLevel") if threatVal then State.threatLevel = threatVal.Value State.fear = threatVal.Value * 100 end end end -- Получение данных от PsychologyUpdate remote local PsychologyUpdateRemote = RemotesFolder:FindFirstChild("PsychologyUpdate") if PsychologyUpdateRemote then PsychologyUpdateRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end State.paranoia = data.paranoia or State.paranoia State.anxiety = data.paranoia or State.anxiety State.sanity = data.sanity or State.sanity State.fear = data.fear or State.fear State.threatLevel = data.threatLevel or State.threatLevel end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN CAMERA CONSTRUCTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ConstructCameraFrame(dt) if not State.rootPart then return end -- Базовая позиция камеры local basePosition = State.rootPart.Position + State.currentHeightOffset -- Ориентация local yawRad = math.rad(State.cameraYaw) local pitchRad = math.rad(State.cameraPitch) -- Базовый CFrame local baseCFrame = CFrame.new(basePosition) * CFrame.Angles(0, yawRad, 0) * CFrame.Angles(pitchRad, 0, 0) -- Смещение камеры вперёд (чтобы не находиться внутри головы) baseCFrame = baseCFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, -Config.CAMERA_FORWARD_OFFSET) -- Head Bob local bobOffset = CFrame.new(State.bobOffsetX, State.bobOffsetY + State.stepLandBob, 0) -- Наклон при ходьбе local bobTiltCFrame = CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(State.bobTilt)) -- Дыхание local breathCFrame = CFrame.new(0, State.breathOffset, 0) -- Anxiety Sway local anxietyCFrame = CFrame.new(State.anxietySwayX, State.anxietySwayY, 0) -- Landing Impact local landingCFrame = CFrame.new(0, State.landingImpact, 0) -- Lean local leanCFrame = CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(State.leanAmount * 1.5)) -- Комбинация всех эффектов local finalCFrame = baseCFrame * bobOffset * bobTiltCFrame * breathCFrame * anxietyCFrame * landingCFrame * leanCFrame Camera.CFrame = finalCFrame end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- BODY TRANSPARENCY MAINTENANCE ------------------------------------------------------------ local lastTransparencyUpdate = 0 local function UpdateBodyTransparency() if not State.character then return end local now = tick() if now - lastTransparencyUpdate < 0.2 then return end lastTransparencyUpdate = now for _, part in ipairs(State.character:GetDescendants()) do if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SURFACE CHECK THROTTLE ------------------------------------------------------------ local lastSurfaceCheck = 0 local SURFACE_CHECK_INTERVAL = 0.15 ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN UPDATE LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt) if not State.initialized then return end if not State.rootPart or not State.rootPart.Parent then return end if not State.humanoid or State.humanoid.Health <= 0 then return end State.lastDelta = dt -- Обеспечиваем скриптовую камеру if Camera.CameraType ~= Enum.CameraType.Scriptable then Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable end -- Блокировка мыши if UserInputService.MouseBehavior ~= Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter end -- Input камеры UpdateCameraInput(dt) -- Передвижение UpdateMovement(dt) -- Приседание UpdateCrouch(dt) -- Усталость UpdateStamina(dt) -- Поверхность (throttled) local now = tick() if now - lastSurfaceCheck >= SURFACE_CHECK_INTERVAL then lastSurfaceCheck = now UpdateSurfaceDetection() UpdatePsychologyFromShared() end -- Head Bob UpdateHeadBob(dt) -- Дыхание UpdateBreathing(dt) -- Anxiety Sway UpdateAnxietySway(dt) -- Шаги UpdateFootsteps(dt) -- Шум UpdateNoiseLevel(dt) -- Landing UpdateLandingImpact(dt) -- Motion Blur UpdateMotionBlur(dt) -- FOV UpdateFOV(dt) -- Взаимодействие UpdateInteraction(dt) -- Прозрачность тела UpdateBodyTransparency() -- Финальная камера ConstructCameraFrame(dt) end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CHARACTER CONNECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function OnCharacterAdded(character) -- Ожидаем загрузку character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 15) character:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 15) character:WaitForChild("Head", 15) -- Задержка для полной загрузки task.wait(0.5) SetupCharacter(character) end local function OnCharacterRemoving() CleanupCharacter() end LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(OnCharacterAdded) LocalPlayer.CharacterRemoving:Connect(OnCharacterRemoving) if LocalPlayer.Character then task.spawn(function() OnCharacterAdded(LocalPlayer.Character) end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INTERACT PROMPT GUI (минимальный — UI система расширит) ------------------------------------------------------------ local InteractGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui") InteractGui.Name = "InteractPromptGui" InteractGui.ResetOnSpawn = false InteractGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true InteractGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling InteractGui.Parent = LocalPlayer.PlayerGui local InteractFrame = Instance.new("Frame") InteractFrame.Name = "InteractPrompt" InteractFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 220, 0, 60) InteractFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -110, 0.65, 0) InteractFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 15, 25) InteractFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3 InteractFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0 InteractFrame.Visible = false InteractFrame.Parent = InteractGui local InteractCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") InteractCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 8) InteractCorner.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke") InteractStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(80, 120, 180) InteractStroke.Thickness = 1.5 InteractStroke.Transparency = 0.3 InteractStroke.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel") InteractLabel.Name = "Label" InteractLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0.5, 0) InteractLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 4) InteractLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1 InteractLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium InteractLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 230) InteractLabel.TextSize = 14 InteractLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left InteractLabel.Text = "[E] Взаимодействовать" InteractLabel.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractProgressBg = Instance.new("Frame") InteractProgressBg.Name = "ProgressBg" InteractProgressBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, -20, 0, 6) InteractProgressBg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 1, -14) InteractProgressBg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 50) InteractProgressBg.BorderSizePixel = 0 InteractProgressBg.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractProgressBgCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") InteractProgressBgCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3) InteractProgressBgCorner.Parent = InteractProgressBg local InteractProgressFill = Instance.new("Frame") InteractProgressFill.Name = "Fill" InteractProgressFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0) InteractProgressFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 160, 255) InteractProgressFill.BorderSizePixel = 0 InteractProgressFill.Parent = InteractProgressBg local InteractProgressFillCorner = Instance.new("UICorner") InteractProgressFillCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3) InteractProgressFillCorner.Parent = InteractProgressFill -- Обновление GUI взаимодействия RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function() if State.interactPromptVisible and State.lookAtObject then InteractFrame.Visible = true local objectName = State.lookAtObject:GetAttribute("DisplayName") or State.lookAtObject.Name local interactVerb = State.lookAtObject:GetAttribute("InteractVerb") or "Взаимодействовать" InteractLabel.Text = "[E] " .. interactVerb .. " — " .. objectName if State.interacting and State.interactProgress > 0 then InteractProgressFill.Size = UDim2.new(State.interactProgress, 0, 1, 0) -- Цвет по прогрессу local r = math.floor(80 + State.interactProgress * 100) local g = math.floor(160 - State.interactProgress * 60) local b = math.floor(255 - State.interactProgress * 155) InteractProgressFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(r, g, b) else InteractProgressFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0) end else InteractFrame.Visible = false end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- STAMINA UI (минимальный — UI система расширит) ------------------------------------------------------------ local StaminaGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui") StaminaGui.Name = "StaminaGui" StaminaGui.ResetOnSpawn = false FlashlightPoint.Brightness = 0.15 FlashlightPoint.Range = 8 FlashlightPoint.Color = CFG.FLASH_COLOR FlashlightPoint.Enabled = false FlashlightPoint.Parent = FlashlightPart end local function UpdateFlashlight(dt) if not FlashlightPart then return end if not S.flashOn then FlashlightSpot.Enabled = false FlashlightPoint.Enabled = false return end -- Battery drain S.flashBatt = S.flashBatt - CFG.FLASH_BATTERY_DRAIN * dt S.flashBatt = math.max(S.flashBatt, 0) if S.flashBatt <= CFG.FLASH_BATTERY_DEAD_THRESHOLD then S.flashOn = false FlashlightSpot.Enabled = false FlashlightPoint.Enabled = false return end FlashlightSpot.Enabled = true FlashlightPoint.Enabled = true -- Position local cf = Camera.CFrame FlashlightPart.CFrame = cf * CFrame.new(0.3, -0.15, -0.5) -- Battery effects local battRatio = S.flashBatt / CFG.FLASH_BATTERY_MAX if S.flashBatt <= CFG.FLASH_BATTERY_FLICKER_THRESHOLD then -- Flicker if math.random() < CFG.FLASH_FLICKER_CHANCE * (1 - battRatio) then S.flashFlickering = true FlashlightSpot.Brightness = CFG.FLASH_BRIGHTNESS * (math.random() * 0.3) FlashlightSpot.Color = CFG.FLASH_DIM_COLOR FlashlightSpot.Range = CFG.FLASH_RANGE * 0.6 FlashlightPoint.Brightness = 0.03 if not SndFlashFlicker.IsPlaying then SndFlashFlicker:Play() end else S.flashFlickering = false FlashlightSpot.Brightness = CFG.FLASH_BRIGHTNESS * (0.5 + battRatio * 0.5) FlashlightSpot.Color = CFG.FLASH_DIM_COLOR:Lerp(CFG.FLASH_COLOR, battRatio) FlashlightSpot.Range = CFG.FLASH_RANGE * (0.6 + battRatio * 0.4) FlashlightPoint.Brightness = 0.08 + battRatio * 0.07 end else S.flashFlickering = false FlashlightSpot.Brightness = CFG.FLASH_BRIGHTNESS FlashlightSpot.Color = CFG.FLASH_COLOR FlashlightSpot.Range = CFG.FLASH_RANGE FlashlightPoint.Brightness = 0.15 end end local function ToggleFlashlight() S.flashOn = not S.flashOn if SndFlashClick then SndFlashClick:Play() end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- UTILITY ------------------------------------------------------------ local function Lerp(a, b, t) return a + (b - a) * t end local function ExpDecay(a, b, rate, dt) return Lerp(a, b, 1 - math.exp(-rate * dt)) end local function ClampA(a, mn, mx) return math.clamp(a, mn, mx) end local function GetFloorInfo(root) if not root then return Enum.Material.Concrete, nil, true, Vector3.yAxis end local rp = RaycastParams.new() rp.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude rp.FilterDescendantsInstances = {root.Parent} local r = workspace:Raycast(root.Position, Vector3.new(0, -3.5, 0), rp) if r then return r.Material, r.Instance, true, r.Normal end return Enum.Material.Concrete, nil, false, Vector3.yAxis end local function GetSurf(mat) return CFG.SURFACES[mat] or CFG.SURFACE_DEFAULT end BottomBar.BorderSizePixel = 0 BottomBar.ZIndex = 4 BottomBar.Parent = HudGui Instance.new("UICorner", BottomBar).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10) local bbStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke") bbStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(40, 60, 90) bbStroke.Thickness = 1 bbStroke.Transparency = 0.5 bbStroke.Parent = BottomBar -- Bar creation utility local function MkBar(name, parent, posY, color, labelText) local container = Instance.new("Frame") container.Name = name container.Size = UDim2.new(1, -30, 0, 10) container.Position = UDim2.new(0, 15, 0, posY) container.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 22, 35) container.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3 container.BorderSizePixel = 0 container.Parent = parent Instance.new("UICorner", container).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) local fill = Instance.new("Frame") fill.Name = "Fill" fill.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0) fill.BackgroundColor3 = color fill.BorderSizePixel = 0 fill.Parent = container Instance.new("UICorner", fill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) local label = Instance.new("TextLabel") label.Name = "Label" label.Size = UDim2.new(0, 80, 0, 14) label.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -15) label.BackgroundTransparency = 1 label.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(150, 165, 190) label.TextSize = 10 label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left label.Text = labelText label.Parent = container local valLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel") valLabel.Name = "Value" valLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 40, 0, 14) valLabel.Position = UDim2.new(1, -40, 0, -15) valLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1 valLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold valLabel.TextColor3 = color valLabel.TextSize = 10 valLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Right valLabel.Text = "100%" valLabel.Parent = container return container, fill, valLabel end local staminaCont, staminaFill, staminaVal = MkBar("Stamina", BottomBar, 18, Color3.fromRGB(60, 145, 220), "СТАМИНА") local sanityCont, sanityFill, sanityVal = MkBar("Sanity", BottomBar, 42, Color3.fromRGB(120, 200, 130), "РАССУДОК") local battCont, battFill, battVal = MkBar("Battery", BottomBar, 66, Color3.fromRGB(220, 200, 60), "ФОНАРЬ") -- Flashlight icon local flashIcon = Instance.new("TextLabel") flashIcon.Name = "FlashIcon" flashIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20) flashIcon.Position = UDim2.new(1, -48, 0, 62) flashIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1 flashIcon.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold flashIcon.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220, 200, 60) flashIcon.TextSize = 16 flashIcon.Text = "◉" flashIcon.Parent = BottomBar -- Interact prompt local InteractFrame = Instance.new("Frame") InteractFrame.Name = "InteractPrompt" InteractFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 260, 0, 70) InteractFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -130, 0.62, 0) InteractFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(10, 12, 22) InteractFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.25 InteractFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0 InteractFrame.Visible = false InteractFrame.ZIndex = 5 InteractFrame.Parent = HudGui Instance.new("UICorner", InteractFrame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 10) local ipStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke") ipStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(70, 110, 170) ipStroke.Thickness = 1.5 ipStroke.Transparency = 0.2 ipStroke.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractIcon = Instance.new("TextLabel") InteractIcon.Name = "KeyIcon" InteractIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 32, 0, 32) InteractIcon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 0.5, -16) InteractIcon.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 55, 85) InteractIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3 InteractIcon.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold InteractIcon.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 215, 240) InteractIcon.TextSize = 16 InteractIcon.Text = "E" InteractIcon.ZIndex = 6 InteractIcon.Parent = InteractFrame Instance.new("UICorner", InteractIcon).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6) Instance.new("UIStroke", InteractIcon).Color = Color3.fromRGB(80, 120, 180) local InteractLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel") InteractLabel.Name = "Label" InteractLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0.45, 0) InteractLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 52, 0, 8) InteractLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1 InteractLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamMedium InteractLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 210, 230) InteractLabel.TextSize = 13 InteractLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left InteractLabel.Text = "Взаимодействовать" InteractLabel.ZIndex = 6 InteractLabel.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractSubLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel") InteractSubLabel.Name = "SubLabel" InteractSubLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, -60, 0.3, 0) InteractSubLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 52, 0.45, 2) InteractSubLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1 InteractSubLabel.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham InteractSubLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120, 135, 160) InteractSubLabel.TextSize = 10 InteractSubLabel.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left InteractSubLabel.Text = "Удерживайте" InteractSubLabel.ZIndex = 6 InteractSubLabel.Parent = InteractFrame local InteractProgBg = Instance.new("Frame") InteractProgBg.Name = "ProgBg" InteractProgBg.Size = UDim2.new(1, -24, 0, 5) InteractProgBg.Position = UDim2.new(0, 12, 1, -12) InteractProgBg.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 28, 45) InteractProgBg.BorderSizePixel = 0 InteractProgBg.ZIndex = 6 InteractProgBg.Parent = InteractFrame Instance.new("UICorner", InteractProgBg).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3) local InteractProgFill = Instance.new("Frame") InteractProgFill.Name = "Fill" InteractProgFill.Size = UDim2.new(0, 0, 1, 0) InteractProgFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 160, 255) InteractProgFill.BorderSizePixel = 0 InteractProgFill.ZIndex = 7 InteractProgFill.Parent = InteractProgBg Instance.new("UICorner", InteractProgFill).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 3) -- Status warnings (top center) local WarningLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel") WarningLabel.Name = "StatusWarning" WarningLabel.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0, 24) WarningLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -150, 0, 40) WarningLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1 WarningLabel.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold WarningLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80) WarningLabel.TextSize = 13 WarningLabel.TextTransparency = 1 WarningLabel.Text = "" WarningLabel.ZIndex = 8 WarningLabel.Parent = HudGui -- Zoom indicator local ZoomIndicator = Instance.new("Frame") ZoomIndicator.Name = "ZoomBorder" ZoomIndicator.Size = UDim2.new(1, -40, 1, -40) ZoomIndicator.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 20) ZoomIndicator.BackgroundTransparency = 1 ZoomIndicator.BorderSizePixel = 0 ZoomIndicator.Visible = false ZoomIndicator.ZIndex = 2 ZoomIndicator.Parent = HudGui local zoomStroke = Instance.new("UIStroke") zoomStroke.Color = Color3.fromRGB(60, 90, 140) zoomStroke.Thickness = 1 zoomStroke.Transparency = 0.6 zoomStroke.Parent = ZoomIndicator Instance.new("UICorner", ZoomIndicator).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 6) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INPUT ------------------------------------------------------------ UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp, gp) if gp then return end local kc = inp.KeyCode local ut = inp.UserInputType if kc == Enum.KeyCode.W then S.inW = true elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.A then S.inA = true elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.S then S.inS = true elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.D then S.inD = true elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then S.inSprint = true elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.LeftControl or kc == Enum.KeyCode.C then S.inCrouch = not S.inCrouch elseif kc == CFG.INTERACT_KEY then S.inInteract = true S.inInteractHeld = true S.interactStart = tick() elseif kc == CFG.FLASH_KEY then ToggleFlashlight() elseif kc == CFG.ZOOM_KEY then S.inZoom = true end if ut == CFG.ZOOM_MOUSE then S.inZoom = true end end) UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(inp, gp) local kc = inp.KeyCode local ut = inp.UserInputType if kc == Enum.KeyCode.W then S.inW = false elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.A then S.inA = false elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.S then S.inS = false elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.D then S.inD = false elseif kc == Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then S.inSprint = false elseif kc == CFG.INTERACT_KEY then S.inInteract = false S.inInteractHeld = false S.interactProg = 0 S.interacting = false elseif kc == CFG.ZOOM_KEY then S.inZoom = false end if ut == CFG.ZOOM_MOUSE then S.inZoom = false end end) UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = false ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CHARACTER SETUP WITH VISIBLE BODY ------------------------------------------------------------ local function SetupChar(char) S.char = char S.hum = char:WaitForChild("Humanoid", 10) S.root = char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 10) S.head = char:WaitForChild("Head", 10) if not S.hum or not S.root or not S.head then warn("[FPSystem] Character components missing!") return end Camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable Camera.FieldOfView = CFG.CAM_FOV_NORMAL -- Visible body — hide only Head and face-related S.bodyParts = {} for _, p in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do if p:IsA("BasePart") then if p.Name == "Head" then p.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 elseif p.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then -- do nothing, already invisible else -- Keep body visible p.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 table.insert(S.bodyParts, p) end elseif p:IsA("Accessory") then local handle = p:FindFirstChild("Handle") if handle then -- Hide hair/hat accessories on head local att = handle:FindFirstChildOfClass("Attachment") if att and (att.Name == "HatAttachment" or att.Name == "HairAttachment" or att.Name == "FaceFrontAttachment" or att.Name == "FaceCenterAttachment") then handle.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 else handle.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 table.insert(S.bodyParts, handle) end end elseif p:IsA("Decal") and p.Parent and p.Parent.Name == "Head" then p.Transparency = 1 end end char.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(desc) if desc:IsA("BasePart") then if desc.Name == "Head" then desc.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 end elseif desc:IsA("Decal") and desc.Parent and desc.Parent.Name == "Head" then desc.Transparency = 1 end end) S.hum.WalkSpeed = CFG.WALK_SPEED S.hum.JumpPower = 0 S.hum.AutoRotate = false if S.root then local look = S.root.CFrame.LookVector S.yaw = math.deg(math.atan2(-look.X, -look.Z)) S.pitch = 0 S.tYaw = S.yaw S.tPitch = 0 end -- Reset state S.stam = CFG.STAM_MAX S.exhausted = false S.sprinting = false S.crouching = false S.curSpeed = 0 S.bobCycle = 0 S.breathT = 0 S.stepTimer = 0 S.landImpact = 0 S.fov = CFG.CAM_FOV_NORMAL S.tFov = CFG.CAM_FOV_NORMAL S.heightOff = CFG.CAM_HEIGHT S.tHeightOff = CFG.CAM_HEIGHT S.interacting = false S.interactProg = 0 S.mblur = 0 S.lean = 0 S.camLock = false S.flashBatt = CFG.FLASH_BATTERY_MAX S.flashOn = false S.zooming = false S.zoomAlpha = 0 CreateFlashlight() if not SndBreathIdle.IsPlaying then SndBreathIdle.Volume = 0.02; SndBreathIdle:Play() end if not SndHeartbeat.IsPlaying then SndHeartbeat.Volume = 0; SndHeartbeat:Play() end S.initialized = true print("[FPSystem] Character setup complete (visible body)") end local function CleanupChar() S.initialized = false S.char = nil S.hum = nil S.root = nil S.head = nil S.bodyParts = {} SndBreathIdle:Stop() SndBreathHeavy:Stop() SndBreathAnxious:Stop() SndHeartbeat:Stop() if FXMotionBlur then FXMotionBlur.Size = 0; FXMotionBlur.Enabled = false end if FXTunnelBlur then FXTunnelBlur.Size = 0; FXTunnelBlur.Enabled = false end if FlashlightSpot then FlashlightSpot.Enabled = false end if FlashlightPoint then FlashlightPoint.Enabled = false end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CAMERA INPUT ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdCamInput(dt) if S.camLock or not S.camOn then return end local md = UserInputService:GetMouseDelta() local sx = CFG.CAM_SENS_X local sy = CFG.CAM_SENS_Y -- Zoom reduces sensitivity if S.zooming then sx = sx * CFG.ZOOM_SENSITIVITY_MULT sy = sy * CFG.ZOOM_SENSITIVITY_MULT end -- Anxiety jitter if S.anxiety > 30 then local af = ClampA((S.anxiety - 30) / 70, 0, 1) local j = af * CFG.ANXIETY_INPUT_JITTER md = Vector2.new(md.X + (math.random()-0.5)*j*100, md.Y + (math.random()-0.5)*j*100) local drift = af * CFG.ANXIETY_MOUSE_DRIFT * dt S.tYaw = S.tYaw + (math.random()-0.5) * drift S.tPitch = S.tPitch + (math.random()-0.5) * drift * 0.5 end S.tYaw = S.tYaw - md.X * sx S.tPitch = ClampA(S.tPitch - md.Y * sy, CFG.CAM_VERT_MIN, CFG.CAM_VERT_MAX) S.yaw = ExpDecay(S.yaw, S.tYaw, 1/CFG.CAM_INERTIA_H, dt) S.pitch = ExpDecay(S.pitch, S.tPitch, 1/CFG.CAM_INERTIA_V, dt) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MOVEMENT ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdMove(dt) if not S.hum or not S.root then return end if not S.moveEnabled then S.hum:Move(Vector3.zero, false) S.moving = false return end local mx, mz = 0, 0 if S.inW then mz = mz - 1 end if S.inS then mz = mz + 1 end if S.inA then mx = mx - 1 end if S.inD then mx = mx + 1 end local raw = Vector3.new(mx, 0, mz) local hasInput = raw.Magnitude > 0.01 if hasInput then raw = raw.Unit end local yr = math.rad(S.yaw) local camCF = CFrame.Angles(0, yr, 0) local worldDir = camCF:VectorToWorldSpace(raw) worldDir = Vector3.new(worldDir.X, 0, worldDir.Z) if worldDir.Magnitude > 0.01 then worldDir = worldDir.Unit end S.moving = hasInput local canSprint = S.inSprint and hasInput and not S.crouching and S.stam > CFG.STAM_SPRINT_MIN and not S.exhausted S.sprinting = canSprint -- Target speed + FOV if S.crouching then S.maxSpd = CFG.CROUCH_SPEED S.tFov = CFG.CAM_FOV_CROUCH elseif S.sprinting then S.maxSpd = CFG.SPRINT_SPEED S.tFov = CFG.CAM_FOV_SPRINT else S.maxSpd = CFG.WALK_SPEED S.tFov = CFG.CAM_FOV_NORMAL end -- Zoom overrides FOV if S.zooming then S.tFov = CFG.CAM_FOV_ZOOM end -- Speed modifiers local mult = 1.0 if S.anxiety > 50 then mult = mult - ((S.anxiety-50)/50) * CFG.ANXIETY_SPEED_RED end if S.stam < 30 then mult = mult - ((30-S.stam)/30) * CFG.FATIGUE_SPEED_RED end if S.sanity < 40 then mult = mult - ((40-S.sanity)/40) * CFG.SANITY_SPEED_RED end if S.grounded and S.groundNorm.Y < 0.95 then local slope = math.acos(S.groundNorm.Y) mult = mult - ClampA(slope/math.rad(45),0,1) * CFG.SLOPE_SPEED_RED end mult = ClampA(mult, 0.25, 1.0) S.maxSpd = S.maxSpd * mult -- Smooth speed local acc = S.sprinting and CFG.SPRINT_ACCEL or CFG.ACCEL if hasInput then S.curSpeed = ExpDecay(S.curSpeed, S.maxSpd, acc, dt) else S.curSpeed = ExpDecay(S.curSpeed, 0, CFG.DECEL, dt) end if S.curSpeed > 0.1 and hasInput then S.hum.WalkSpeed = S.curSpeed S.hum:Move(worldDir, false) else S.hum:Move(Vector3.zero, false) S.hum.WalkSpeed = 0 end if S.root then S.root.CFrame = CFrame.new(S.root.Position) * CFrame.Angles(0, yr, 0) end -- Lean S.tLean = hasInput and (-mx * 0.9) or 0 S.lean = ExpDecay(S.lean, S.tLean, 6, dt) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- STAMINA ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdStamina(dt) if S.sprinting and S.moving then S.stam = S.stam - CFG.STAM_DRAIN * dt S.stamDraining = true S.stamRegenT = 0 if S.stam <= CFG.STAM_EXHAUST_MIN then S.stam = 0; S.exhausted = true; S.sprinting = false SndExhaust.Volume = 0.35; SndExhaust:Play() end else S.stamDraining = false S.stamRegenT = S.stamRegenT + dt if S.stamRegenT >= CFG.STAM_REGEN_DELAY then local rate = CFG.STAM_REGEN if S.crouching then rate = rate * 1.3 end if not S.moving then rate = rate * 1.5 end S.stam = math.min(S.stam + rate * dt, CFG.STAM_MAX) if S.exhausted and S.stam >= CFG.STAM_EXHAUST_RECOVER then S.exhausted = false end end end S.stam = ClampA(S.stam, 0, CFG.STAM_MAX) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CROUCH ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdCrouch(dt) if S.inCrouch then S.crouching = true S.tHeightOff = CFG.CROUCH_HEIGHT if S.hum then S.hum.HipHeight = ExpDecay(S.hum.HipHeight, CFG.CROUCH_HIP_CROUCH, CFG.CROUCH_SPEED_TR, dt) end else S.crouching = false S.tHeightOff = CFG.CAM_HEIGHT if S.hum then S.hum.HipHeight = ExpDecay(S.hum.HipHeight, CFG.CROUCH_HIP_NORMAL, CFG.CROUCH_SPEED_TR, dt) end end S.heightOff = Vector3.new( ExpDecay(S.heightOff.X, S.tHeightOff.X, CFG.CROUCH_SPEED_TR, dt), ExpDecay(S.heightOff.Y, S.tHeightOff.Y, CFG.CROUCH_SPEED_TR, dt), ExpDecay(S.heightOff.Z, S.tHeightOff.Z, CFG.CROUCH_SPEED_TR, dt) ) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- REALISTIC HEAD BOB ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdBob(dt) local tF, tAY, tAX, tAR, tAP, tST if S.moving and S.curSpeed > 0.5 then if S.sprinting then tF = CFG.BOB_SPRINT_FREQ tAY = CFG.BOB_SPRINT_AMP_Y tAX = CFG.BOB_SPRINT_AMP_X tAR = CFG.BOB_SPRINT_AMP_ROLL tAP = CFG.BOB_SPRINT_AMP_PITCH tST = CFG.BOB_SPRINT_FORWARD_TILT elseif S.crouching then tF = CFG.BOB_CROUCH_FREQ tAY = CFG.BOB_CROUCH_AMP_Y tAX = CFG.BOB_CROUCH_AMP_X tAR = CFG.BOB_CROUCH_AMP_ROLL tAP = CFG.BOB_CROUCH_AMP_PITCH tST = 0 else tF = CFG.BOB_WALK_FREQ tAY = CFG.BOB_WALK_AMP_Y tAX = CFG.BOB_WALK_AMP_X tAR = CFG.BOB_WALK_AMP_ROLL tAP = CFG.BOB_WALK_AMP_PITCH tST = 0 end -- Scale by actual speed ratio local ratio = ClampA(S.curSpeed / CFG.SPRINT_SPEED, 0.3, 1.2) tAY = tAY * ratio tAX = tAX * ratio tAR = tAR * ratio tAP = tAP * ratio else tF = CFG.BOB_IDLE_FREQ tAY = CFG.BOB_IDLE_AMP_Y tAX = CFG.BOB_IDLE_AMP_X tAR = CFG.BOB_IDLE_AMP_ROLL tAP = CFG.BOB_IDLE_AMP_PITCH tST = 0 end -- Anxiety amplification if S.anxiety > 35 then local af = ClampA((S.anxiety-35)/65, 0, 1) tAY = tAY * (1 + af * 0.35) tAX = tAX * (1 + af * 0.3) tAR = tAR * (1 + af * 0.25) end local sm = CFG.BOB_SMOOTHING S.cBobFreq = ExpDecay(S.cBobFreq, tF, sm, dt) S.cBobAmpY = ExpDecay(S.cBobAmpY, tAY, sm, dt) S.cBobAmpX = ExpDecay(S.cBobAmpX, tAX, sm, dt) S.cBobAmpRoll = ExpDecay(S.cBobAmpRoll, tAR, sm, dt) S.cBobAmpPitch = ExpDecay(S.cBobAmpPitch, tAP, sm, dt) S.tSprintTilt = tST S.sprintTilt = ExpDecay(S.sprintTilt, S.tSprintTilt, 4, dt) -- Full-cycle step: one full sine = two steps (L+R) S.bobCycle = S.bobCycle + dt * S.cBobFreq * math.pi * 2 -- Realistic vertical: double-bounce per stride (figure-8 pattern) local sinC = math.sin(S.bobCycle) local cosC = math.cos(S.bobCycle) local sin2C = math.sin(S.bobCycle * 2) -- Y: main vertical bounce (abs sine for double-tap feel) S.bobY = -math.abs(sinC) * S.cBobAmpY + sin2C * S.cBobAmpY * 0.15 -- X: lateral sway (single frequency, feels like hip sway) S.bobX = cosC * S.cBobAmpX -- Roll: shoulder roll with walking S.bobRoll = sinC * S.cBobAmpRoll -- Pitch: slight forward nod per step S.bobPitch = -math.abs(sinC) * S.cBobAmpPitch + S.sprintTilt -- Step impact decay S.stepImpact = ExpDecay(S.stepImpact, 0, CFG.BOB_IMPACT_DECAY, dt) S.landImpact = ExpDecay(S.landImpact, 0, 8, dt) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- BREATHING ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdBreath(dt) if S.exhausted or (S.stam < 20 and S.stamDraining) then S.tBreathFreq = CFG.BREATH_HEAVY_FREQ S.tBreathAmp = CFG.BREATH_HEAVY_AMP elseif S.anxiety > 50 or S.fear > 50 then S.tBreathFreq = CFG.BREATH_ANXIETY_FREQ S.tBreathAmp = CFG.BREATH_ANXIETY_AMP else S.tBreathFreq = CFG.BREATH_IDLE_FREQ S.tBreathAmp = CFG.BREATH_IDLE_AMP end S.cBreathFreq = ExpDecay(S.cBreathFreq, S.tBreathFreq, CFG.BREATH_TRANSITION, dt) S.cBreathAmp = ExpDecay(S.cBreathAmp, S.tBreathAmp, CFG.BREATH_TRANSITION, dt) S.breathT = S.breathT + dt * S.cBreathFreq S.breathOff = math.sin(S.breathT * math.pi * 2) * S.cBreathAmp -- Sound volumes local heavyV, anxV, idleV = 0, 0, 0.02 if S.exhausted or S.stam < 20 then heavyV = 0.28; idleV = 0 elseif S.anxiety > 50 or S.fear > 50 then anxV = ClampA((math.max(S.anxiety,S.fear)-50)/50,0,1) * 0.18; idleV = 0.01 end local ti = TweenInfo.new(0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine) TweenService:Create(SndBreathIdle, ti, {Volume=idleV}):Play() if heavyV > 0.01 then if not SndBreathHeavy.IsPlaying then SndBreathHeavy:Play() end TweenService:Create(SndBreathHeavy, ti, {Volume=heavyV}):Play() else TweenService:Create(SndBreathHeavy, ti, {Volume=0}):Play() end if anxV > 0.01 then if not SndBreathAnxious.IsPlaying then SndBreathAnxious:Play() end TweenService:Create(SndBreathAnxious, ti, {Volume=anxV}):Play() else TweenService:Create(SndBreathAnxious, ti, {Volume=0}):Play() end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ANXIETY SWAY ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdSway(dt) if S.anxiety < 15 and S.paranoia < 15 then S.swayX = ExpDecay(S.swayX, 0, 4, dt) S.swayY = ExpDecay(S.swayY, 0, 4, dt) return end local af = ClampA(math.max(S.anxiety,S.paranoia)/100, 0, 1) S.swayT = S.swayT + dt local freq = CFG.ANXIETY_SWAY_FREQ * (1 + af*0.5) local amp = CFG.ANXIETY_SWAY_AMP * af S.swayX = math.sin(S.swayT*freq*1.3)*amp + math.sin(S.swayT*freq*0.7)*amp*0.5 S.swayY = math.cos(S.swayT*freq*1.1)*amp*0.7 + math.cos(S.swayT*freq*0.5)*amp*0.3 end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- FOOTSTEPS (with speed-based pitch) ------------------------------------------------------------ local function PlayStep() local prof = S.surfProf local setName = prof.set or "concrete" local set = StepSets[setName] or StepSets["concrete"] if not set or #set == 0 then return end -- Alternate feet local idx if S.footSide == "left" then idx = math.random(1, 3) S.footSide = "right" else idx = math.random(4, 6) S.footSide = "left" end idx = ClampA(idx, 1, #set) local snd = set[idx] if not snd then return end -- Volume local baseVol if S.sprinting then baseVol = CFG.STEP_VOL_SPRINT elseif S.crouching then baseVol = CFG.STEP_VOL_CROUCH else baseVol = CFG.STEP_VOL_WALK end baseVol = baseVol * prof.vol -- Pitch with speed scaling local basePitch = prof.pitch local variance = (math.random()-0.5)*2*CFG.STEP_PITCH_VAR if CFG.STEP_SPEED_PITCH_SCALE then local speedRatio = ClampA(S.curSpeed / CFG.SPRINT_SPEED, 0.3, 1.3) basePitch = basePitch * (0.85 + speedRatio * 0.25) end if S.sprinting then basePitch = basePitch + CFG.STEP_SPRINT_PITCH_BOOST end if S.crouching then basePitch = basePitch + CFG.STEP_CROUCH_PITCH_DROP end snd.Volume = baseVol snd.PlaybackSpeed = basePitch + variance snd:Play() -- Camera step impact S.stepImpact = -0.006 * baseVol * 3 end local function UpdSteps(dt) if not S.moving or S.curSpeed < 0.5 or not S.grounded then S.stepTimer = 0 return end local interval if S.sprinting then interval = CFG.STEP_SPRINT_INT elseif S.crouching then interval = CFG.STEP_CROUCH_INT else interval = CFG.STEP_WALK_INT end -- Speed-based interval scaling local speedRatio = ClampA(S.curSpeed / CFG.SPRINT_SPEED, 0.3, 1.5) interval = interval / speedRatio S.stepTimer = S.stepTimer + dt if S.stepTimer >= interval then S.stepTimer = S.stepTimer - interval PlayStep() end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SURFACE & GROUND ------------------------------------------------------------ local lastSurfT = 0 local function UpdSurface() if not S.root then return end local now = tick() if now - lastSurfT < 0.12 then return end lastSurfT = now local mat, fp, grnd, norm = GetFloorInfo(S.root) S.grounded = grnd S.groundNorm = norm if grnd then if mat ~= S.surfMat then S.surfMat = mat S.surfProf = GetSurf(mat) end S.floorPart = fp end -- Landing if grnd and not S.wasGrounded then local fall = S.fallStartY - S.root.Position.Y if fall > 2 then local imp = ClampA((fall-2)/10, 0, 1) S.landImpact = -imp * 0.1 PlayStep() end elseif not grnd and S.wasGrounded then S.fallStartY = S.root.Position.Y end S.wasGrounded = grnd end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- NOISE ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdNoise(dt) local n if S.sprinting and S.moving then n = CFG.NOISE_SPRINT elseif S.crouching and S.moving then n = CFG.NOISE_CROUCH elseif S.moving then n = CFG.NOISE_WALK else n = CFG.NOISE_IDLE end if S.surfProf then n = n * S.surfProf.noise end if S.flashOn then n = n + CFG.FLASH_NOISE_ADD end S.noise = n local now = tick() if now - S.lastNoiseT >= CFG.NOISE_INTERVAL and n > 0.01 then S.lastNoiseT = now if PlayerNoiseRemote then PlayerNoiseRemote:FireServer(n) end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ZOOM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdZoom(dt) if S.inZoom and CFG.ZOOM_ENABLED then S.zooming = true S.zoomAlpha = ExpDecay(S.zoomAlpha, 1, 1/CFG.ZOOM_TRANSITION, dt) if S.zoomAlpha > 0.95 and not ZoomIndicator.Visible then ZoomIndicator.Visible = true if SndZoomIn then SndZoomIn:Play() end end else if S.zooming and S.zoomAlpha > 0.5 then if SndZoomOut then SndZoomOut:Play() end end S.zooming = false S.zoomAlpha = ExpDecay(S.zoomAlpha, 0, 1/CFG.ZOOM_TRANSITION, dt) if S.zoomAlpha < 0.05 then ZoomIndicator.Visible = false end end -- Zoom DOF if FXZoomDof then if S.zoomAlpha > 0.01 then FXZoomDof.Enabled = true FXZoomDof.FarIntensity = S.zoomAlpha * 0.3 FXZoomDof.NearIntensity = S.zoomAlpha * 0.15 FXZoomDof.FocusDistance = CFG.ZOOM_DOF_DISTANCE FXZoomDof.InFocusRadius = CFG.ZOOM_DOF_RADIUS else FXZoomDof.Enabled = false end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- VISUAL EFFECTS (Reality distortion, grain, chromatic, etc) ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdVFX(dt) local san = S.sanity local fear = S.fear local para = S.paranoia local anx = S.anxiety -- Film grain (low sanity) if san < CFG.VFX_GRAIN_START_SANITY then local t = ClampA((CFG.VFX_GRAIN_START_SANITY - san) / CFG.VFX_GRAIN_START_SANITY, 0, 1) S.vfxGrain = t * CFG.VFX_GRAIN_MAX_AMOUNT GrainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1 - S.vfxGrain -- Randomize grain color slightly local g = math.random(100, 155) GrainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(g, g, g) else S.vfxGrain = 0 GrainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1 end -- Chromatic aberration (low sanity) if san < CFG.VFX_CHROMATIC_START_SANITY then local t = ClampA((CFG.VFX_CHROMATIC_START_SANITY - san) / CFG.VFX_CHROMATIC_START_SANITY, 0, 1) S.vfxChromatic = t * CFG.VFX_CHROMATIC_MAX FXChromatic.Enabled = true local r = ClampA(255 + S.vfxChromatic * 60, 0, 255) local gv = ClampA(255 - S.vfxChromatic * 30, 0, 255) local b = ClampA(255 - S.vfxChromatic * 45, 0, 255) FXChromatic.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(r, gv, b) FXChromatic.Contrast = S.vfxChromatic * 0.15 FXChromatic.Saturation = -S.vfxChromatic * 0.3 else S.vfxChromatic = 0 FXChromatic.Enabled = false end -- Fear pulse (brightness oscillation) if fear > CFG.VFX_PULSE_START_FEAR then local t = ClampA((fear - CFG.VFX_PULSE_START_FEAR) / (100 - CFG.VFX_PULSE_START_FEAR), 0, 1) S.vfxPulseT = S.vfxPulseT + dt * CFG.VFX_PULSE_FREQ * (1 + t * 0.5) S.vfxPulse = math.sin(S.vfxPulseT * math.pi * 2) * CFG.VFX_PULSE_AMP * t else S.vfxPulse = ExpDecay(S.vfxPulse, 0, 3, dt) end -- Vignette (paranoia) if para > CFG.VFX_VIGNETTE_START_PARANOIA then local t = ClampA((para - CFG.VFX_VIGNETTE_START_PARANOIA) / (100 - CFG.VFX_VIGNETTE_START_PARANOIA), 0, 1) S.vfxVignette = t * CFG.VFX_VIGNETTE_MAX FXVignette.Enabled = true FXVignette.Brightness = -S.vfxVignette FXVignette.Saturation = -t * 0.2 FXVignette.Contrast = t * 0.08 else S.vfxVignette = 0 FXVignette.Enabled = false end -- Vignette overlay transparency local vigAlpha = ClampA(S.vfxVignette / CFG.VFX_VIGNETTE_MAX, 0, 1) vigAlpha = vigAlpha + S.zoomAlpha * CFG.ZOOM_VIGNETTE_AMOUNT VignetteFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 1 - ClampA(vigAlpha * 0.5, 0, 0.6) -- Reality distortion (very low sanity) if san < CFG.VFX_REALITY_DISTORT_SANITY then local t = ClampA((CFG.VFX_REALITY_DISTORT_SANITY - san) / CFG.VFX_REALITY_DISTORT_SANITY, 0, 1) S.vfxRealityT = S.vfxRealityT + dt * CFG.VFX_REALITY_DISTORT_FREQ * (1 + t) local distort = math.sin(S.vfxRealityT * math.pi * 2) * CFG.VFX_REALITY_DISTORT_AMP * t -- Wobble FOV S.vfxReality = distort -- Color shift if FXColor then local baseB = FXColor.Brightness FXColor.Brightness = baseB + distort * 0.5 -- Occasional color flash if math.random() < 0.005 * t then FXColor.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB( math.random(180, 255), math.random(150, 220), 255 ) task.delay(0.15, function() if FXColor then FXColor.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(200, 215, 255) end end) end end -- Random micro-teleport of view (very subtle) if math.random() < 0.003 * t then S.tYaw = S.tYaw + (math.random() - 0.5) * t * 3 S.tPitch = S.tPitch + (math.random() - 0.5) * t * 1.5 end else S.vfxReality = ExpDecay(S.vfxReality, 0, 3, dt) end -- Desaturation (low sanity) if san < CFG.VFX_DESATURATION_SANITY then local t = ClampA((CFG.VFX_DESATURATION_SANITY - san) / CFG.VFX_DESATURATION_SANITY, 0, 1) S.vfxDesat = t * CFG.VFX_DESATURATION_MAX else S.vfxDesat = ExpDecay(S.vfxDesat, 0, 2, dt) end -- Tunnel vision blur (high fear) if fear > CFG.VFX_TUNNEL_VISION_FEAR then local t = ClampA((fear - CFG.VFX_TUNNEL_VISION_FEAR) / (100 - CFG.VFX_TUNNEL_VISION_FEAR), 0, 1) S.vfxTunnel = t * CFG.VFX_TUNNEL_VISION_MAX FXTunnelBlur.Enabled = true FXTunnelBlur.Size = S.vfxTunnel else S.vfxTunnel = ExpDecay(S.vfxTunnel, 0, 4, dt) FXTunnelBlur.Enabled = S.vfxTunnel > 0.5 FXTunnelBlur.Size = S.vfxTunnel end -- Heartbeat pulse effect (visual + sound) if fear > CFG.VFX_HEARTBEAT_PULSE_FEAR then local t = ClampA((fear - CFG.VFX_HEARTBEAT_PULSE_FEAR) / (100 - CFG.VFX_HEARTBEAT_PULSE_FEAR), 0, 1) S.vfxHeartPulseT = S.vfxHeartPulseT + dt * (0.8 + t * 1.2) -- Double-beat pattern local cycle = S.vfxHeartPulseT % 1.0 local beat1 = math.exp(-((cycle - 0.1) * 12)^2) local beat2 = math.exp(-((cycle - 0.25) * 12)^2) S.vfxHeartPulse = (beat1 + beat2 * 0.7) * t * 0.02 -- Sound local hbVol = t * 0.35 if math.abs(SndHeartbeat.Volume - hbVol) > 0.02 then TweenService:Create(SndHeartbeat, TweenInfo.new(0.3), {Volume = hbVol}):Play() end SndHeartbeat.PlaybackSpeed = 0.8 + t * 0.6 else S.vfxHeartPulse = ExpDecay(S.vfxHeartPulse, 0, 5, dt) if SndHeartbeat.Volume > 0.01 then TweenService:Create(SndHeartbeat, TweenInfo.new(1), {Volume = 0}):Play() end end -- Motion blur local tBlur = 0 if S.sprinting and S.curSpeed > CFG.MBLUR_THRESHOLD then local over = S.curSpeed - CFG.MBLUR_THRESHOLD local maxOver = CFG.SPRINT_SPEED - CFG.MBLUR_THRESHOLD if maxOver > 0 then tBlur = (over/maxOver) * CFG.MBLUR_MAX end end S.mblur = ExpDecay(S.mblur, tBlur, CFG.MBLUR_SPEED, dt) if S.mblur > 0.2 then FXMotionBlur.Enabled = true FXMotionBlur.Size = S.mblur else FXMotionBlur.Enabled = false FXMotionBlur.Size = 0 end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INTERACTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GetLookObj() if not S.root then return nil, 0 end local cf = Camera.CFrame local rp = RaycastParams.new() rp.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude rp.FilterDescendantsInstances = {S.char} local r = workspace:Raycast(cf.Position, cf.LookVector * CFG.INTERACT_DIST, rp) if r and r.Instance then local tgt = r.Instance for _ = 1, 5 do if tgt:GetAttribute("Interactable") or tgt:FindFirstChild("InteractConfig") then local dot = cf.LookVector:Dot((r.Position - cf.Position).Unit) if dot >= CFG.INTERACT_DOT then return tgt, (r.Position - cf.Position).Magnitude end end if tgt.Parent and tgt.Parent ~= workspace then tgt = tgt.Parent else break end end end return nil, 0 end local function UpdInteract(dt) local obj, dist = GetLookObj() S.lookObj = obj S.lookDist = dist S.interactPrompt = obj ~= nil if S.inInteractHeld and obj then S.interacting = true S.interactTgt = obj local hold = CFG.INTERACT_HOLD if S.anxiety > 40 then hold = hold * (1 + ((S.anxiety-40)/60) * (CFG.INTERACT_ANXIETY_MULT - 1)) end S.interactHold = hold local elapsed = tick() - S.interactStart S.interactProg = ClampA(elapsed / hold, 0, 1) if S.interactProg >= 1 then local iName = obj.Name local iType = obj:GetAttribute("InteractType") or "USE" local remote = RemotesFolder:FindFirstChild("ObjectInteract") if remote then remote:FireServer(iName, iType, {path=obj:GetFullName(), dist=dist}) end S.interacting = false S.interactProg = 0 S.inInteractHeld = false S.interactStart = 0 end else if not S.inInteractHeld then S.interacting = false S.interactProg = 0 S.interactTgt = nil end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- FOV ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdFOV(dt) local baseFov = S.tFov -- Reality distortion wobble baseFov = baseFov + S.vfxReality * 30 -- Heartbeat pulse baseFov = baseFov + S.vfxHeartPulse * 80 -- Fear pulse baseFov = baseFov + S.vfxPulse * 30 S.fov = ExpDecay(S.fov, baseFov, CFG.CAM_FOV_SPEED, dt) Camera.FieldOfView = S.fov end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- PSYCHOLOGY SYNC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function SyncPsych() if SharedDataFolder then local tv = SharedDataFolder:FindFirstChild("ThreatLevel") if tv then S.threat = tv.Value; S.fear = tv.Value * 100 end end end local PsychRemote = RemotesFolder:FindFirstChild("PsychologyUpdate") if PsychRemote then PsychRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(d) if not d then return end S.paranoia = d.paranoia or S.paranoia S.anxiety = d.paranoia or S.anxiety S.sanity = d.sanity or S.sanity S.fear = d.fear or S.fear S.threat = d.threatLevel or S.threat end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- BODY TRANSPARENCY MAINTENANCE ------------------------------------------------------------ local lastBodyT = 0 local function UpdBody() if not S.char then return end local now = tick() if now - lastBodyT < 0.25 then return end lastBodyT = now for _, p in ipairs(S.char:GetDescendants()) do if p:IsA("BasePart") then if p.Name == "Head" then p.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 elseif p.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then p.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CAMERA CONSTRUCTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function BuildCamera(dt) if not S.root then return end local basePos = S.root.Position + S.heightOff local yr = math.rad(S.yaw) local pr = math.rad(S.pitch) local baseCF = CFrame.new(basePos) * CFrame.Angles(0, yr, 0) * CFrame.Angles(pr, 0, 0) * CFrame.new(0, 0, -CFG.CAM_FORWARD) -- Combine all offsets local bobCF = CFrame.new(S.bobX, S.bobY + S.stepImpact, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(S.bobPitch), 0, math.rad(S.bobRoll)) local breathCF = CFrame.new(0, S.breathOff, 0) local swayCF = CFrame.new(S.swayX, S.swayY, 0) local landCF = CFrame.new(0, S.landImpact, 0) local leanCF = CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(S.lean * 1.8)) -- Heartbeat pulse: subtle zoom in camera offset local heartCF = CFrame.new(0, 0, -S.vfxHeartPulse * 2) -- Sprint forward tilt local tiltCF = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(S.sprintTilt), 0, 0) Camera.CFrame = baseCF * bobCF * breathCF * swayCF * landCF * leanCF * heartCF * tiltCF end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- "%" if sanR > 0.6 then sanityFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(120,200,130) elseif sanR > 0.3 then sanityFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200,180,60) else sanityFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200,60,60) end -- Battery bar local battR = ClampA(S.flashBatt / CFG.FLASH_BATTERY_MAX, 0, 1) battFill.Size = UDim2.new(battR, 0, 1, 0) battVal.Text = math.floor(S.flashBatt) .. "%" if battR > 0.5 then battFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220,200,60) elseif battR > 0.2 then battFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220,140,40) else battFill.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(220,60,40) end flashIcon.Text = S.flashOn and "◉" or "○" flashIcon.TextColor3 = S.flashOn and Color3.fromRGB(255,230,80) or Color3.fromRGB(100,100,120) battCont.Visible = true -- Bottom bar visibility BottomBar.Visible = true -- Interact prompt if S.interactPrompt and S.lookObj then InteractFrame.Visible = true local dn = S.lookObj:GetAttribute("DisplayName") or S.lookObj.Name local verb = S.lookObj:GetAttribute("InteractVerb") or "Взаимодействовать" InteractLabel.Text = verb .. 16 end else InteractFrame.Visible = false end -- Crosshair behavior local crossAlpha = 0.4 if S.zooming then crossAlpha = 0.15 end if S.interactPrompt then CrossFrame.BackgroundColor3 = crossR.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 180, 255) else CrossFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 200, 220) crossT.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 200, 220) crossB.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 200, 220) crossL.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 200, 220) crossR.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(180, 200, 220) end CrossFrame.BackgroundTransparency = crossAlpha crossT.BackgroundTransparency = crossAlpha crossB.BackgroundTransparency = crossAlpha crossL.BackgroundTransparency = crossAlpha crossR.BackgroundTransparency = crossAlpha -- Status warnings local warning = "" local warnColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 80, 80) if S.exhausted then warning = "ИСТОЩЕНИЕ" elseif S.sanity < 20 then warning = "РАССУДОК ТЕРЯЕТСЯ"; warnColor = Color3.fromRGB(200,60,200) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt) if not
