осталось лишь пофиксит некоторые вещи, поправь чтоб не было видно головы, волос и головных акксесуаров, мешает. А также вытяни камеру немного вперед, потому что от первого лица будто в центре головы камера, а не на глазах ai: # Патч камеры и скрытия головы (First Person Fix Patch) **Тип скрипта:** LocalScript **Размещение:** StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → FirstPersonFixPatch ```lua --[[ FIRST PERSON FIX PATCH — Production LocalScript Исправляет: полное скрытие головы/волос/шапок/лицевых аксессуаров, смещение камеры вперёд на уровень глаз (не из центра головы). Работает поверх FirstPersonMovementSystem, перезаписывая нужные параметры. Размещение: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/FirstPersonFixPatch ]] local Players = game:GetService("Players") local RunService = game:GetService("RunService") local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CONFIGURATION ------------------------------------------------------------ -- Смещение камеры вперёд от центра головы (studs) -- Реальные глаза примерно 0.4-0.6 studs впереди центра Head local EYE_FORWARD_OFFSET = 0.55 -- Высота глаз относительно HumanoidRootPart -- Стандартная голова на высоте ~1.5, глаза чуть ниже верха local EYE_HEIGHT_OFFSET = Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0) -- Список названий аттачментов, которые считаются «на голове» local HEAD_ATTACHMENT_NAMES = { ["HatAttachment"] = true, ["HairAttachment"] = true, ["FaceFrontAttachment"] = true, ["FaceCenterAttachment"] = true, ["HeadAttachment"] = true, ["NeckAttachment"] = true, } -- Список названий частей, которые всегда скрываем local ALWAYS_HIDE_PARTS = { ["Head"] = true, } -- Части, которые всегда оставляем видимыми local ALWAYS_SHOW_PARTS = { ["Left Arm"] = true, ["Right Arm"] = true, ["LeftHand"] = true, ["RightHand"] = true, ["LeftLowerArm"] = true, ["RightLowerArm"] = true, ["LeftUpperArm"] = true, ["RightUpperArm"] = true, ["Torso"] = true, ["UpperTorso"] = true, ["LowerTorso"] = true, ["Left Leg"] = true, ["Right Leg"] = true, ["LeftFoot"] = true, ["RightFoot"] = true, ["LeftLowerLeg"] = true, ["RightLowerLeg"] = true, ["LeftUpperLeg"] = true, ["RightUpperLeg"] = true, } ------------------------------------------------------------ -- STATE ------------------------------------------------------------ local currentCharacter = nil local currentHead = nil local currentRoot = nil local hiddenInstances = {} local connections = {} local patchActive = false ------------------------------------------------------------ -- HIDING LOGIC ------------------------------------------------------------ local function IsHeadAccessory(instance) -- Проверяем аксессуар: если Handle прикреплён к голове if not instance:IsA("Accessory") then return false end local handle = instance:FindFirstChild("Handle") if not handle then return true end -- нет хэндла — скрываем на всякий случай -- Проверка через Attachment for _, child in ipairs(handle:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("Attachment") then if HEAD_ATTACHMENT_NAMES[child.Name] then return true end end end -- Проверка через AccessoryType local accType = instance:FindFirstChild("AccessoryType") if accType and accType:IsA("StringValue") then local val = accType.Value:lower() if val == "hat" or val == "hair" or val == "face" or val == "neck" or val == "head" then return true end end -- Проверка через атрибут local at = instance:GetAttribute("AccessoryType") if at then local val = tostring(at):lower() if val == "hat" or val == "hair" or val == "face" or val == "neck" or val == "head" then return true end end -- Проверяем, к чему прикреплён Weld/RigidJoint хэндла for _, child in ipairs(handle:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("Weld") or child:IsA("Motor6D") or child:IsA("RigidConstraint") then if child.Part0 and child.Part0.Name == "Head" then return true end if child.Part1 and child.Part1.Name == "Head" then return true end end end -- Проверяем, находится ли Handle рядом с головой if currentHead and handle then local dist = (handle.Position - currentHead.Position).Magnitude if dist < 2.5 then return true end end return false end local function HideInstance(instance) if not instance then return end if instance:IsA("BasePart") then instance.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 hiddenInstances[instance] = true elseif instance:IsA("Decal") or instance:IsA("Texture") then instance.Transparency = 1 hiddenInstances[instance] = true elseif instance:IsA("SpecialMesh") then -- Скрываем меш головы через масштаб instance.Scale = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0) hiddenInstances[instance] = true end end local function ShowInstance(instance) if not instance then return end if instance:IsA("BasePart") then instance.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 end hiddenInstances[instance] = nil end local function ProcessDescendant(descendant) if not descendant then return end -- BasePart: Head и HumanoidRootPart скрываем if descendant:IsA("BasePart") then if ALWAYS_HIDE_PARTS[descendant.Name] then HideInstance(descendant) -- Скрыть все декали и текстуры на голове for _, child in ipairs(descendant:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("Decal") or child:IsA("Texture") or child:IsA("SpecialMesh") then HideInstance(child) end end return end if descendant.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then -- HumanoidRootPart и так невидим return end -- Остальные части тела — показываем if ALWAYS_SHOW_PARTS[descendant.Name] then descendant.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 return end -- Неизвестная часть — показываем по умолчанию descendant.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 end -- Accessory if descendant:IsA("Accessory") then if IsHeadAccessory(descendant) then -- Скрываем все части аксессуара local handle = descendant:FindFirstChild("Handle") if handle then HideInstance(handle) for _, child in ipairs(handle:GetChildren()) do if child:IsA("SpecialMesh") then HideInstance(child) elseif child:IsA("Decal") or child:IsA("Texture") then HideInstance(child) end end end -- Скрыть все BasePart внутри аксессуара for _, child in ipairs(descendant:GetDescendants()) do if child:IsA("BasePart") then HideInstance(child) end end else -- Не головной аксессуар — показываем local handle = descendant:FindFirstChild("Handle") if handle then handle.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 end end return end -- Decal/Texture на голове if (descendant:IsA("Decal") or descendant:IsA("Texture")) then if descendant.Parent and descendant.Parent.Name == "Head" then HideInstance(descendant) return end end -- SpecialMesh на голове if descendant:IsA("SpecialMesh") then if descendant.Parent and descendant.Parent.Name == "Head" then HideInstance(descendant) return end end -- ShirtGraphic, Shirt, Pants — оставляем -- CharacterMesh — проверяем if descendant:IsA("CharacterMesh") then -- CharacterMesh для головы (BodyPart = Head, значение 0 в Enum) if descendant.BodyPart == Enum.BodyPart.Head then descendant.Parent = nil -- удаляем кастомный меш головы end end end local function ProcessFullCharacter(character) if not character then return end for _, descendant in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do ProcessDescendant(descendant) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CONTINUOUS ENFORCEMENT enforceInterval then return end lastEnforceTime = now if not currentCharacter then return end -- Принудительно поддерживаем скрытие for instance, _ in pairs(hiddenInstances) do if instance and ALWAYS_SHOW_PARTS[part.Name] then if part.LocalTransparencyModifier ~= 0 then part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0 end end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- ApplyCameraOffset() if not currentRoot or not currentHead then return end -- Получаем текущее положение камеры, установленное основным скриптом local currentCF = Camera.CFrame -- Вычисляем, насколько S.flashOn=false; FLSpot.Enabled=false; FLPoint.Enabled=false; return end FLSpot.Enabled=true; FLPoint.Enabled=true FLPart.CFrame = cam.CFrame * CFrame.new(0.3,-0.15,-0.5) local br = S.flashBatt/C.FL_BATT_MAX if S.flashBatt <= C.FL_FLICKER_TH then if math.random() < C.FL_FLICKER_CH*(1-br) then S.flashFlicker=true FLSpot.Brightness=C.FL_BRIGHT*(math.random()*0.3) FLSpot.Color=C.FL_DIM; FLSpot.Range=C.FL_RANGE*0.6; FLPoint.Brightness=0.03 if not SFlashFl.IsPlaying then SFlashFl:Play() end else S.flashFlicker=false FLSpot.Brightness=C.FL_BRIGHT*(0.5+br*0.5) FLSpot.Color=C.FL_DIM:Lerp(C.FL_COLOR,br) FLSpot.Range=C.FL_RANGE*(0.6+br*0.4); FLPoint.Brightness=0.08+br*0.07 end else S.flashFlicker=false FLSpot.Brightness=C.FL_BRIGHT; FLSpot.Color=C.FL_COLOR FLSpot.Range=C.FL_RANGE; FLPoint.Brightness=0.15 end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- HEAD / HAIR / HAT HIDING ------------------------------------------------------------ local function IsHeadAcc(acc) if not acc:IsA("Accessory") then return false end local h = acc:FindFirstChild("Handle") if not h then return true end for _,ch in ipairs(h:GetChildren()) do if ch:IsA("Attachment") and C.HEAD_ATTACH[ch.Name] then return true end if (ch:IsA("Weld") or ch:IsA("Motor6D")) then if (ch.Part0 and ch.Part0.Name=="Head") or (ch.Part1 and ch.Part1.Name=="Head") then return true end end end if S.head and h then if (h.Position - S.head.Position).Magnitude < 2.5 then return true end end return false end local function HidePart(p) if p:IsA("BasePart") then p.LocalTransparencyModifier=1; S.hiddenParts[p]=true elseif p:IsA("Decal") or p:IsA("Texture") then p.Transparency=1; S.hiddenParts[p]=true elseif p:IsA("SpecialMesh") then p.Scale=Vector3.zero; S.hiddenParts[p]=true end end local function ProcessChar(char) if not char then return end for _,d in ipairs(char:GetDescendants()) do if d:IsA("BasePart") and d.Name=="Head" then HidePart(d) for _,ch in ipairs(d:GetChildren()) do if ch:IsA("Decal") or ch:IsA("Texture") or ch:IsA("SpecialMesh") then HidePart(ch) end end elseif d:IsA("Accessory") then if IsHeadAcc(d) then for _,sub in ipairs(d:GetDescendants()) do if sub:IsA("BasePart") or sub:IsA("Decal") or sub:IsA("Texture") or sub:IsA("SpecialMesh") then HidePart(sub) end end end elseif d:IsA("Decal") or d:IsA("Texture") then if d.Parent and d.Parent.Name=="Head" then HidePart(d) end elseif d:IsA("SpecialMesh") then if d.Parent and d.Parent.Name=="Head" then HidePart(d) end elseif d:IsA("CharacterMesh") then if d.BodyPart == Enum.BodyPart.Head then d:Destroy() end end end end local lastEnforceT = 0 local function EnforceHide() local now = tick() if now - lastEnforceT < 0.12 then return end lastEnforceT = now for inst,_ in pairs(S.hiddenParts) do if inst and inst.Parent then if inst:IsA("BasePart") then if inst.LocalTransparencyModifier ~= 1 then inst.LocalTransparencyModifier=1 end elseif inst:IsA("Decal") or inst:IsA("Texture") then if inst.Transparency ~= 1 then inst.Transparency=1 end elseif inst:IsA("SpecialMesh") then if inst.Scale ~= Vector3.zero then inst.Scale=Vector3.zero end end else S.hiddenParts[inst]=nil end end -- Head force hide if S.head and S.head.Parent then S.head.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1 for _,ch in ipairs(S.head:GetChildren()) do if ch:IsA("Decal") or ch:IsA("Texture") then ch.Transparency=1 elseif ch:IsA("SpecialMesh") then ch.Scale=Vector3.zero end end end -- Body visible if S.char then for _,p in ipairs(S.char:GetChildren()) do if p:IsA("BasePart") and p.Name~="Head" and p.Name~="HumanoidRootPart" then if p.LocalTransparencyModifier ~= 0 then p.LocalTransparencyModifier=0 end end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- HUD ------------------------------------------------------------ local HG = Instance.new("ScreenGui"); HG.Name="FPHud"; Instance.new("UICorner",IPFl).CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,3) local WarnLbl=Instance.new("TextLabel"); WarnLbl.Size=UDim2.new(0,300,0,24) WarnLbl.Position=UDim2.new(0.5,-150,0,40); WarnLbl.BackgroundTransparency=1 WarnLbl.Font=Enum.Font.GothamBold; WarnLbl.TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(255,80,80) WarnLbl.TextSize=13; WarnLbl.TextTransparency=1; WarnLbl.Text=""; WarnLbl.ZIndex=8; WarnLbl.Parent=HG local ZoomInd=Instance.new("Frame"); ZoomInd.Size=UDim2.new(1,-40,1,-40) ZoomInd.Position=UDim2.new(0,20,0,20); ZoomInd.BackgroundTransparency=1; ZoomInd.BorderSizePixel=0 ZoomInd.Visible=false; ZoomInd.ZIndex=2; ZoomInd.Parent=HG local zs=Instance.new("UIStroke"); zs.Color=Color3.fromRGB(60,90,140); zs.Thickness=1; zs.Transparency=0.6; zs.Parent=ZoomInd Instance.new("UICorner",ZoomInd).CornerRadius=UDim.new(0,6) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INPUT ------------------------------------------------------------ UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp,gp) if gp then return end local k=inp.KeyCode; local u=inp.UserInputType if k==Enum.KeyCode.W then S.inW=true elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.A then S.inA=true elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.S then S.inS=true elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.D then S.inD=true elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then S.inSprint=true elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.LeftControl or k==Enum.KeyCode.C then S.inCrouch=not S.inCrouch elseif k==C.INT_KEY then S.inInt=true; S.inIntHeld=true; S.intStart=tick() elseif k==C.FL_KEY then S.flashOn=not S.flashOn; SFlashCl:Play() elseif k==C.ZOOM_KEY then S.inZoom=true end if u==C.ZOOM_MOUSE then S.inZoom=true end end) UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(inp) local k=inp.KeyCode; local u=inp.UserInputType if k==Enum.KeyCode.W then S.inW=false elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.A then S.inA=false elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.S then S.inS=false elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.D then S.inD=false elseif k==Enum.KeyCode.LeftShift then S.inSprint=false elseif k==C.INT_KEY then S.inInt=false; S.inIntHeld=false; S.intProg=0; S.interacting=false elseif k==C.ZOOM_KEY then S.inZoom=false end if u==C.ZOOM_MOUSE then S.inZoom=false end end) UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = false ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CHARACTER SETUP ------------------------------------------------------------ local function Setup(char) S.char=char S.hum=char:WaitForChild("Humanoid",10) S.root=char:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart",10) S.head=char:WaitForChild("Head",10) if not S.hum or not S.root or not S.head then warn("[FPS] Missing parts!"); return end workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Scriptable workspace.CurrentCamera.FieldOfView = C.CAM_FOV_NORMAL -- Disconnect old hide connections for _,cn in ipairs(S.hideConns) do if cn.Connected then cn:Disconnect() end end S.hideConns = {} S.hiddenParts = {} -- Initial hide task.wait(0.2) ProcessChar(char) -- Watch for new descendants (late-loading accessories) table.insert(S.hideConns, char.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(d) task.defer(function() if d:IsA("BasePart") and d.Name=="Head" then HidePart(d) for _,ch in ipairs(d:GetChildren()) do if ch:IsA("Decal") or ch:IsA("Texture") or ch:IsA("SpecialMesh") then HidePart(ch) end end elseif d:IsA("Accessory") then task.wait(0.1) if IsHeadAcc(d) then for _,sub in ipairs(d:GetDescendants()) do if sub:IsA("BasePart") or sub:IsA("Decal") or sub:IsA("Texture") or sub:IsA("SpecialMesh") then HidePart(sub) end end end elseif (d:IsA("Decal") or d:IsA("Texture")) and d.Parent and d.Parent.Name=="Head" then HidePart(d) elseif d:IsA("SpecialMesh") and d.Parent and d.Parent.Name=="Head" then HidePart(d) end end) end)) -- Re-process after delay for late accessories task.delay(1, function() if S.char==char then ProcessChar(char) end end) task.delay(3, function() if S.char==char then ProcessChar(char) end end) S.hum.WalkSpeed=C.WALK_SPEED; S.hum.JumpPower=0; S.hum.AutoRotate=false local lk=S.root.CFrame.LookVector S.yaw=math.deg(math.atan2(-lk.X,-lk.Z)); S.pitch=0; S.tYaw=S.yaw; S.tPitch=0 S.stam=C.STAM_MAX; S.exhausted=false; S.sprinting=false; S.crouching=false S.curSpd=0; S.bobCycle=0; S.brT=0; S.stepT=0; S.landImp=0 S.fov=C.CAM_FOV_NORMAL; S.tFov=C.CAM_FOV_NORMAL S.eyeOff=C.EYE_OFFSET; S.tEyeOff=C.EYE_OFFSET S.flashBatt=C.FL_BATT_MAX; S.flashOn=false; S.zooming=false; S.zoomA=0 CreateFL() if not SBreathI.IsPlaying then SBreathI.Volume=0.02; SBreathI:Play() end if not SHeart.IsPlaying then SHeart.Volume=0; SHeart:Play() end S.init=true print("[FPS] Setup done — eye-level camera, head hidden, body visible") end local function Cleanup() S.init=false; S.char=nil; S.hum=nil; S.root=nil; S.head=nil for _,cn in ipairs(S.hideConns) do if cn.Connected then cn:Disconnect() end end S.hideConns={}; S.hiddenParts={} SBreathI:Stop(); SBreathH:Stop(); SBreathA:Stop(); SHeart:Stop() if FXMBlur then FXMBlur.Size=0; FXMBlur.Enabled=false end if FXTunnel then FXTunnel.Size=0; FXTunnel.Enabled=false end if FLSpot then FLSpot.Enabled=false end if FLPoint then FLPoint.Enabled=false end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- UPDATE FUNCTIONS ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UCam(dt) if S.camLock then return end local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera if not cam then return end local md=UserInputService:GetMouseDelta() local sx,sy=C.CAM_SENS_X,C.CAM_SENS_Y if S.zooming then sx=sx*C.ZOOM_SENS_MULT; sy=sy*C.ZOOM_SENS_MULT end if S.anxiety>30 then local af=Cl((S.anxiety-30)/70,0,1) md=Vector2.new(md.X+(math.random()-0.5)*af*C.ANX_JITTER*100, md.Y+(math.random()-0.5)*af*C.ANX_JITTER*100) S.tYaw=S.tYaw+(math.random()-0.5)*af*C.ANX_DRIFT*dt end S.tYaw=S.tYaw-md.X*sx S.tPitch=Cl(S.tPitch-md.Y*sy,C.CAM_VERT_MIN,C.CAM_VERT_MAX) S.yaw=ED(S.yaw,S.tYaw,1/C.CAM_INERTIA_H,dt) S.pitch=ED(S.pitch,S.tPitch,1/C.CAM_INERTIA_V,dt) end local function UMove(dt) if not S.hum or not S.root then return end if not S.moveOn then S.hum:Move(Vector3.zero); S.moving=false; return end local mx,mz=0,0 if S.inW then mz=mz-1 end; if S.inS then mz=mz+1 end if S.inA then mx=mx-1 end; if S.inD then mx=mx+1 end local raw=Vector3.new(mx,0,mz); local has=raw.Magnitude>0.01 if has then raw=raw.Unit end local yr=math.rad(S.yaw) local wd=CFrame.Angles(0,yr,0):VectorToWorldSpace(raw) wd=Vector3.new(wd.X,0,wd.Z); if wd.Magnitude>0.01 then wd=wd.Unit end S.moving=has S.sprinting=S.inSprint and has and not S.crouching and S.stam>C.STAM_SPRINT_MIN and not S.exhausted if S.crouching then S.maxSpd=C.CROUCH_SPEED; S.tFov=C.CAM_FOV_CROUCH elseif S.sprinting then S.maxSpd=C.SPRINT_SPEED; S.tFov=C.CAM_FOV_SPRINT else S.maxSpd=C.WALK_SPEED; S.tFov=C.CAM_FOV_NORMAL end if S.zooming then S.tFov=C.CAM_FOV_ZOOM end local m=1 if S.anxiety>50 then m=m-((S.anxiety-50)/50)*C.ANXIETY_SPD end if S.stam<30 then m=m-((30-S.stam)/30)*C.FATIGUE_SPD end if S.sanity<40 then m=m-((40-S.sanity)/40)*C.SANITY_SPD end if S.grounded and S.gNorm.Y<0.95 then m=m-Cl(math.acos(S.gNorm.Y)/math.rad(45),0,1)*C.SLOPE_SPD end m=Cl(m,0.25,1); S.maxSpd=S.maxSpd*m local ac=S.sprinting and C.SPRINT_ACCEL or C.ACCEL S.curSpd = has and ED(S.curSpd,S.maxSpd,ac,dt) or ED(S.curSpd,0,C.DECEL,dt) if S.curSpd>0.1 and has then S.hum.WalkSpeed=S.curSpd; S.hum:Move(wd) else S.hum:Move(Vector3.zero); S.hum.WalkSpeed=0 end S.root.CFrame=CFrame.new(S.root.Position)*CFrame.Angles(0,yr,0) S.tLean=has and (-mx*0.9) or 0 S.lean=ED(S.lean,S.tLean,6,dt) end local function UStam(dt) if S.sprinting and S.moving then S.stam=S.stam-C.STAM_DRAIN*dt; S.stamDrain=true; S.stamRegenT=0 if S.stam<=C.STAM_EXHAUST_MIN then S.stam=0; S.exhausted=true; S.sprinting=false; SExhaust.Volume=0.35; SExhaust:Play() end else S.stamDrain=false; S.stamRegenT=S.stamRegenT+dt if S.stamRegenT>=C.STAM_REGEN_DELAY then local r=C.STAM_REGEN; if S.crouching then r=r*1.3 end; if not S.moving then r=r*1.5 end S.stam=math.min(S.stam+r*dt,C.STAM_MAX) if S.exhausted and S.stam>=C.STAM_EXHAUST_REC then S.exhausted=false end end end S.stam=Cl(S.stam,0,C.STAM_MAX) end local function UCrouch(dt) if S.inCrouch then S.crouching=true; S.tEyeOff=C.CROUCH_EYE if S.hum then S.hum.HipHeight=ED(S.hum.HipHeight,C.CROUCH_HIP_C,C.CROUCH_TR,dt) end else S.crouching=false; S.tEyeOff=C.EYE_OFFSET if S.hum then S.hum.HipHeight=ED(S.hum.HipHeight,C.CROUCH_HIP_N,C.CROUCH_TR,dt) end end S.eyeOff=Vector3.new(ED(S.eyeOff.X,S.tEyeOff.X,C.CROUCH_TR,dt),ED(S.eyeOff.Y,S.tEyeOff.Y,C.CROUCH_TR,dt),ED(S.eyeOff.Z,S.tEyeOff.Z,C.CROUCH_TR,dt)) end local function UBob(dt) local tF,tY,tX,tR,tP,tST if S.moving and S.curSpd>0.5 then if S.sprinting then tF=C.BOB_SPRINT_FREQ; tY=C.BOB_SPRINT_Y; tX=C.BOB_SPRINT_X; tR=C.BOB_SPRINT_ROLL; tP=C.BOB_SPRINT_PITCH; tST=C.BOB_SPRINT_TILT elseif S.crouching then tF=C.BOB_CROUCH_FREQ; tY=C.BOB_CROUCH_Y; tX=C.BOB_CROUCH_X; tR=C.BOB_CROUCH_ROLL; tP=C.BOB_CROUCH_PITCH; tST=0 else tF=C.BOB_WALK_FREQ; tY=C.BOB_WALK_Y; tX=C.BOB_WALK_X; tR=C.BOB_WALK_ROLL; tP=C.BOB_WALK_PITCH; tST=0 end local r=Cl(S.curSpd/C.SPRINT_SPEED,0.3,1.2); tY=tY*r; tX=tX*r; tR=tR*r; tP=tP*r else tF=C.BOB_IDLE_FREQ; tY=C.BOB_IDLE_Y; tX=C.BOB_IDLE_X; tR=C.BOB_IDLE_ROLL; tP=C.BOB_IDLE_PITCH; tST=0 end if S.anxiety>35 then local af=Cl((S.anxiety-35)/65,0,1); tY=tY*(1+af*0.35); tX=tX*(1+af*0.3); tR=tR*(1+af*0.25) end local sm=C.BOB_SMOOTH S.cF=ED(S.cF,tF,sm,dt); S.cAY=ED(S.cAY,tY,sm,dt); S.cAX=ED(S.cAX,tX,sm,dt) S.cAR=ED(S.cAR,tR,sm,dt); S.cAP=ED(S.cAP,tP,sm,dt) S.tSpTilt=tST; S.spTilt=ED(S.spTilt,S.tSpTilt,4,dt) S.bobCycle=S.bobCycle+dt*S.cF*math.pi*2 local sn=math.sin(S.bobCycle); local cs=math.cos(S.bobCycle); local s2=math.sin(S.bobCycle*2) S.bobY=-math.abs(sn)*S.cAY+s2*S.cAY*0.15 S.bobX=cs*S.cAX S.bobRoll=sn*S.cAR S.bobPitch=-math.abs(sn)*S.cAP+S.spTilt S.stepImp=ED(S.stepImp,0,C.BOB_IMPACT_DECAY,dt) S.landImp=ED(S.landImp,0,8,dt) end local function UBreath(dt) if S.exhausted or (S.stam<20 and S.stamDrain) then S.tBrF=C.BR_HEAVY_F; S.tBrA=C.BR_HEAVY_A elseif S.anxiety>50 or S.fear>50 then S.tBrF=C.BR_ANX_F; S.tBrA=C.BR_ANX_A else S.tBrF=C.BR_IDLE_F; S.tBrA=C.BR_IDLE_A end S.cBrF=ED(S.cBrF,S.tBrF,C.BR_TR,dt); S.cBrA=ED(S.cBrA,S.tBrA,C.BR_TR,dt) S.brT=S.brT+dt*S.cBrF; S.brOff=math.sin(S.brT*math.pi*2)*S.cBrA local hv,av,iv=0,0,0.02 if S.exhausted or S.stam<20 then hv=0.28; iv=0 elseif S.anxiety>50 or S.fear>50 then av=Cl((math.max(S.anxiety,S.fear)-50)/50,0,1)*0.18; iv=0.01 end local ti=TweenInfo.new(0.5,Enum.EasingStyle.Sine) TweenService:Create(SBreathI,ti,{Volume=iv}):Play() if hv>0.01 then if not SBreathH.IsPlaying then SBreathH:Play() end; TweenService:Create(SBreathH,ti,{Volume=hv}):Play() else TweenService:Create(SBreathH,ti,{Volume=0}):Play() end if av>0.01 then if not SBreathA.IsPlaying then SBreathA:Play() end; TweenService:Create(SBreathA,ti,{Volume=av}):Play() else TweenService:Create(SBreathA,ti,{Volume=0}):Play() end end local function USway(dt) if S.anxiety<15 and S.paranoia<15 then S.swayX=ED(S.swayX,0,4,dt); S.swayY=ED(S.swayY,0,4,dt); return end local af=Cl(math.max(S.anxiety,S.paranoia)/100,0,1); S.swayT=S.swayT+dt local f=C.ANX_SWAY_F*(1+af*0.5); local a=C.ANX_SWAY_A*af S.swayX=math.sin(S.swayT*f*1.3)*a+math.sin(S.swayT*f*0.7)*a*0.5 S.swayY=math.cos(S.swayT*f*1.1)*a*0.7+math.cos(S.swayT*f*0.5)*a*0.3 end local function PlayStep() local p=S.surfP; local set=StepSets[p.s or "concrete"] or StepSets["concrete"] if not set or #set==0 then return end local idx; if S.footSide=="left" then idx=math.random(1,3); S.footSide="right" else idx=math.random(4,6); S.footSide="left" end idx=Cl(idx,1,#set); local snd=set[idx]; if not snd then return end local bv; if S.sprinting then bv=C.STEP_VOL_S elseif S.crouching then bv=C.STEP_VOL_C else bv=C.STEP_VOL_W end bv=bv*p.v local bp=p.p+(math.random()-0.5)*2*C.STEP_PITCH_VAR local sr=Cl(S.curSpd/C.SPRINT_SPEED,0.3,1.3); bp=bp*(0.85+sr*0.25) if S.sprinting then bp=bp+C.STEP_SPRINT_PITCH end if S.crouching then bp=bp+C.STEP_CROUCH_PITCH end snd.Volume=bv; snd.PlaybackSpeed=bp; snd:Play() S.stepImp=-0.006*bv*3 end local function USteps(dt) if not S.moving or S.curSpd<0.5 or not S.grounded then S.stepT=0; return end local iv; if S.sprinting then iv=C.STEP_SPRINT_I elseif S.crouching then iv=C.STEP_CROUCH_I else iv=C.STEP_WALK_I end iv=iv/Cl(S.curSpd/C.SPRINT_SPEED,0.3,1.5) S.stepT=S.stepT+dt; if S.stepT>=iv then S.stepT=S.stepT-iv; PlayStep() end end local lastSurfT=0 local function USurf() if not S.root then return end local now=tick(); if now-lastSurfT<0.12 then return end; lastSurfT=now local rp=RaycastParams.new(); rp.FilterType=Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude; rp.FilterDescendantsInstances={S.char} local r=workspace:Raycast(S.root.Position,Vector3.new(0,-3.5,0),rp) if r then S.grounded=true; S.gNorm=r.Normal; if r.Material~=S.surfMat then S.surfMat=r.Material; S.surfP=C.SURF[r.Material] or C.SURF_DEF end else S.grounded=false end if S.grounded and not S.wasGround then local fall=S.fallY-S.root.Position.Y; if fall>2 then S.landImp=-Cl((fall-2)/10,0,1)*0.1; PlayStep() end elseif not S.grounded and S.wasGround then S.fallY=S.root.Position.Y end S.wasGround=S.grounded end local function UNoise(dt) local n; if S.sprinting and S.moving then n=C.NOISE_S elseif S.crouching and S.moving then n=C.NOISE_C elseif S.moving then n=C.NOISE_W else n=C.NOISE_I end if S.surfP then n=n*S.surfP.n end; if S.flashOn then n=n+C.FL_NOISE end; S.noise=n local now=tick(); if now-S.lastNoiseT>=C.NOISE_INT and n>0.01 then S.lastNoiseT=now; if PlayerNoiseRemote then PlayerNoiseRemote:FireServer(n) end end end local function UZoom(dt) if S.inZoom then S.zooming=true; S.zoomA=ED(S.zoomA,1,1/C.ZOOM_TRANSITION,dt) if S.zoomA>0.95 and not ZoomInd.Visible then ZoomInd.Visible=true; SZoomIn:Play() end else if S.zooming and S.zoomA>0.5 then SZoomOut:Play() end S.zooming=false; S.zoomA=ED(S.zoomA,0,1/C.ZOOM_TRANSITION,dt) if S.zoomA<0.05 then ZoomInd.Visible=false end end if FXZDof then if S.zoomA>0.01 then FXZDof.Enabled=true; FXZDof.FarIntensity=S.zoomA*0.3; FXZDof.NearIntensity=S.zoomA*0.15; FXZDof.FocusDistance=50; FXZDof.InFocusRadius=60 else FXZDof.Enabled=false end end end local function UVFX(dt) local san,fear,para=S.sanity,S.fear,S.paranoia if sanC.VFX_PULSE_FEAR then local t=Cl((fear-C.VFX_PULSE_FEAR)/(100-C.VFX_PULSE_FEAR),0,1) S.vPulseT=S.vPulseT+dt*C.VFX_PULSE_F*(1+t*0.5); S.vPulse=math.sin(S.vPulseT*math.pi*2)*C.VFX_PULSE_A*t else S.vPulse=ED(S.vPulse,0,3,dt) end if para>C.VFX_VIG_PARA then local t=Cl((para-C.VFX_VIG_PARA)/(100-C.VFX_VIG_PARA),0,1); S.vVig=t*C.VFX_VIG_MAX FXVig.Enabled=true; FXVig.Brightness=-S.vVig; FXVig.Saturation=-t*0.2; FXVig.Contrast=t*0.08 else S.vVig=0; FXVig.Enabled=false end local vigA=Cl(S.vVig/math.max(C.VFX_VIG_MAX,0.001),0,1)+S.zoomA*C.ZOOM_VIGNETTE VigF.BackgroundTransparency=1-Cl(vigA*0.5,0,0.6) if sanC.VFX_TUNNEL_FEAR then local t=Cl((fear-C.VFX_TUNNEL_FEAR)/(100-C.VFX_TUNNEL_FEAR),0,1) S.vTunnel=t*C.VFX_TUNNEL_MAX; FXTunnel.Enabled=true; FXTunnel.Size=S.vTunnel else S.vTunnel=ED(S.vTunnel,0,4,dt); FXTunnel.Enabled=S.vTunnel>0.5; FXTunnel.Size=S.vTunnel end if fear>C.VFX_HB_FEAR then local t=Cl((fear-C.VFX_HB_FEAR)/(100-C.VFX_HB_FEAR),0,1) S.vHbT=S.vHbT+dt*(0.8+t*1.2); local cy=S.vHbT%1 S.vHb=(math.exp(-((cy-0.1)*12)^2)+math.exp(-((cy-0.25)*12)^2)*0.7)*t*0.02 local hv=t*0.35; if math.abs(SHeart.Volume-hv)>0.02 then TweenService:Create(SHeart,TweenInfo.new(0.3),{Volume=hv}):Play() end SHeart.PlaybackSpeed=0.8+t*0.6 else S.vHb=ED(S.vHb,0,5,dt); if SHeart.Volume>0.01 then TweenService:Create(SHeart,TweenInfo.new(1),{Volume=0}):Play() end end local tb=0; if S.sprinting and S.curSpd>C.MB_TH then local o=S.curSpd-C.MB_TH; local mx=C.SPRINT_SPEED-C.MB_TH; if mx>0 then tb=(o/mx)*C.MB_MAX end end S.mblur=ED(S.mblur,tb,C.MB_SPD,dt); if S.mblur>0.2 then FXMBlur.Enabled=true; FXMBlur.Size=S.mblur else FXMBlur.Enabled=false; FXMBlur.Size=0 end end local function UInt(dt) if not S.root then return end local cam=workspace.CurrentCamera; if not cam then return end local rp=RaycastParams.new(); rp.FilterType=Enum.RaycastFilterType.Exclude; rp.FilterDescendantsInstances={S.char} local r=workspace:Raycast(cam.CFrame.Position,cam.CFrame.LookVector*C.INT_DIST,rp) local obj,dist=nil,0 if r and r.Instance then local tgt=r.Instance for _=1,5 do if tgt:GetAttribute("Interactable") or tgt:FindFirstChild("InteractConfig") then if then S.interacting=false; S.intProg=0; S.intTgt=nil end end end local function SyncPsych() if SharedDataFolder then local tv=SharedDataFolder:FindFirstChild("ThreatLevel"); if tv then S.threat=tv.Value; S.fear=tv.Value*100 end end end local PR=RemotesFolder:FindFirstChild("PsychologyUpdate") if PR then PR.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(d) if not d then return end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- CAMERA BUILD ------------------------------------------------------------ local function BuildCam(dt) if not S.root then return end local cam = workspace.CurrentCamera if not cam then return end -- Eye position: root + eye height offset + forward from head center local basePos = S.root.Position + S.eyeOff local yr = math.rad(S.yaw) local pr = math.rad(S.pitch) -- Build camera CFrame: position at eye level, looking forward with yaw+pitch, -- then shift forward by EYE_FORWARD to be at actual eye position (not center of head) local baseCF = CFrame.new(basePos) * CFrame.Angles(0, yr, 0) * CFrame.Angles(pr, 0, 0) * CFrame.new(0, 0, -C.EYE_FORWARD) -- All additive offsets local bobCF = CFrame.new(S.bobX, S.bobY + S.stepImp, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(S.bobPitch), 0, math.rad(S.bobRoll)) local brCF = CFrame.new(0, S.brOff, 0) local swCF = CFrame.new(0, S.swayX, S.swayY) -- note: X→Y, Y→side for subtle variety local lnCF = CFrame.new(0, S.landImp, 0) local leCF = CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(S.lean * 1.8)) local hbCF = CFrame.new(0, 0, -S.vHb * 2) local tlCF = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(S.spTilt), 0, 0) local rlCF = CFrame.new(0, S.vReal * 0.3, 0) -- FOV with effects local baseFov = S.tFov + S.vReal * 30 + S.vHb * 80 + S.vPulse * 30 S.fov = ED(S.fov, baseFov, C.CAM_FOV_SPEED, dt) cam.FieldOfView = Радио не принимает сигналы — оно их создаёт. Частота 96.6 — это дверь. Не открывай. Не отвечай. Выключи всё и дождись рассвета. Это единственный способ. — Козлов, последняя запись, 1989.", shortMessage = "СЕКРЕТ — Последняя запись Козлова", voiceType = "OLD_RECORDING", frequency = 91.1, duration = 60, decodeTime = 10.0, nights = {6, 7}, repeatable = false, loreValue = 15, dangerModifier = -0.10, isHiddenEnding = true, conditions = {"SAFE_OLDSTATION_01_LOGGED", "DANGER_OLDOP_01_LOGGED"}, }, }, } ------------------------------------------------------------ -- RADIO STATE ------------------------------------------------------------ local RadioState = { active = false, currentFrequency = 98.0, targetFrequency = 98.0, powerOn = true, -- Active signals on the spectrum activeSignals = {}, signalIdCounter = 0, -- Currently detected signal detectedSignal = nil, signalStrength = 0, signalLocked = false, -- Decode decoding = false, decodeProgress = 0, decodeTarget = nil, decodeStartTime = 0, decodeTotalTime = 0, -- Static staticLevel = RadioConfig.STATIC_BASE_VOLUME, interferenceActive = false, interferenceTimer = 0, interferenceDuration = 0, -- Journal journal = {}, loggedSignalIds = {}, -- Timers lastTuneTime = 0, lastLogTime = 0, lastScanTime = 0, lastStateSyncTime = 0, lastSignalCheckTime = 0, lastInterferenceCheckTime = 0, lastDriftCheckTime = 0, -- Stats totalSignalsDetected = 0, totalSignalsLogged = 0, totalDangerousLogged = 0, totalFalseIdentified = 0, totalCriticalLogged = 0, hiddenSignalFound = false, -- Per-night tracking nightSignalPool = {}, usedSignalIds = {}, spawnedThisNight = 0, } ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL GENERATION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GenerateFrequency() local freq = RadioConfig.FREQ_MIN + math.random() * (RadioConfig.FREQ_MAX - RadioConfig.FREQ_MIN) freq = math.floor(freq * 10 + 0.5) / 10 return freq end local function GetAvailableSignals(signalType, nightNumber) local pool = SignalDatabase[signalType] if not pool then return {} end local available = {} for _, sig in ipairs(pool) do local nightValid = false for _, n in ipairs(sig.nights) do if n == nightNumber then nightValid = true; break end end if nightValid then if sig.repeatable or not RadioState.usedSignalIds[sig.id] then -- Check conditions for hidden signals if sig.conditions then local allMet = true for _, cond in ipairs(sig.conditions) do if not RadioState.loggedSignalIds[cond:gsub("_LOGGED", "")] then allMet = false break end end if not allMet then nightValid = false end end if nightValid then table.insert(available, sig) end end end end return available end local function CreateActiveSignal(template, signalType) RadioState.signalIdCounter = RadioState.signalIdCounter + 1 local signalId = "RSIG_" .. tostring(RadioState.signalIdCounter) .. "_" .. tostring(tick()) local freq = template.frequency or GenerateFrequency() -- Ensure frequency doesn't overlap with existing signals local attempts = 0 while attempts < 20 do local overlap = false for _, existing in ipairs(RadioState.activeSignals) do if math.abs(existing.frequency - freq) < 1.0 then overlap = true break end end if not overlap then break end freq = GenerateFrequency() attempts = attempts + 1 end local duration = template.duration or (RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DURATION_MIN + math.random() * (RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DURATION_MAX - RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DURATION_MIN)) local signal = { id = signalId, templateId = template.id, type = signalType, frequency = freq, originalFrequency = freq, title = template.title, message = template.message, shortMessage = template.shortMessage, voiceType = template.voiceType, decodeTime = template.decodeTime or RadioConfig.DECODE_TIME_BASE, duration = duration, spawnTime = tick(), active = true, detected = false, decoded = false, logged = false, strength = 0, fading = false, fadeStartTime = 0, -- Danger properties dangerModifier = template.dangerModifier or 0, anomalyTrigger = template.anomalyTrigger, entityAttraction = template.entityAttraction or 0, entitySpawn = template.entitySpawn or false, powerOutage = template.powerOutage or false, powerOutageDuration = template.powerOutageDuration or 0, -- False signal indicators falseIndicators = template.falseIndicators, -- Lore loreValue = template.loreValue or 0, -- Hidden isHiddenEnding = template.isHiddenEnding or false, -- Night data nightNumber = GetNightNumber(), phase = GetNightPhase(), } return signal end local function SpawnSignalOfType(signalType) local nightNum = GetNightNumber() local available = GetAvailableSignals(signalType, nightNum) if #available == 0 then -- Fallback to repeatable signals of any night available = GetAvailableSignals(signalType, nightNum) if #available == 0 then return nil end end local template = available[math.random(1, #available)] local signal = CreateActiveSignal(template, signalType) table.insert(RadioState.activeSignals, signal) RadioState.spawnedThisNight = RadioState.spawnedThisNight + 1 if not template.repeatable then RadioState.usedSignalIds[template.id] = true end -- Notify night cycle CallNightAPI("SpawnSignal", signalType) print("[RadioSystem] Signal spawned: " .. signal.type .. " — " .. signal.title .. " @ " .. string.format("%.1f", signal.frequency) .. " MHz") return signal end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL DETECTION ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CalculateSignalStrength(signalFreq, tuneFreq) local diff = math.abs(signalFreq - tuneFreq) if diff <= RadioConfig.SIGNAL_PERFECT_RANGE then return RadioConfig.STRENGTH_PERFECT elseif diff <= RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DETECTION_RANGE then local t = (diff - RadioConfig.SIGNAL_PERFECT_RANGE) / (RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DETECTION_RANGE - RadioConfig.SIGNAL_PERFECT_RANGE) return RadioConfig.STRENGTH_PERFECT - t * (RadioConfig.STRENGTH_PERFECT - RadioConfig.STRENGTH_GOOD) elseif diff <= RadioConfig.SIGNAL_WEAK_RANGE then local t = (diff - RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DETECTION_RANGE) / (RadioConfig.SIGNAL_WEAK_RANGE - RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DETECTION_RANGE) return RadioConfig.STRENGTH_GOOD - t * (RadioConfig.STRENGTH_GOOD - RadioConfig.STRENGTH_WEAK) end return RadioConfig.STRENGTH_NONE end local function ScanForSignals() local freq = RadioState.currentFrequency local bestSignal = nil local bestStrength = 0 for _, signal in ipairs(RadioState.activeSignals) do if signal.active then local strength = CalculateSignalStrength(signal.frequency, freq) -- Fading reduction if signal.fading then local fadeElapsed = tick() - signal.fadeStartTime local fadeFactor = 1 - math.clamp(fadeElapsed / RadioConfig.SIGNAL_FADE_DURATION, 0, 1) strength = strength * fadeFactor end signal.strength = strength if strength > bestStrength then bestStrength = strength bestSignal = signal end end end -- Update detection state local prevDetected = RadioState.detectedSignal RadioState.detectedSignal = bestSignal RadioState.signalStrength = bestStrength -- Signal found/lost events if bestSignal and (not prevDetected or prevDetected.id ~= bestSignal.id) then if not bestSignal.detected then bestSignal.detected = true RadioState.totalSignalsDetected = RadioState.totalSignalsDetected + 1 end for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioSignalFound:FireClient(player, { signalId = bestSignal.id, type = bestSignal.type, strength = bestStrength, frequency = bestSignal.frequency, voiceType = bestSignal.voiceType, }) end elseif not bestSignal and prevDetected then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioSignalLost:FireClient(player, { signalId = prevDetected.id, reason = "OUT_OF_RANGE", }) end -- Interrupt decode if RadioState.decoding and RadioState.decodeTarget and RadioState.decodeTarget.id == prevDetected.id then RadioState.decoding = false RadioState.decodeProgress = 0 RadioState.decodeTarget = nil end end -- Update static level local staticBase = RadioConfig.STATIC_BASE_VOLUME if bestStrength > 0.1 then staticBase = staticBase * (1 - bestStrength * RadioConfig.STATIC_SIGNAL_REDUCTION) end if RadioState.interferenceActive then staticBase = staticBase + RadioConfig.STATIC_INTERFERENCE_BOOST end staticBase = staticBase + GetThreatLevel() * RadioConfig.STATIC_THREAT_BOOST RadioState.staticLevel = math.clamp(staticBase, 0, 1) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- DECODE SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function StartDecode(signal, player) if not signal or signal.decoded then return end if RadioState.decoding then return end local decodeTime = signal.decodeTime or RadioConfig.DECODE_TIME_BASE -- Type multipliers if signal.type == "DANGEROUS" then decodeTime = math.max(decodeTime, RadioConfig.DECODE_TIME_DANGEROUS) elseif signal.type == "CRITICAL" then decodeTime = math.max(decodeTime, RadioConfig.DECODE_TIME_CRITICAL) elseif signal.type == "HIDDEN" then decodeTime = math.max(decodeTime, RadioConfig.DECODE_TIME_HIDDEN) end -- Strength bonus (better signal = faster decode) if RadioState.signalStrength >= RadioConfig.STRENGTH_PERFECT then decodeTime = decodeTime * RadioConfig.DECODE_STRENGTH_BONUS elseif RadioState.signalStrength >= RadioConfig.STRENGTH_GOOD then decodeTime = decodeTime * 0.85 end RadioState.decoding = true RadioState.decodeProgress = 0 RadioState.decodeTarget = signal RadioState.decodeStartTime = tick() RadioState.decodeTotalTime = decodeTime for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(p, { signalId = signal.id, started = true, totalTime = decodeTime, progress = 0, }) end end local function UpdateDecode(dt) if not RadioState.decoding or not RadioState.decodeTarget then return end local signal = RadioState.decodeTarget -- Check signal still active and in range if not signal.active or RadioState.signalStrength < RadioConfig.DECODE_INTERRUPT_THRESHOLD then -- Decode interrupted RadioState.decoding = false RadioState.decodeProgress = 0 RadioState.decodeTarget = nil for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(player, { signalId = signal.id, interrupted = true, reason = signal.active and "SIGNAL_WEAK" or "SIGNAL_LOST", }) end return end -- Interference interrupts decode if RadioState.interferenceActive then RadioState.decodeProgress = math.max(0, RadioState.decodeProgress - dt * 0.3) for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(player, { signalId = signal.id, progress = RadioState.decodeProgress / RadioState.decodeTotalTime, interference = true, }) end return end RadioState.decodeProgress = RadioState.decodeProgress + dt local progress = math.clamp(RadioState.decodeProgress / RadioState.decodeTotalTime, 0, 1) -- Send progress updates for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(player, { signalId = signal.id, progress = progress, timeRemaining = RadioState.decodeTotalTime - RadioState.decodeProgress, }) end -- Decode complete if progress >= 1.0 then signal.decoded = true RadioState.decoding = false RadioState.decodeProgress = 0 RadioState.decodeTarget = nil -- Send decoded message for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioMessageEvent:FireClient(player, { signalId = signal.id, type = signal.type, title = signal.title, message = signal.message, shortMessage = signal.shortMessage, voiceType = signal.voiceType, frequency = signal.frequency, dangerLevel = signal.dangerModifier, falseIndicators = signal.falseIndicators, loreValue = signal.loreValue, isHidden = signal.isHiddenEnding, }) RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(player, { signalId = signal.id, completed = true, }) end -- Trigger effects based on signal type if signal.anomalyTrigger then task.delay(0.5 + math.random() * 2, function() CallNightAPI("TriggerAnomaly", signal.anomalyTrigger) end) end if signal.entitySpawn then task.delay(2 + math.random() * 4, function() CallNightAPI("SpawnEntity") end) end if signal.powerOutage then task.delay(0.5, function() CallNightAPI("TriggerPowerOutage", "CRITICAL_SIGNAL", signal.powerOutageDuration) end) end if signal.entityAttraction > 0 then -- Increase noise for entity for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CallNightAPI("AddPlayerNoise", player, signal.entityAttraction) end end -- Camera effects for dangerous/critical if signal.type == "DANGEROUS" or signal.type == "CRITICAL" then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do CameraEffectRequest:FireClient(player, { effect = signal.type == "CRITICAL" and "REALITY_TEAR" or "TEMPORAL_DISTORTION", intensity = signal.dangerModifier * 2, duration = 2.0, }) end end print("[RadioSystem] Signal decoded: " .. signal.type .. " — " .. signal.title) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- LOG SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function LogSignal(signal, player) if not signal or signal.logged then return false end if not signal.decoded then return false end signal.logged = true RadioState.totalSignalsLogged = RadioState.totalSignalsLogged + 1 RadioState.loggedSignalIds[signal.templateId] = true if signal.type == "DANGEROUS" then RadioState.totalDangerousLogged = RadioState.totalDangerousLogged + 1 elseif signal.type == "FALSE" then RadioState.totalFalseIdentified = RadioState.totalFalseIdentified + 1 elseif signal.type == "CRITICAL" then RadioState.totalCriticalLogged = RadioState.totalCriticalLogged + 1 end -- Hidden ending trigger if signal.isHiddenEnding then RadioState.hiddenSignalFound = true CallNightAPI("SetHiddenSignalFound", true) end -- Journal entry local entry = { signalId = signal.id, templateId = signal.templateId, type = signal.type, title = signal.title, shortMessage = signal.shortMessage, frequency = signal.frequency, nightNumber = signal.nightNumber, logTime = tick(), loreValue = signal.loreValue, falseIndicators = signal.falseIndicators, isHidden = signal.isHiddenEnding, } table.insert(RadioState.journal, 1, entry) if #RadioState.journal > RadioConfig.MAX_JOURNAL_ENTRIES then table.remove(RadioState.journal) end -- Notify night cycle CallNightAPI("LogSignal", signal.id, player) -- Send journal update for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioJournalUpdate:FireClient(p, { entry = entry, totalLogged = RadioState.totalSignalsLogged, journal = RadioState.journal, }) UINotification:FireClient(p, { type = "SIGNAL_LOGGED", signalType = signal.type, title = signal.title, shortMessage = signal.shortMessage, }) end print("[RadioSystem] Signal logged: " .. signal.type .. " — " .. signal.title) return true end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INTERFERENCE SYSTEM ------------------------------------------------------------ local function CheckInterference() if RadioState.interferenceActive then return end local chance = RadioConfig.INTERFERENCE_CHANCE_BASE chance = chance + GetThreatLevel() * RadioConfig.INTERFERENCE_THREAT_MULT * 0.01 if math.random() < chance then RadioState.interferenceActive = true RadioState.interferenceTimer = 0 RadioState.interferenceDuration = RadioConfig.INTERFERENCE_DURATION_MIN + math.random() * (RadioConfig.INTERFERENCE_DURATION_MAX - RadioConfig.INTERFERENCE_DURATION_MIN) for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioInterference:FireClient(player, { active = true, duration = RadioState.interferenceDuration, intensity = 0.5 + GetThreatLevel() * 0.5, }) end end end local function UpdateInterference(dt) if not RadioState.interferenceActive then return end RadioState.interferenceTimer = RadioState.interferenceTimer + dt if RadioState.interferenceTimer >= RadioState.interferenceDuration then RadioState.interferenceActive = false RadioState.interferenceTimer = 0 for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioInterference:FireClient(player, { active = false, }) end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL DRIFT ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateSignalDrift() for _, signal in ipairs(RadioState.activeSignals) do if signal.active and not signal.fading then if math.random() < RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DRIFT_CHANCE then local drift = (math.random() - 0.5) * 2 * RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DRIFT_AMOUNT signal.frequency = math.clamp( signal.frequency + drift, RadioConfig.FREQ_MIN, RadioConfig.FREQ_MAX ) signal.frequency = math.floor(signal.frequency * 10 + 0.5) / 10 end end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL LIFECYCLE ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateSignalLifecycle(dt) local toRemove = {} for i, signal in ipairs(RadioState.activeSignals) do if signal.active then local elapsed = tick() - signal.spawnTime -- Start fading before expiry if elapsed >= signal.duration - RadioConfig.SIGNAL_FADE_DURATION and not signal.fading then signal.fading = true signal.fadeStartTime = tick() end -- Expire if elapsed >= signal.duration then signal.active = false table.insert(toRemove, i) -- Notify if currently detected if RadioState.detectedSignal and RadioState.detectedSignal.id == signal.id then for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioSignalLost:FireClient(player, { signalId = signal.id, reason = "EXPIRED", }) end RadioState.detectedSignal = nil RadioState.signalStrength = 0 end end end end for i = #toRemove, 1, -1 do table.remove(RadioState.activeSignals, toRemove[i]) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SIGNAL SPAWN LOGIC (based on night phase) ------------------------------------------------------------ local function ShouldSpawnNewSignal() if #RadioState.activeSignals >= RadioConfig.MAX_ACTIVE_SIGNALS then return false end if not IsNightActive() then return false end local phase = GetNightPhase() local threat = GetThreatLevel() local nightNum = GetNightNumber() local baseChance = 0 if phase == "PREPARATION" then baseChance = 0.0 elseif phase == "EARLY" then baseChance = 0.04 elseif phase == "RISING" then baseChance = 0.08 elseif phase == "MID" then baseChance = 0.12 elseif phase == "ESCALATION" then baseChance = 0.16 elseif phase == "PEAK" then baseChance = 0.20 elseif phase == "CLIMAX" then baseChance = 0.25 elseif phase == "RESOLUTION" then baseChance = 0.02 end baseChance = baseChance + threat * 0.05 baseChance = baseChance * (0.8 + nightNum * 0.05) return math.random() < baseChance end local function ChooseSignalType() local phase = GetNightPhase() local nightNum = GetNightNumber() local threat = GetThreatLevel() -- Weight table local weights = { SAFE = 40, FALSE = 0, DANGEROUS = 0, CRITICAL = 0, HIDDEN = 0, } -- Phase-based adjustments if phase == "EARLY" then weights.SAFE = 70 weights.FALSE = nightNum >= 2 and 20 or 0 weights.DANGEROUS = nightNum >= 3 and 10 or 0 elseif phase == "RISING" then weights.SAFE = 45 weights.FALSE = nightNum >= 2 and 25 or 0 weights.DANGEROUS = nightNum >= 3 and 25 or 5 weights.CRITICAL = nightNum >= 4 and 5 or 0 elseif phase == "MID" then weights.SAFE = 30 weights.FALSE = 25 weights.DANGEROUS = 35 weights.CRITICAL = nightNum >= 4 and 10 or 0 elseif phase == "ESCALATION" then weights.SAFE = 15 weights.FALSE = 20 weights.DANGEROUS = 45 weights.CRITICAL = nightNum >= 4 and 15 or 5 weights.HIDDEN = nightNum >= 6 and 5 or 0 elseif phase == "PEAK" then weights.SAFE = 10 weights.FALSE = 15 weights.DANGEROUS = 45 weights.CRITICAL = nightNum >= 4 and 25 or 10 weights.HIDDEN = nightNum >= 6 and 5 or 0 elseif phase == "CLIMAX" then weights.SAFE = 5 weights.FALSE = 10 weights.DANGEROUS = 40 weights.CRITICAL = 35 weights.HIDDEN = nightNum >= 6 and 10 or 0 elseif phase == "RESOLUTION" then weights.SAFE = 80 weights.DANGEROUS = 15 weights.CRITICAL = 5 end -- Hidden signal only if conditions are met if weights.HIDDEN > 0 then local available = GetAvailableSignals("HIDDEN", nightNum) if #available == 0 then weights.HIDDEN = 0 end end -- Threat boost for dangerous weights.DANGEROUS = weights.DANGEROUS + threat * 20 weights.CRITICAL = weights.CRITICAL + threat * 10 -- Calculate total local total = 0 for _, w in pairs(weights) do total = total + w end if total <= 0 then return "SAFE" end local roll = math.random() * total local cumulative = 0 for signalType, weight in pairs(weights) do cumulative = cumulative + weight if roll <= cumulative then return signalType end end return "SAFE" end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- REMOTE EVENT HANDLERS ------------------------------------------------------------ -- Player tunes radio frequency RadioTuneEvent.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, data) if not data then return end local now = tick() if now - RadioState.lastTuneTime < RadioConfig.TUNE_COOLDOWN then return end RadioState.lastTuneTime = now local newFreq = data.frequency if type(newFreq) ~= "number" then return end newFreq = math.clamp(newFreq, RadioConfig.FREQ_MIN, RadioConfig.FREQ_MAX) newFreq = math.floor(newFreq * 10 + 0.5) / 10 RadioState.currentFrequency = newFreq RadioState.targetFrequency = newFreq -- Cancel decode if frequency changes significantly if RadioState.decoding and RadioState.decodeTarget then local diff = math.abs(RadioState.decodeTarget.frequency - newFreq) if diff > RadioConfig.SIGNAL_DETECTION_RANGE then RadioState.decoding = false RadioState.decodeProgress = 0 for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(p, { signalId = RadioState.decodeTarget.id, interrupted = true, reason = "FREQUENCY_CHANGED", }) end RadioState.decodeTarget = nil end end -- Immediate scan ScanForSignals() -- Update all clients for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioStaticUpdate:FireClient(p, { frequency = RadioState.currentFrequency, staticLevel = RadioState.staticLevel, signalStrength = RadioState.signalStrength, signalType = RadioState.detectedSignal and RadioState.detectedSignal.type or nil, voiceType = RadioState.detectedSignal and RadioState.detectedSignal.voiceType or nil, interference = RadioState.interferenceActive, }) end end) -- Player requests decode local DecodeRequestEvent = MakeRemote("RemoteEvent", "RadioDecodeRequest") DecodeRequestEvent.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, data) if not data then return end if data.action == "START" then if RadioState.detectedSignal and not RadioState.detectedSignal.decoded then StartDecode(RadioState.detectedSignal, player) end elseif data.action == "CANCEL" then if RadioState.decoding then RadioState.decoding = false RadioState.decodeProgress = 0 if RadioState.decodeTarget then for _, p in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioDecodeProgress:FireClient(p, { signalId = RadioState.decodeTarget.id, interrupted = true, reason = "CANCELLED", }) end end RadioState.decodeTarget = nil end end end) -- Player logs signal RadioLogSignal.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, data) if not data then return end local now = tick() if now - RadioState.lastLogTime < RadioConfig.LOG_COOLDOWN then return end RadioState.lastLogTime = now local signalId = data.signalId if type(signalId) ~= "string" then return end for _, signal in ipairs(RadioState.activeSignals) do if signal.id == signalId then LogSignal(signal, player) break end end end) -- Get radio state GetRadioState.OnServerInvoke = function(player) return { active = RadioState.active, frequency = RadioState.currentFrequency, staticLevel = RadioState.staticLevel, signalStrength = RadioState.signalStrength, signalDetected = RadioState.detectedSignal ~= nil, signalType = RadioState.detectedSignal and RadioState.detectedSignal.type or nil, signalDecoded = RadioState.detectedSignal and RadioState.detectedSignal.decoded or false, decoding = RadioState.decoding, decodeProgress = RadioState.decoding and (RadioState.decodeProgress / math.max(RadioState.decodeTotalTime, 0.01)) or 0, interference = RadioState.interferenceActive, journal = RadioState.journal, totalLogged = RadioState.totalSignalsLogged, powerOn = RadioState.powerOn, freqMin = RadioConfig.FREQ_MIN, freqMax = RadioConfig.FREQ_MAX, } end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- NIGHT EVENTS INTEGRATION ------------------------------------------------------------ -- Listen for night start/end if SharedData then local nightActive = SharedData:FindFirstChild("NightActive") if nightActive then nightActive.Changed:Connect(function(value) if value then -- Night started — reset radio RadioState.active = true RadioStateChanged:FireClient(player, { powerOff = true, }) end else for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do RadioStateChanged:FireClient(player, { powerOn = true, frequency = RadioState.currentFrequency, }) end end end) end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN UPDATE LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt) if not RadioState.active then return end if not RadioState.powerOn then return end if not IsNightActive() then return end local now = tick() -- Scan for ------------------------------------------------------------ local function GetSignalColor(sigType) if sigType == "SAFE" then return RC.COL_SIGNAL_SAFE elseif sigType == "FALSE" then return RC.COL_SIGNAL_FALSE elseif sigType == "DANGEROUS" then return RC.COL_SIGNAL_DANGER elseif sigType == "CRITICAL" then return RC.COL_SIGNAL_CRITICAL elseif sigType == "HIDDEN" then return RC.COL_SIGNAL_HIDDEN end return RC.COL_SIGNAL_UNKNOWN end local function GetSignalTypeName(sigType) if sigType == "SAFE" then return "БЕЗОПАСНЫЙ" elseif sigType == "FALSE" then return "ЛОЖНЫЙ" elseif sigType == "DANGEROUS" then return "ОПАСНЫЙ" elseif sigType == "CRITICAL" then return "КРИТИЧЕСКИЙ" elseif sigType == "HIDDEN" then return "СКРЫТЫЙ" end return "НЕИЗВЕСТНЫЙ" end local function TweenSndVol(snd, vol, dur) if not snd then return end TweenService:Create(snd, TweenInfo.new(dur or 0.5, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine), {Volume = vol}):Play() end local function SetFrequency(freq) freq = math.clamp(freq, RC.FREQ_MIN, RC.FREQ_MAX) freq = math.floor(freq * 10 + 0.5) / 10 RS.frequency = freq RS.targetFreq = freq if RadioTuneEvent then RadioTuneEvent:FireServer({frequency = freq}) end end local function AddJournalEntry(entry) local frame = Instance.new("Frame") frame.Name = "JE_" .. (entry.signalId or "unknown") frame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 24) frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(15, 18, 28) frame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3 frame.BorderSizePixel = 0 frame.LayoutOrder = -#RS.journal frame.ZIndex = 4 frame.Parent = JournalScroll Instance.new("UICorner", frame).CornerRadius = UDim.new(0, 4) local typeDot = Instance.new("Frame") typeDot.Size = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0, 6) typeDot.Position = UDim2.new(0, 6, 0.5, -3) typeDot.BackgroundColor3 = GetSignalColor(entry.type) typeDot.BorderSizePixel = 0 typeDot.ZIndex = 5 typeDot.Parent = frame Instance.new("UICorner", typeDot).CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0) local freqLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel") freqLbl.Size = UDim2.new(0, 42, 1, 0) freqLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 16, 0, 0) freqLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1 freqLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Code freqLbl.TextColor3 = RC.COL_FREQ_DIM freqLbl.TextSize = 9 freqLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left freqLbl.Text = string.format("%.1f", entry.frequency or 0) freqLbl.ZIndex = 5 freqLbl.Parent = frame local msgLbl = Instance.new("TextLabel") msgLbl.Size = UDim2.new(1, -70, 1, 0) msgLbl.Position = UDim2.new(0, 62, 0, 0) msgLbl.BackgroundTransparency = 1 msgLbl.Font = Enum.Font.Gotham msgLbl.TextColor3 = RC.COL_TEXT msgLbl.TextSize = 9 msgLbl.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left msgLbl.TextTruncate = Enum.TextTruncate.AtEnd msgLbl.Text = entry.shortMessage or entry.title or "—" msgLbl.ZIndex = 5 msgLbl.Parent = frame JournalScroll.CanvasSize = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, JournalLayout.AbsoluteContentSize.Y + 4) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- DIAL INTERACTION ------------------------------------------------------------ DialKnob.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function(x, y) RS.dialDragging = true RS.dialLastX = x end) UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(inp) if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then RS.dialDragging = false end end) UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(inp, gp) if not RS.visible then return end if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement and RS.dialDragging then local dx = inp.Position.X - RS.dialLastX RS.dialLastX = inp.Position.X local sens = RS.dialFineTune and RC.DIAL_FINE_SENSITIVITY or RC.DIAL_SENSITIVITY RS.dialVelocity = RS.dialVelocity + dx * sens RS.dialVelocity = math.clamp(RS.dialVelocity, -RC.DIAL_MAX_VELOCITY, RC.DIAL_MAX_VELOCITY) end if inp.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseWheel and not gp then -- Check if mouse is over radio GUI local mousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation() local absPos = MainFrame.AbsolutePosition local absSize = MainFrame.AbsoluteSize if mousePos.X >= absPos.X and mousePos.X <= absPos.X + absSize.X and mousePos.Y >= absPos.Y and mousePos.Y <= absPos.Y + absSize.Y then local scrollDir = inp.Position.Z local step = RS.dialFineTune and RC.FREQ_FINE_STEP or RC.DIAL_SCROLL_STEP SetFrequency(RS.frequency + scrollDir * step) SndTuneClick.PlaybackSpeed = 0.9 + math.random() * 0.2 SndTuneClick:Play() end end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- BUTTON HANDLERS ------------------------------------------------------------ DecodeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() if RS.signalDetected and not RS.signalDecoded and not RS.decoding then if RadioDecodeRequest then RadioDecodeRequest:FireServer({action = "START"}) end elseif RS.decoding then if RadioDecodeRequest then RadioDecodeRequest:FireServer({action = "CANCEL"}) end end end) LogBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function() if RS.signalDecoded and not RS.signalLogged and RS.currentMessage then if RadioLogSignal then RadioLogSignal:FireServer({signalId = RS.currentMessage.signalId}) end SndLogConfirm:Play() end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INPUT ------------------------------------------------------------ UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(inp, gp) if gp then return end if inp.KeyCode == RC.TOGGLE_KEY then RS.visible = not RS.visible if RS.visible then SndOpen:Play() else SndClose:Play() end end if inp.KeyCode == RC.DECODE_KEY and RS.visible then if RS.signalDetected and not RS.signalDecoded and not RS.decoding then if RadioDecodeRequest then RadioDecodeRequest:FireServer({action = "START"}) end end end if inp.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftAlt then RS.dialFineTune = true end end) UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(inp) if inp.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.LeftAlt then RS.dialFineTune = false end end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- SERVER EVENT HANDLERS ------------------------------------------------------------ if RadioSignalUpdate then RadioSignalUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end RS.frequency = data.frequency or RS.frequency RS.staticLevel = data.staticLevel or RS.staticLevel RS.signalStrength = data.signalStrength or 0 RS.signalDetected = data.signalDetected or false RS.signalType = data.signalType RS.signalTitle = data.signalTitle RS.signalDecoded = data.signalDecoded or false RS.signalLogged = data.signalLogged or false RS.voiceType = data.voiceType RS.decoding = data.decoding or false RS.decodeProgress = data.decodeProgress or 0 RS.interference = data.interference or false RS.activeSignalCount = data.activeSignalCount or 0 RS.totalLogged = data.totalLogged or 0 end) end if RadioStaticUpdate then RadioStaticUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end RS.staticLevel = data.staticLevel or RS.staticLevel RS.signalStrength = data.signalStrength or RS.signalStrength RS.interference = data.interference or false end) end if RadioSignalFound then RadioSignalFound.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end RS.signalDetected = true RS.signalType = data.type RS.voiceType = data.voiceType RS.signalStrength = data.strength or 0 RS.signalDecoded = false RS.signalLogged = false SndSignalFound:Play() end) end if RadioSignalLost then RadioSignalLost.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end RS.signalDetected = false RS.signalStrength = 0 RS.signalType = nil RS.signalDecoded = false RS.signalLogged = false SndSignalLost:Play() end) end if RadioDecodeProgress then RadioDecodeProgress.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end if data.started then RS.decoding = true RS.decodeProgress = 0 RS.decodeCompleted = false RS.decodeInterrupted = false SndDecodeStart:Play() if not SndDecodeProgress.IsPlaying then SndDecodeProgress:Play() end TweenSndVol(SndDecodeProgress, 0.08, 0.3) elseif data.interrupted then RS.decoding = false RS.decodeProgress = 0 RS.decodeInterrupted = true SndDecodeFail:Play() TweenSndVol(SndDecodeProgress, 0, 0.2) elseif data.completed then RS.decoding = false RS.decodeProgress = 1 RS.decodeCompleted = true RS.signalDecoded = true SndDecodeComplete:Play() TweenSndVol(SndDecodeProgress, 0, 0.2) else RS.decodeProgress = data.progress or RS.decodeProgress if data.interference then RS.decodeProgress = math.max(0, RS.decodeProgress - 0.01) end end end) end if RadioMessageEvent then RadioMessageEvent.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end RS.currentMessage = data RS.messageTimer = RC.MESSAGE_DISPLAY_TIME RS.messageVisible = true RS.signalDecoded = true -- Alert sounds if data.type == "DANGEROUS" then SndDangerAlert:Play() elseif data.type == "CRITICAL" then SndCriticalAlert:Play() elseif data.type == "HIDDEN" then SndHiddenFound:Play() end end) end if RadioInterference then RadioInterference.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end RS.interference = data.active or false RS.interferenceIntensity = data.intensity or 0 if RS.interference then if not SndInterference.IsPlaying then SndInterference:Play() end TweenSndVol(SndInterference, 0.15 + RS.interferenceIntensity * 0.2, 0.3) else TweenSndVol(SndInterference, 0, 0.5) end end) end if RadioStateChanged then RadioStateChanged.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end if data.active ~= nil then RS.powered = data.active if data.active then SndPowerOn:Play() RS.poweringOn = true RS.powerAnimT = 0 end end if data.powerOff then RS.powered = false SndPowerOff:Play() RS.poweringOff = true RS.powerAnimT = 0 TweenSndVol(SndStatic, 0, 0.3) end if data.powerOn then RS.powered = true SndPowerOn:Play() RS.poweringOn = true RS.powerAnimT = 0 end if data.frequency then RS.frequency = data.frequency end end) end if RadioJournalUpdate then RadioJournalUpdate.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(data) if not data then return end if data.entry then table.insert(RS.journal, 1, data.entry) AddJournalEntry(data.entry) RS.signalLogged = true SndPageTurn:Play() end RS.totalLogged = data.totalLogged or RS.totalLogged end) end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- UPDATE FUNCTIONS ------------------------------------------------------------ local function UpdateDial(dt) -- Apply velocity with friction if not RS.dialDragging then RS.dialVelocity = RS.dialVelocity * RC.DIAL_FRICTION if math.abs(RS.dialVelocity) < 0.01 then RS.dialVelocity = 0 end end if math.abs(RS.dialVelocity) > 0.01 then local step = RS.dialFineTune and RC.FREQ_FINE_STEP or RC.FREQ_STEP local freqChange = RS.dialVelocity * step SetFrequency(RS.frequency + freqChange) if math.abs(freqChange) > 0.05 then SndTuneClick.PlaybackSpeed = 0.85 + math.abs(RS.dialVelocity) * 0.15 SndTuneClick.Volume = math.clamp(math.abs(RS.dialVelocity) * 0.04, 0.02, 0.1) if not SndTuneClick.IsPlaying then SndTuneClick:Play() end end end -- Dial visual rotation local freqRange = RC.FREQ_MAX - RC.FREQ_MIN local freqNorm = (RS.frequency - RC.FREQ_MIN) / freqRange RS.dialAngle = -RC.DIAL_ROTATION_RANGE / 2 + freqNorm * RC.DIAL_ROTATION_RANGE DialKnob.Rotation = RS.dialAngle end local function UpdateSpectrum(dt) local now = tick() if now - RS.lastSpectrumUpdate < RC.SPECTRUM_UPDATE_RATE then return end RS.lastSpectrumUpdate = now local freqRange = RC.FREQ_MAX - RC.FREQ_MIN local currentNorm = (RS.frequency - RC.FREQ_MIN) / freqRange for i = 1, RC.SPECTRUM_BARS do local barNorm = (i - 0.5) / RC.SPECTRUM_BARS local noise = RC.SPECTRUM_NOISE_BASE + math.random() * RC.SPECTRUM_NOISE_VARIANCE -- Interference boost if RS.interference then noise = noise + RS.interferenceIntensity * 0.3 * math.random() end -- Signal peaks (simulated, actual signal positions not known to client precisely) local signalBoost = 0 if RS.signalDetected and RS.signalStrength > 0.1 then local signalNorm = currentNorm local dist = math.abs(barNorm - signalNorm) if dist < 0.05 then signalBoost = (1 - dist / 0.05) * RC.SPECTRUM_SIGNAL_HEIGHT * RS.signalStrength end end RS.spectrumTargets[i] = math.clamp(noise + signalBoost, 0, 1) -- Smooth decay RS.spectrumBars[i] = math.max( RS.spectrumBars[i] * RC.SPECTRUM_DECAY, RS.spectrumTargets[i] ) -- Update peak hold if RS.spectrumBars[i] > RS.spectrumPeaks[i] then RS.spectrumPeaks[i] = RS.spectrumBars[i] else RS.spectrumPeaks[i] = RS.spectrumPeaks[i] * 0.97 end -- Visual update local bar = SpectrumBarFrames[i] if bar then local height = math.max(2, RS.spectrumBars[i] * (SpecBarsContainer.AbsoluteSize.Y - 18)) bar.Size = UDim2.new(barW, -1, 0, height) bar.Position = UDim2.new((i - 1) * barW, 0, 1, -height) if RS.spectrumBars[i] > 0.5 then bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_SPECTRUM_PEAK:Lerp(RC.COL_SIGNAL_DANGER, (RS.spectrumBars[i] - 0.5) * 2) elseif RS.spectrumBars[i] > 0.15 then bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_SPECTRUM_BAR:Lerp(RC.COL_SPECTRUM_PEAK, (RS.spectrumBars[i] - 0.15) / 0.35) else bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_SPECTRUM_NOISE:Lerp(RC.COL_SPECTRUM_BAR, RS.spectrumBars[i] / 0.15) end end end -- Frequency indicator position FreqIndicator.Position = UDim2.new(currentNorm, -1, 0, 0) -- Scanline animation RS.scanlineOffset = (RS.scanlineOffset + dt * 0.3) % 1 ScanLine.Position = UDim2.new(RS.scanlineOffset, 0, 0, 0) ScanLine.BackgroundTransparency = 0.7 + math.sin(tick() * 3) * 0.15 end local function UpdateMeter(dt) local now = tick() if now - RS.lastMeterUpdate < RC.METER_UPDATE_RATE then return end RS.lastMeterUpdate = now RS.meterTarget = RS.signalStrength RS.meterValue = RS.meterValue + (RS.meterTarget - RS.meterValue) * 0.2 local activeBars = math.floor(RS.meterValue * RC.METER_SEGMENTS) for i, bar in ipairs(MeterBars) do if i <= activeBars then if i <= 4 then bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_METER_MED elseif i <= 8 then bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_METER_HIGH elseif i <= 10 then bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_METER_HIGH else bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_METER_PEAK end bar.BackgroundTransparency = 0 else bar.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_METER_LOW bar.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5 end end end local function UpdateUI(dt) -- Frequency display FreqValueLabel.Text = string.format("%.1f", RS.frequency) -- Frequency scale indicator local freqNorm = (RS.frequency - RC.FREQ_MIN) / (RC.FREQ_MAX - RC.FREQ_MIN) FreqScaleIndicator.Position = UDim2.new(freqNorm, -1, 0, -1) -- Signal type label if RS.signalDetected then if RS.signalDecoded and RS.signalType then SignalTypeLabel.Text = GetSignalTypeName(RS.signalType) SignalTypeLabel.TextColor3 = GetSignalColor(RS.signalType) else SignalTypeLabel.Text = "СИГНАЛ ОБНАРУЖЕН" SignalTypeLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_FREQ end else SignalTypeLabel.Text = "НЕТ СИГНАЛА" SignalTypeLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_SIGNAL_UNKNOWN end -- Signal strength percentage SignalStrengthPct.Text = math.floor(RS.signalStrength * 100) .. "%" -- Status label if RS.interference then StatusLabel.Text = "⚠ ПОМЕХИ" StatusLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_INTERFERENCE elseif RS.decoding then StatusLabel.Text = "◉ ДЕКОДИРОВАНИЕ..." StatusLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_DECODE_FILL elseif RS.signalDetected then StatusLabel.Text = "◉ СИГНАЛ НАЙДЕН" StatusLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_FREQ else StatusLabel.Text = "○ ПОИСК СИГНАЛА..." StatusLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_TEXT_DIM end -- Power indicator PowerIndicator.BackgroundColor3 = RS.powered and RC.COL_POWER_ON or RC.COL_POWER_OFF -- Decode panel DecodeBarFill.Size = UDim2.new(RS.decodeProgress, 0, 1, 0) DecodePercentLbl.Text = math.floor(RS.decodeProgress * 100) .. "%" if RS.decoding then DecodeBarFill.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_DECODE_FILL DecodeStatusLbl.Text = "Декодирование..." DecodeStatusLbl.TextColor3 = RC.COL_DECODE_FILL DecodeBtn.Text = "[G] ОТМЕНА" DecodeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 30, 30) elseif RS.signalDecoded then DecodeBarFill.BackgroundColor3 = RC.COL_DECODE_COMPLETE DecodeStatusLbl.Text = "✓ Декодировано" DecodeStatusLbl.TextColor3 = RC.COL_DECODE_COMPLETE DecodeBtn.Text = "ДЕКОДИРОВАНО" DecodeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(25, 50, 35) elseif RS.signalDetected then DecodeStatusLbl.Text = "Готов к декодированию" DecodeStatusLbl.TextColor3 = RC.COL_TEXT DecodeBtn.Text = "[G] ДЕКОДИРОВАТЬ" DecodeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 50, 80) else DecodeStatusLbl.Text = "Ожидание сигнала" DecodeStatusLbl.TextColor3 = RC.COL_TEXT_DIM DecodeBtn.Text = "[G] ДЕКОДИРОВАТЬ" DecodeBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(20, 30, 45) end -- Log button visibility LogBtn.Visible = RS.signalDecoded and not RS.signalLogged -- Message panel if RS.currentMessage and RS.messageVisible then local msg = RS.currentMessage MsgTitle.Text = msg.title or "Неизвестный сигнал" MsgTitle.TextColor3 = GetSignalColor(msg.type) MsgBody.Text = msg.message or "" MsgTypeBadge.Text = GetSignalTypeName(msg.type) MsgTypeBadge.BackgroundColor3 = GetSignalColor(msg.type) MsgTypeBadge.Visible = true if msg.falseIndicators and #msg.falseIndicators > 0 then MsgIndicators.Text = "⚠ " .. table.concat(msg.falseIndicators, " | ") MsgIndicators.Visible = true else MsgIndicators.Visible = false end end -- Journal count JournalCount.Text = tostring(RS.totalLogged) .. " записей" -- Fine tune indicator FineTuneLbl.TextColor3 = RS.dialFineTune and RC.COL_FREQ or RC.COL_TEXT_DIM -- Interference visual if RS.interference then local flicker = math.random() * RS.interferenceIntensity * 0.1 MainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.02 + flicker FreqValueLabel.TextTransparency = math.random() < 0.1 * RS.interferenceIntensity and 0.6 or 0 FreqValueLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10 + (math.random() - 0.5) * RS.interferenceIntensity * 3, 0, 18) else MainFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.02 FreqValueLabel.TextTransparency = 0 FreqValueLabel.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 18) end -- Glow pulse on signal RS.glowPulseT = RS.glowPulseT + dt if RS.signalDetected then local pulse = 0.3 + math.sin(RS.glowPulseT * 3) * 0.1 MainStroke.Color = GetSignalColor(RS.signalType or "SAFE"):Lerp(RC.COL_BORDER, pulse) MainStroke.Transparency = 0.1 + math.sin(RS.glowPulseT * 2) * 0.05 else MainStroke.Color = RC.COL_BORDER MainStroke.Transparency = 0.2 end -- Frequency color glow based on signal if RS.signalDetected and RS.signalStrength > 0.3 then FreqValueLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_FREQ:Lerp(GetSignalColor(RS.signalType or "SAFE"), RS.signalStrength * 0.5) else FreqValueLabel.TextColor3 = RC.COL_FREQ end end local function UpdateStatic(dt) local targetVol = 0 if RS.visible and RS.powered then targetVol = RS.staticLevel * RC.STATIC_VOLUME_MAX if RS.interference then targetVol = targetVol + RS.interferenceIntensity * 0.1 end end if not SndStatic.IsPlaying then SndStatic:Play() end local currentVol = SndStatic.Volume SndStatic.Volume = currentVol + (targetVol - currentVol) * (1 - math.exp(-8 * dt)) -- Static pitch variation RS.staticAnimT = RS.staticAnimT + dt local pitchVar = 1.0 + math.sin(RS.staticAnimT * 2.3) * 0.03 if RS.interference then pitchVar = pitchVar + (math.random() - 0.5) * 0.1 end SndStatic.PlaybackSpeed = pitchVar end local function UpdateVisibility(dt) local target = RS.visible and 1 or 0 RS.openProgress = RS.openProgress + (target - RS.openProgress) * (1 - math.exp(-10 * dt)) RadioGui.Enabled = RS.openProgress > 0.01 local scale = 0.85 + RS.openProgress * 0.15 local alpha = RS.openProgress MainFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 680 * scale, 0, 520 * scale) MainFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -340 * scale, 0.5, -260 * scale) MainFrame.GroupTransparency = 1 - alpha -- Mouse behavior if RS.visible then UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.Default UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = true else UserInputService.MouseBehavior = Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter UserInputService.MouseIconEnabled = false end end local function UpdateMessage(dt) if RS.messageVisible then RS.messageTimer = RS.messageTimer - dt if RS.messageTimer <= 0 then RS.messageVisible = false end end end ------------------------------------------------------------ -- MAIN LOOP ------------------------------------------------------------ RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt) UpdateVisibility(dt) if not RS.visible then UpdateStatic(dt) return end if not RS.powered then UpdateStatic(dt) return end UpdateDial(dt) UpdateSpectrum(dt) UpdateMeter(dt) UpdateUI(dt) UpdateStatic(dt) UpdateMessage(dt) end) ------------------------------------------------------------ -- INITIAL SYNC ------------------------------------------------------------ task.spawn(function() task.wait(4) if GetRadioState then local success, data = pcall(function() return GetRadioState:InvokeServer() end) if success and data then RS.powered = data.active or false RS.frequency = data.frequency or 98.0 RS.staticLevel = data.staticLevel or 0.35 RS.signalStrength = data.signalStrength or 0 RS.signalDetected = data.signalDetected or false RS.signalType = data.signalType RS.signalDecoded = data.signalDecoded or false RS.decoding = data.decoding or false RS.decodeProgress = data.decodeProgress or 0 RS.interference = data.interference or false RS.totalLogged = data.totalLogged or 0 if data.journal then RS.journal = data.journal for _, entry in ipairs(RS.journal) do AddJournalEntry(entry) end end print("[RadioUI] Synced with server. Freq: " .. string.format("%.1f", RS.frequency)) end end end) print("[RadioUI] Radio Client UI System initialized — [R] to toggle, scroll/drag to tune, [G] to decode") ```
